This is consumed to harmonize with the water’s numinous essence. The ingredients include left-facing oysters from the Eastern Sea, white halloysite from Wu Commandery, mica flakes, earthworm soil, talc, and alum—six substances in equal parts. The Supreme Ultimate Perfected One inscribed the *Supreme Emperor’s Scripture for Nurturing the Five Viscera* on the eastern wall of the Purple Tenuity Jade Forest Hall in the Palace of Supreme Ultimate. This is one of the Eight Dragon Writings of Highest Clarity, incomprehensible to worldly scholars. The Red Pine Master of Southern Marchmount received and ingested it, seeking commentary from the Supreme Ultimate Perfected One.

The Azure Lad also said: "The fat of the Five Lords nurtures the five viscera, refines the white and transforms the body, restoring youthful complexion." Purification and the daubing of the turtle-shaped crucible are essential for refinement. The cloud-fat has a fragrantly sweet and uniquely delicious taste, strengthening the blood, fortifying the bones, preserving *qi*, congealing fluids, nurturing the five viscera, cultivating the hun and po souls—it is a true superior medicine. The Perfected One said: "This surpasses the refinement of the eight minerals and the ingestion of mica." This refers to those who refine their forms in the Great Yang and transcend the Three Bureaus.

It is also said: The Supreme Ultimate Perfected One’s *Azure Essence [missing text] Grain Formula*. According to the *Biography of Pengzu*: "In Dayuan, there was a Master of Azure Essence who could eat nine times a day or fast for an entire year without hunger." This is the same method. It is a wondrous formula of the supreme immortals and a marvelous technique for abstaining from grains. The Perfected One of Pure Emptiness recounted that in Mount Huo, a Daoist practitioner named Deng Boyuan and Wang Xuanfu received the method of ingesting azure essence stone and swallowing sunlight, enabling them to write at night. Another immortal, Long Bogao, received the method of ingesting azure earth and, in a drunken state, vanished into seclusion at Fang Terrace. The Rectifier of Registers commanded his subordinate, saying: "Next, ingest earth-grain, and do not abandon ordinary grains. It will replenish marrow, eliminate ailments, and plump the skin." The subordinate also wrote to the Director, requesting rice medicine to dye and make grain, fearing the herbs would dry out. The Director wrote to the Senior Attendant, sending a small amount of white rice to dye and make grain. These six instances are recorded in texts.

The Supreme Ultimate Perfected One’s *Ten-Stone Azure [missing text] Grain* is a divine formula of the highest immortals, with commentary by Lord Wang. The large script is from the *Original Scripture of Supreme Simplicity* and the oral instructions of Western Liang, while the ink annotations are the explanations of the Perfected One of Pure Emptiness, compiled and transcribed by Lady Wei of Southern Marchmount and Attendant Yang, the Controller of Destinies. Five perfected ones jointly completed this method, which is truly wondrous.

The *Precious Scripture of the Highest Prime* states: "You ingest the kingly *qi* of plants and trees to commune with the divine. You ingest the essence of azure candles." This is what is meant. Transmitted by Supreme Simplicity, compiled by the Supreme Ultimate, it is the ultimate essential of the highest perfected immortals, unlike other arts. Ingesting [missing text] grain renders one invulnerable to harm, untouched by epidemics, free from distracting thoughts, and able to extinguish the Three Worms. The ears and eyes become keen, the steps light and swift. One gains the ability to conceal, transform, and vanish, and prolonged ingestion extends life.

Lord Mao, Controller of Destinies, addressed his two younger brothers, saying: "You should ingest the *Four-Fan Powder*. This is the Dao of reversing aging and restoring youth, once transmitted by the Yellow Emperor to Wind Lord. I received it from Master Gaoqiu and now pass it to you."

He further instructed his youngest brother, Lord Baoming, saying: "You should ingest the *Queen Mother’s Four Lads Powder*—this is the secret Dao of returning to infancy. If there is any deficiency in the body, this formula should be taken to replenish the brain." It is recorded that when Lord Xiaomao ingested it, he was already one hundred and twenty years old.

These two formulas are both wondrous methods and must be prepared with fasting and purification.

He also said: "Master Pei received from Zhi Ziyuan the method of ingesting *fuling* (poria). This was transmitted by Jiang the Mountain Man of Jiaoshan, and it grants longevity and enduring vision. When compounding it, one must observe strict fasting and purification."

Master Pei further received from Zhi Ziyuan the method of ingesting *huma* (black sesame). Jiang the Master ingested only these two formulas and attained the rank of immortal perfected.

These two formulas, though slightly different from those known to the world, were secretly employed by Master Pei and proven effective. While many methods exist for ingesting *fuling* and *huma*, this one—having been practiced by a perfected immortal and recorded in his own hand—must be the most spiritually potent of all. With consistent ingestion, the Dao of immortality may be attained. The difficulty lies in people discontinuing the practice before perceiving its benefits, thus few achieve its full effects.

If the body is not yet depleted and one is still young, one should ingest *fuling*. After the age of thirty, one should ingest *huma*.

Jiang the Master said: "These two formulas are the essential methods of *Dayou*—the great treasure of longevity and immortality." *Dayou* refers to the scriptural methods of the *Dayou* Palace within the Grotto-Heaven of Weiyu Mountain, where those who ingest them dwell.

The *Scripture of Treasured Mystery* states: "*Fuling* remedies youth, *huma* remedies old age. Combined with fasting and taken at dawn, they form the *huili* (luxuriant elixir) of a hundred flowers." The Five Lords called this *huimeng huayu* (flowery luxuriance of the hundred herbs).

*Fire essence* is *fuling*—its nature is warm and aligned with fire, thus it is the essence of fire. *Water treasure* is *huma*—its nature is cool, its color black, and it contains vital moisture, thus it is the treasure of water. Blended as one, they return essence to the treasury. This is what is meant.

Lord Pei, having used these methods in his youth, thus consumed *fuling*. The Perfected One of Pure Emptiness received this formula at the age of twelve—at that time, he had not yet suffered any depletion, which is why it is said that consuming *fuling* allowed him to see light at night. These two methods are both extraordinary formulas for prolonging life. If the two ingredients are combined in double measure, ground together, and decocted into pills, the effect is even finer.

According to the *Green Essence Formula*, *fuling* prohibits the consumption of sour flavors, but this method, which uses *fuling* exclusively, does not require such a restriction.

It is further said: The Perfected Lord Wang of Pure Emptiness transmitted the *Licorice Pill Formula of Valley Immortality* to Lady Wei of South Marchmount. In her youth, Lady Wei suffered from many illnesses. Lord Wang, while in Xiuwu County, instructed her: "Those who cultivate the Dao must first dispel illness, filling the Five Viscera to abundance, so that ears and eyes grow sharp—only then may one engage in visualization and ingestion practices."

Lord Wang first descended as a perfected being in the winter of the ninth year of *Yuan Kang* during the Jin dynasty, within the boundaries of Xiuwu County in Ji Commandery. At that time, Lady Wei was forty-eight years old. She followed his instructions and consumed the pills, and when she concealed her form and departed this world, she was eighty-three. This was in the eighth year of *Xianhe* during the reign of Emperor Cheng of Jin, the *jiawu* year—meaning Lady Wei had taken the medicine for thirty-five years. Though she did not necessarily take it continuously, she suffered no further ailments. Her prior illnesses were entirely cured; her hair did not turn white, her teeth did not fall out, her ears and eyes remained keen, and she regularly transcribed Daoist talismans by moonlight. As Lady Wei served as a Female Libationer, she still demonstrated her traces through talismans and scriptures. When engaging in visualization within her chamber, she could remain for a hundred days or several tens of days without feeling fatigue. Though she lived in the mundane world, her household affairs often disrupted her practice, so she would use seclusion in her chamber as a pretext to pursue purification, study, and recitation.

The smooth digestion and vigorous limbs—this is the efficacy of the Licorice Pill, known as the Grain Immortal Formula. When the spleen and stomach are harmonized, one can eat without harm, the skin becomes full and the essence keen, daily life is regulated, and there is no affliction of constipation or diarrhea. To attain immortality through consuming grain is why it is called the Grain Immortal. This formula was originally compiled by Right Perfected Lord Guo of the Nine Palaces, and it had long existed in various palaces. Guo later reorganized it, arranging and explaining its therapeutic applications—much like the Azure Essence, which is the method of the Grand Simplicity, yet is now attributed to the Perfected of the Supreme Ultimate. Those who study the Daoist path should take this first.

In the past, Lord Shaojin transmitted this formula to Jie Xiang, and later to Liu Gen, Zhang Ling, and dozens of others, who also called this pill the Shaojin Pill. It should be prepared with fasting and purification; it is non-toxic and has no dietary restrictions. Its benefits accrue over a year, not merely in a day or night. Even laypeople may take it.

It is also said: The Cloud Mushroom Essence may be prepared without regard to auspicious days. When used to treat the Three Corpses, ingesting one dose kills the grain worms, causing the Three Corpses to wither. Daoists who regularly consume grain should take this. Once the grain worms are eradicated, one may eat grain without illness and overindulge without harm. Many medicines eliminate the corpse worms, but none surpass this.

In ancient times, Master Yang Xiu, Ji Qiuzi, Dongfang Shuo, Cui Wenzi, and Shang Qiuzi all took this medicine to harmonize with grain and attained immortality. Emperor Jing of Han and Emperor Wu sought Dongfang Shuo and Master Yang Xiu’s secret formulas, but they were never transmitted.

It is further said: Lord Juanzi of Beihai, whose given name and surname are obscure, was a disciple of the Green Lad and the master of Su Lin. In his youth, he consumed Wooden Yellow Essence and was taught the Way of Guarding the One and the Mystery Elixir, living for 2,800 years. Su Lin, styled Zixuan, a Courtier of the Dark Continent and disciple of Juanzi, was also the master of the Purple Yang. A native of Qu Shui in Puyang, he left home at the age of twenty to study the Dao. Later, he was transmitted the Three Origins and the True One, wandering and transforming among the people.

It is further said: The Perfected One of Grand Clarity and Orthodox Unity, Zhang Daoling of Pei State, was originally a great Confucian scholar. In the fourth year of the *Yanguang* era of the Han, he began to study the Dao. By the end of the Han, immortals from the Wugou Mountain descended and transmitted to him the teachings of Orthodox Unity and the Covenant of Might, along with the methods for transforming and guiding the people. He was titled the Celestial Master. This is what *True Reports* refers to as "those who serve Zhang Daoling’s Orthodox Unity and harmonize the qi." The *Preface to the Five Talismans of the Numinous Treasure* and the *Preface to the Grand Clarity’s Golden Liquid Elixir* by the Celestial Master are both fine works, with separate biographies already circulating in the world.

It is further said: Those who ingest the Five Minerals can eat nine meals in a day, with their hundred meridians flowing with purity, and may also go a full year without hunger, reversing aging to return to infancy. When they encounter food, they eat; when they do not, they remain at ease. This is the wondrous formula of the highest immortals and the marvelous efficacy of grain avoidance. Tao Yinju’s commentary states: Though they eat nine meals in a day, they absorb and transform the essence, leaving no residue, and though they go a year without eating, their complexion grows ever more radiant.

It is further said: In the ease of absorption and transformation, nothing surpasses the Seven Luminaries; in the swiftness of cultivation and attainment, nothing exceeds the Nine Ways; in the firmness of preservation and protection, nothing compares to *Zhensheng*; in the urgency of defense and application, nothing arises before the *Hunshen*; in the rapid efficacy of medicinal stones, what rivals *Qingjing*? In the responsiveness of prayer and worship, what excels the morning and evening offerings?

It is further said: Ingesting the Five Mineral Elixirs preserves the Five Viscera from decay.

It is further said: The nine-plumed phoenix brain, the Hidden Mushroom of the Great Ultimate, the golden liquid of the cinnabar furnace, the purple blossoms and rainbow essences, the Nine Cycles of Grand Clarity, the nectar of the Five Clouds, the white fragrance of the Eastern Sea, the azure coins of the Canglang, the lingering essence of the lofty hills, and the flying fields of the Jishi Mountains—all can bestow longevity upon people. Master Qin Gao received the Way of the Elixir for Prolonging Life and practiced the methods of replenishing the brain and reverting the elixir.

*The Upper Conclusion of the Sacred Sword* states: Those who ingest the *Eightfold Radiance Pill of the Curved Dawn of the Great Ultimate* can soar through the Great Void.

It is further said: The Perfected One of the Great Void ingested the *Cloud Teeth of the Four Poles*.

It is further said: The *Flying Dragon Cloud Paste* refines the quintessence of the Five Minerals into an ointment, bestowing a jade-like radiance upon the body and enabling one to write in the dark. This medicine surpasses the ingestion of the Eight Stones.

It is further said: Those who ingest the essence of the sun and moon should consume bamboo shoots in moderation. Bamboo shoots are the embryo of the sun’s essence, also called *Great Brightness*. They should also consume pine needles in moderation. The pine is the finest of trees, and those who ingest the sun and moon should eat these substances to harmonize with their qi. The Perfected One of the Great Void said: The pine and cypress are the finest of trees.

It is further said: The Perfected One embraces the primordial radiance of the Five Directions’ dawn and ingests the essence of the Nine Auroras. The commentary states: This refers to the primordial qi of the clear dawn and the auroral essence of the first light, where the yang number nine is called the *Nine Auroras*. The original text states: *The divine light shines inwardly, while vermilion blossoms unfold outwardly.*

*The Yellow Plain Scripture of the Supreme* states: Whenever Daoists take a meal, they should first offer it to the Great Harmony.

*The Scripture of Great Peace* states: The Green Lad gathers flying roots and swallows the radiance of the sun.

*The Numinous Chapters of the Hollow Cavern* state: At dawn, they dine on the qi of the Five Clouds; at dusk, they chant the light of the Three Dawns. It also states: They consume the amber and purple nectar of the true.

*True Reports* states: On Kunlun Mountain, there is the marrow of the Crimson Mountain and the fruit of the jade trees.

It is further said: The method of the *Purple Texts of the Numinous Writings of the Golden Gates of Supreme Clarity*—adopting the yin blossoms and swallowing the essence of the moon—was once transmitted by the Celestial Sovereign of the Great Tenuity. It is also called *The Scripture of the Yellow Qi and the Hidden Moon, the Treasury of the Sun’s Essence*.

It is further said: For all who practice the Dao, wine and meat are the greatest taboos. Wine, as a substance, can cloud the mind and confuse the will, leading to perverse and disordered behavior. Among all medicines, only the *Four Lads Pill* mentions the use of wine, though water may also be used. The *Wooden Pill* is simmered with wine, but no other texts mention ingesting medicines with wine.

It is further said: During the Later Han, Zuo Ci begged the Controller of Destinies for cinnabar and obtained twelve pounds, which he used to compound the *Ninefold Radiance Elixir*.

It is further said: Zhi Mingqi and Zhang Zhengli of the Later Han era dwelled in Mount Heng, where they received and ingested the *Rainbow Radiance Elixir* of Lord Wang, practicing it for over thirty years.

It is further said: Zhao Guangxin, a native of Yangcheng, came to Mount Kuaiji during the Wei era. He received the method of ingesting qi and guarded the Way of the Mysterious Center. Later, he ingested the *Ninefold Radiance Elixir*.

It is further said: Zhu Ruzi, a man of the Wu era, entered the Red Water Mountain, where he ingested chrysanthemum flowers and wood, and received from the Master of the Western Return the thirty-three chapters of the method for visualizing and guarding the *Niwan* within the chamber.

It is further said: Zheng Jingshi and Zhang Chonghua, both men of the early Jin, dwelled in Mount Wan, where they practiced the method of guarding the Five Viscera and containing the sun, ingesting sesame and the Mysterious Elixir.

It is further said: Ma Mingsheng of Linzi served as a county clerk. While pursuing bandits, he was wounded.

The Lady of Supreme Perfection saved him with the Numinous Origin. After his recovery, he studied under Anqisheng and received the method of ingesting the Great Clarity Elixir.

It is further said: Wang Xuanfu of Pei, together with Deng Boyuan, dwelled on Mount Huo, where they received the method of consuming the Azure Essence Stone Meal and swallowing the solar radiance.

It is further said: The *Huangshan Formula* states: In cultivating nature and ingesting medicinal substances, one should avoid eating garlic and pomegranate seeds. Daoists must not consume them. The *Biographies of the Immortals* records: Chijiang Ziju was a man of the Yellow Emperor’s time. He did not eat the five grains but consumed the flowers of a hundred herbs. It is further said: The Heavenly Immortal Woquan was a gatherer of herbs on Mount Huai. He favored eating pine nuts, his body grew hair, his eyes were square, and he could fly and outrun horses. It is further said: Wu Guang was a man of the Xia era. His ears were seven inches long, he loved the zither, and consumed the roots of cattail and leek. It is further said: Juanzi of Qi favored consuming wood and composed the *Canon of Heaven and Earth* in thirty-eight chapters. Later, while fishing in the marsh, he obtained a talismanic carp, retreated into Rock Mountain, and could summon wind and rain. The Nine Immortals Method of Ji Boyang was briefly obtained by the Prince of Huainan in his youth, though he could not comprehend it. Its three chapters of *Zither Heart* contain profound meaning.

It is further said: Liu Jing, a man of the Former Han, studied under Zhang Jun of Nange and received the method of ingesting mica, through which he discerned good and ill fortune.

The *Baopuzi* states: Those who cultivate the Dao, ingest medicinal substances, and retreat into the mountains must not enter lightly. Many who do so encounter harm, for the aged among the myriad beings can all manifest as spirits and often test humans. Yet they cannot alter their true form in a mirror. Thus, ancient Daoists entering the mountains always carried a bright mirror, at least nine inches in diameter, suspended behind their backs, so that old demons dared not approach. If something came to test them, they would glance into the mirror: if it appeared in human form, it was a mountain immortal or spirit; if it appeared as a bird, beast, or malevolent ghost, it would be revealed. Once, a man in a stone chamber on Mount Yuntai in Shu suddenly saw a figure clad in yellow silk and a kudzu headdress appear before him. When he looked into his mirror, it was a deer—he shouted, and it turned into a deer and fled. There was also an inn at the foot of Mount Linlü where travelers often died or fell ill. Every night, a dozen or so figures—some in white, some in black, some men, some women—would appear. Later, Nie Boyi lodged there, sitting with a bright candle. At midnight, they indeed appeared. Secretly observing them in the mirror, he saw they were straw dogs. Boyi then seized the candle and pretended to drop its ember on their clothing, smelling scorched fur. He drew his blade and slew one dog, and the rest fled in terror.

When entering the mountains, one must select an auspicious day. The *Baopuzi* states: The conditions of heaven and earth, the fortunes of yin and yang—these are vast and difficult to fathom. I do not insist they exist, nor dare I guarantee their absence. Yet the Yellow Emperor and Lü Wang both trusted and submitted to them, and in recent times, Yan Junping and Sima Qian both relied upon them. The classics and histories record the origins of hard and auspicious days. The kings, the Grand Scribe, and the officials of the Feng and Bao sacrifices—when they performed ancestral rites, suburban offerings, and sacrifices to heaven and earth—they all selected their days. According to the *Jade Chime Classic*: Those who wish to enter the mountains must know the secrets of *Dunjia*, though I shall not expound upon its intricacies for others.

End of Scroll Thirteen of the Daoist Canon
Beginning of Scroll Fourteen

The *Scriptures of Transcendents* state: The Nine-Transmutation Elixir, the *Golden Liquid Classic*, and the *Secrets of Guarding the One* are all concealed within the Five Cities of Kunlun, stored in jade cases, inscribed on golden tablets, sealed with purple clay, and stamped with the central seal.

*The Master Embracing Simplicity* says: I have heard Master Zheng speak of the most revered Daoist texts, none surpassing the *Inner Writings of the Three Sovereigns* and the *True Forms of the Five Peaks*. In ancient times, transcendents and those who recorded their deeds held these in utmost secrecy—this Way was not transmitted except to those bearing the name of transcendents. Once received, it was passed on only once every forty years. The transmission was marked in cinnabar and sealed with an oath, binding trust as a covenant. All the famous mountains and the Five Peaks safeguard these texts, yet they are hidden in secluded stone chambers. Those destined for the Dao who enter the mountains and meditate with utmost sincerity will find the mountain spirits opening the way, revealing the texts like silk unfurling. This is how Zhongli obtained them in the mountains.

Those who possess these texts must maintain purity. Before any action, they must first report to them as if serving a sovereign or father. The scriptures say: Those who hold the *Writings of the Three Sovereigns* repel evil spirits, plagues, and misfortunes. Next in rank is the *Hidden Subtleties of the Jade Maiden*, a single scroll that can transform one’s form into flying dragons, various beasts, gold, jade, wood, or stone, and summon clouds and rain—this too is a great art, surpassing even the *Hongbao* and *Wanbi* texts of Huainan.

Master Zheng was profoundly learned in the Five Classics and was one who understood the Dao. He mastered the Nine Palaces and Three Boards, calculated the celestial movements of the world, and aligned the *He* and *Luo* with prophecies and apocrypha. In the first year of the Taihe era, foreseeing the chaos of the Jichen rebellion and the coming turmoil in Jiangnan, he carried his satchel of immortal medicines and entered Mount Huo to the east, unknown to all.

It is also said: Those whose homes hold the *True Forms of the Five Peaks* are shielded from harm, and no one can injure them. Further, it is said: The Yellow Emperor and Laozi, sages of profound insight, revealed secret texts in famous mountains and received immortal scriptures from divine beings. They cast off the dust of the world to shed burdens, soaring to the distant heights, their lifespans equaling gold, stone, tortoises, and cranes. Moved by those of future generations who aspire to the Dao and pitying the unenlightened, they left behind methods, clearly and brilliantly recorded. Yet the shallow-minded, clinging to their narrow views, delight in emptiness and drown in mediocrity. They know that excess in food and drink hastens illness yet cannot restrain themselves; they know that indulgence in passions leads to ruin yet cannot sever them. If even transcendence is attainable, how can they believe it?

According to the *Scriptures of Transcendents*, those who attain transcendence do so because their destinies align with the qi of immortality, naturally perceiving it. Thus, from the moment of conception, they already bear the nature of the Dao. If their awakened minds incline toward such matters, they will inevitably encounter an enlightened master and obtain the method. Otherwise, they will neither believe nor seek, and even if they seek, they will not find.

A lifespan of a hundred years spans over thirty thousand days. In youth, one knows nothing; in old age, joy and pleasure fade. Subtracting the years of childhood, senility, and dotage, along with the ceaseless succession of dangers, hardships, and illnesses, barely half of one’s years in the world remain. For most, a lifespan barely reaches fifty or sixty—alas!—and after accounting for grief, sorrow, and the decline of age, only six or seven thousand days remain. In the blink of an eye, they are gone. As for those who live a full hundred years, not one in ten thousand achieves it. Reflecting deeply, one cannot but pity them, no different from the summer insects or morning mushrooms. This is the profound sorrow of those who understand the Dao.

The *Supreme Jade Writ of the Great Night* says: The Dao is originally formless, yet in response to perception, images arise. The great image is without image, its subtlety difficult to fathom. Thus, when true texts are seen, they coalesce in emptiness to form characters.

It further says: The *Inner Talismans of the Numinous Treasure*, secret texts of the Supreme Transcendent, were bestowed upon Emperor Yu by the Nine Heavens’ True Kings and the Three Heavens’ True Sovereigns, hidden in the northern valley of Mount Zhong. When Yu the Great completed his regulation of the waters, he journeyed to Mount Zhong, where the transcendent of the mountain transmitted them to him.

Yu returned to Kuaiji and further compiled and finalized them into two copies. One copy was concealed in the □ of Miaoshan, to emerge only after ten thousand kalpas. The other was transcribed on silk and entrusted to the Cloud-Water Grotto Chamber, to be delivered at the jia-shen epoch to those such as Fu Bochang, who governed the waters.

It further says: In the twelfth year of King Helü of Wu, during the first month, he dispatched the Elder of Dragon Might to enter the Dongting Grotto of Baoshan and retrieve it, bringing forth talismans but no explanations.

Moreover, the Qi native Le Zichang received it from the Immortal of Huolin, Han Zhong, who then expounded the methods of ingestion and application, concealing them in the northern chamber beneath the Eastern Sea.

The *Scripture of the Golden Liquid of the Great One*, according to the *Preface to the Sword Scripture*, states: Gaoqiuzi ingested the golden liquid water. The *Records of the Grand Scribe* say: In preparing the golden elixir, the intent all refers to this method. Today, there exists Ge Hong’s commentary on the *Yellow Silk Writ* of Xi Yin, along with a separate formula in one scroll. This is also the supreme cinnabar method of the Great Clarity.

The *Concealed Instructions for Ascending to Perfection* says: Master Yang and Attendant Xu jointly transcribed the *Scripture of the Grotto Chamber* on small azure stationery. It also says: in seal script on white hemp paper. It further says: The *Scriptures of the Eight Silks* were personally inscribed by the Sage Lord using white silk and brushes of eight colors.

The *Scripture of Numinous Writs* says: In the ancient era of Longhan, the Supreme Sage inscribed the wondrous scriptures and true writs of the Numinous Treasure upon the azure forests of empty space, revealing the methods to deliver humanity.

The *Scripture of the Golden Root* says: The Golden Lad of the Great Yang and the Jade Maiden of the Great Yin attend the purple script of the supreme method. It further says: The Jade Maiden of Xihua guards the *Scripture of the Hidden Moon* in the Immortal Capital.

The *Hidden Instructions of the Flying Dragon’s Plain Silk* says: The Heavenly Thearch commanded the Feathered Immortal Attendant to hold a golden tablet and request the scriptures.

The *True Reports* says: The *Inner Instructions of the Nine Perfected of the Supreme Clarity* were compiled by the Perfected One of the Great Ultimate, Red Pine. It further says: The *Jade Tablet Inscription of Central Huayang* states: "Cultivate and preserve the Three Primes’ Grotto; I, the Jade Writ, govern the Eight Elders and the Twenty-Four Perfected. Without sleep, inwardly contemplate—these are the essential words of immortality."

It further says: The *Scripture of Treasuring the Spirits* is the text from the brocade pouch of the Perfected Lord Pei Qingxu. It is what attendants constantly carry. Formerly, Pei received this book from the Lady of Purple Tenuity.

It further says: At the western terrace above the northern altar of the Dark Garden, all the secret writs of the Heavenly Perfected are contained within. It further says: The Perfected Consort of Nine Flowers, along with the Lady of Purple Tenuity and the Lady Wei of Southern Marchmount, descended together. After sitting for a long while, the Perfected Consort commanded her attendant to open her brocade pouch and present two scrolls to Master Yang: one, the *Hidden Book of Inner Contemplation Illumined by Jade Radiance and Purple Glow of the Supreme Clarity*; the other, the *Book of the Supreme Clarity on Returning to Dawn and the Sun’s Brilliance amid the Central Mystery*. These are the scriptures of the Three Primes and Eight Assemblies. After Master Yang thoroughly mastered the true characters, he rendered them in clerical script for clarity.

The Dao possesses the *Eight Silk True Scriptures*, the hidden writings of the Supreme Lord. There are also the *Nine Perfected Central Scriptures*, the secret words of the Old Lord. The *Yellow Writ* is also an essential formula for longevity. The *Azure Essentials* and *Purple Scripts*, the *Golden Root* and *Multitudinous Writs*, the *True Instructions of Jade Clarity*, the *Three-Nine Plain Words* and *Cinnabar Scenery Dao Essence*, the *Eight Trees Hidden in Earth*, the *White Tallies* and *Azure Registers*, the *Purple Transmission* and *Flame Elder*—these are all scriptures of the Dao.

There are also the *Seven Steps of the Flying Prime*, the *Scriptures of the Heavenly Net*, the *Seven Transformations of Divine Methods*, the *Scriptures of the Seven Revolutions*. Moreover, the *True Scripture of the Great Grotto* in thirty-nine chapters, the *Hidden Writ of the Great Cinnabar* in eight principles and ten formulas, the *Three Diagrams of the Heavenly Pass*, the *Seven Stars’ Shifting Degrees*, the *Nine Elixirs* and *Golden Liquid Divine Cinnabar*, the *Hidden Zhi of the Great Ultimate*, the *Secret Talismans of the Five Agents*, the *Formulas of the Curved Silk and Plain Words*, the *Yellow Water and Moon Radiance*, the *Jade Essence of Returning Water*, the *Azure Bloom of Water Yang*, the *Crimson Tree and Azure Fruit*, the *Cinnabar of Langgan Blossoms*, the *Celestial Sovereign’s Image Talismans* to harmonize the primordial qi, the *White Feather and Purple Canopy* to wander the Five Marchmounts, the *Inner Writ of the Three Sovereigns* to summon the spirits of heaven and earth, the *Jade Pendants and Golden Earrings* to ascend the Great Ultimate, the *Plain Memorials and Cinnabar Talismans* to summon the Six Jia, the *Golden Perfection and Jade Radiance* to illuminate the world, the *Eight Sceneries’ Chariot* to traverse the Great Clarity, the *Wings of Flight* to transcend the void.

Liu Xiang’s *Accounts of the Transcendents* says: The *Accounts of the Transcendents* was compiled by Liu Xiang, Grand Master of Splendid Happiness of the Han. Initially, Emperor Wu favored the masters of methods, and Prince An of Huainan also gathered retainers, possessing the *Grand Treasure in the Pillow* scriptures. Earlier, Prince An plotted rebellion and was executed; Xiang’s father, De, was appointed by Emperor Wu to adjudicate the Huainan case and obtained those books. Xiang, though young, read them and found them extraordinary. When Emperor Xuan ascended the throne, he revived Emperor Wu’s precedents, and Xiang, along with Wang Bao and others, was advanced for his erudition and outstanding talent to attend the emperor’s side. Xiang also saw Huainan’s alchemical trees and memorialized that gold could be refined. The emperor ordered Xiang and the Director of the Imperial Workshop to refine gold, but the expenses were great and the results unverified, leading to his indictment and a sentence of death. His elder brother, the Marquis of Anyang, Anmin, petitioned to surrender half his state’s households to ransom Xiang’s crime. The emperor, admiring his talent, commuted his sentence to death and appointed him Gentleman of the Yellow Gates, lecturing on the Five Classics at the Stone Canal. By the time of Emperor Cheng, Xiang, having been placed in charge of the imperial archives, observed the emperor’s keen interest in matters of spirit immortality and thus compiled accounts of such affairs from high antiquity through the Three Dynasties, Qin, and Han, drawing from various traditions.

The *Account of King Mu’s Journey to Heaven* says: He ascended the slopes of Kunlun to view the palace of the Yellow Emperor, observing the fasts and rites to sacrifice at Dengchong Mountain, which is the Dark Garden. The Kunlun Mountain spans two thousand li square, with a nine-tiered citadel called the Gate Wind Dark Garden.

The *Classic of Mountains and Seas* says: Resplendent is Kunlun, the Dark Garden above it. King Mu inscribed a stele at the Dark Garden to illuminate later generations. The Son of Heaven feasted with the Queen Mother of the West atop the Jasper Pool, and the Queen Mother sang, "White clouds in the sky." Thereupon, the Son of Heaven ascended the Yanzi Mountain, where the sun sets, and recorded his traces at Qishan.

The *Account of Mao Ying* says: The Queen Mother said to Mao Ying: "The Jade..."

The Way of the Golden Pendants, the *Canon of the Supreme Ultimate and Mysterious Perfection*—those who master it may soar through the Great Void. The Queen Mother commanded Wang Zongzhen of the Western Citadel to expound the *Canon of Mysterious Perfection* in full. She further elucidated the *Canon of the Golden Pendants*, transmitting it orally to Ying, saying: "The Golden Pendants are the radiant canopy of the Supreme Clarity, the inner perfected jade ornaments of the Yin luminants. The Most High’s hidden and wondrous *Flying Cavern* reveals them; those who attain its treasure scriptures ascend to the Cloud Han, recline in the Supreme Ultimate, and hear the words of the Primordial Celestial Constancy. These are the esoteric writings of the Two Luminants of the Great Night, the jade ornaments and Golden Pendants.

There are also the inner true talismans of the Yin and Yang luminants, which accompany the original text. By the Most High’s decree, they are to be transmitted only to the Directors of Destinies. O jade tablet of mysterious potency, inscribed in green characters on gold, its yellow radiance illumines the inner brilliance; the plain script of the Supreme Clarity—you shall be appointed as the Lord Director of Destinies. Yet without first comprehending the Way of the Mysterious Perfection of the Luminous Hall, one cannot obtain the esoteric writings of the Great Night.

The Way of Mysterious Perfection is the method of consuming the sun and moon, the art of refining the Five Spirits. Its canon states:
*Supreme Mystery beyond mystery,
Dual spirits and Fourfold Clarity,
Mysterious Perfection illumines within,
Luminous Hall purifies without.
Swallow the breath of the Two Radiance,
Eternally vitalize the divine essence.
Ascend to assist the Directors of Destinies,
Overseeing and governing the myriad spirits.*"

The Sixfold Splendors overflow, penetrating the gaze of the Yellow Tranquility. These forty characters were engraved by the Most High upon the southern gate of Phoenix Terrace. They are not taught to those who are not disciples of the Perfected Assembly, nor transmitted to any but the most eminent of the Lords of Destinies.

The True Officers of the Most High employ the Way of the Sun’s Rosy Clouds and embrace the method of the Twofold Radiance, enabling communion with the numinous and attainment of the true, their bodies suffused with jade-like luminosity. They command the myriad spirits and ascend to the Celestial Chambers. In former times, the Perfected Lord of Bell Mountain used this Mysterious Perfection method. When Lord Wang bestowed it upon Ying, he returned to the Western City and, following the true instructions, practiced it for three years. His countenance took on the luster of jade. Later, Lord Wang further granted Ying the Nine-Turned Returning Elixir and a prescription, establishing an altar and forming a covenant with the oath that it must not be transmitted or revealed. He then sent Ying home with these words: “After a hundred years, seek me upon the Southern Marchmount, and I shall appoint you to a celestial office in the realm of Hao and Yue.”

Thereafter, Ying attained immortality and dwelt upon Mount Gouqu, whereupon the people renamed it the Mountain of Lord Mao. When Lord Mao’s two younger brothers heard of Ying’s achievement, they at last believed in the reality of immortals. They abandoned their official posts, crossed the river, and sought out their elder brother. Upon meeting, he revealed to them the true instructions. After eighteen years, their Way was accomplished. He then required them to undergo three further years of purification, after which he transmitted the supreme method, instructing them to cultivate the qi of the Luminous Hall and Mysterious Perfection. Only then did Ying report to Lord Wang, recounting how his brothers had obtained the method of becoming earthbound immortals. They were to receive the registers, wear the talismans of the True Ultimate, and be invested with authority.

Lord Wang bestowed upon them the Mysterious Water and Jade Elixir, the Vermilion Sun’s Cinnabar Mushroom, instructing the brothers to purify themselves for three months before consuming them. Ying then commanded a carriage to convey his brothers to Green Isle to inscribe their names upon the golden tablets. They journeyed next to the Grotto Palace of the Western City to pay homage to the Supreme Minister of the Perfected Assembly, then southward to the Vermilion Terrace of Mount Heng to visit the Red Perfected of the Great Void. Upon returning, they sought the strategies of the Two Earthbound Immortals from the Square Cauldron, then proceeded to Red City to receive the True Talismans of Spirit Transformation. They traveled onward to Mount Luo and Huo to obtain embroidered banners of floral streamers, then ascended to the Nine Palaces and presented themselves beneath the Golden Portals, where they received the scriptures of the Sagely Lord. For three months, they prostrated themselves at the gate.

Thereupon, the Sagely Lord commanded the Supreme Minister of the Ninefold Subtlety and Great Perfection, the High Auroral Master and Green Lad, to ascend and petition the Most High. The Vermilion-Crowned Messenger was sent down to invest the two brothers beneath the Golden Portals, bestowing upon them the true tablets before their return.

It is said: The scriptures of divine immortality on the methods of the Yellow and the White comprise twenty-five scrolls and over a thousand chapters. Yet most are profoundly abstruse and difficult to comprehend; only a few can be clearly understood. The worldly often doubt these matters as mere fantasy, no different from those who disbelieve in immortals altogether. In former times, I received from Master Zheng the Nine Elixirs and the Scripture of the Golden Liquid, and subsequently sought from him five scrolls on the methods of the Yellow and the White. Master Zheng recounted how he and Zuo Ci had tested these methods in the Copper Mountains of Lujiang, and all had succeeded. Yet the rigor of purification and the strictness of the prohibitions were no less demanding than those required for compounding the Nine Elixirs of divine immortality.

Vulgar folk often ridicule me for my pursuit of esoteric arts, accusing me of forcing comprehension upon what the world deems incomprehensible. Yet how do the water and fire obtained through the Square Cauldron differ from ordinary water and fire? Both arise from natural resonance, and without plumbing the principles to their depths and exhausting the nature of things, one cannot fathom their ultimate significance. Without tracing origins and grasping ends, one cannot apprehend their true conditions.

Wu Taiwen, the Prefect of Chengdu, was learned and widely knowledgeable. He too recounted past experiences: the Daoist Li Gen had achieved success with certain woods, yet could not obtain the specific wood he sought unless one observed a hundred days of purification. Taiwen, then serving in office, could not fulfill this requirement and often sighed, lamenting the insufficiency of human inquiry.

The *Statutes of the Great Perfection* states: The King of the Lesser Heaven of Pure Emptiness compiled the *Scripture of the Unification of the Three Heavens*.

The *Scripture of the Golden Liquid* says: The *August Scripture of the Primordial Chaos* was presented to the Vermilion Auroral Perfected of the Supreme Truth and sealed within a jade casket. The greatness of the supreme Way accords with the celestial charts; the essential words of the Three Elixirs are recorded by the Supreme August, hidden within the Jade Hall, and their purport must not be transmitted.

The *Scripture of the Great Perfection and Mysterious Elixir* was engraved within the Hall of Pure Emptiness; it is the treasured text of the Supreme August Lord, called the Elixir of Purple Stamens and Luminous Pearls. It reveals the cycles of transformation, blending and distinguishing all things. As yin and yang undergo repeated changes, the Way arises naturally. The Mysterious Chart revolves seven times, returning upon the ninth. The first chapter of the Great Yellow is called the Jade Void. The Perfected of the Supreme Truth preserve it, naming it the Primordial Scripture.

The *Jade Scripture of the Cavern Perfection* of the Supreme Clarity states: The Eightfold Radiance of the Most High was engraved upon the Immortal Terrace of the Eastern Flower, and not proclaimed to the world. Those who receive the Ninefold Yin Instructions of the Lord of Emperors swear an oath with white silk and crimson offerings—this is the oath of the sun’s brilliance. Those who receive the Neighbor-Bonding Chapters of the Most High swear with azure offerings—this is the oath of the moon’s splendor.

The *Mysterious Scripture of the Cavern Perfection of the Lord of the Great One* says: Within the Purple Chamber of the Six Harmonies of the Most High, Jade Maidens attend and guard the Hidden Writings of the Great Elixir.

The *Inner Biography of Ma Mingsheng* states: The Celestial Writings of the Numinous Treasure were sealed above the Nine Heavens, within the Palace of Great Existence, where the Golden Auroral Jade Maidens and the Purple Lads of the Auroral Dawn safeguard them.

The *Scripture of the Eightfold Radiance of Jade Light* says: The Jade Auroral Lads of the Golden Flower attend and guard the *Scripture of the Eightfold Radiance of Jade Light*.

The *Yellow Writ of the Most High* says: Those who read the Hidden Writings of the Great Elixir within the Golden Flower Grotto and the Precious Chapters of the Feminine One are able to consume the flavor of the Mysterious Perfection, encounter all things without obstruction, and summon the Great Simplicity. The Nine Perfected descend in response, and one is thereby entitled to be called a Master of the Three Primordials’ Elixir Methods, presiding over the Perfected of the Supreme Truth.

The *Central Scripture of the Nine Perfected* says: Within the Terrace of the Flowery Terrace of the Western Mystery Mountain are the *Scriptures of the Majestic Sun* and *Neighbor-Bonding*. The jade tablets bear golden characters inscribed with a green brush, recording the Three Primordials upon the Jade Tablets of the Upper Primordial.

The *Later Scripture of the Great Cavern* says: The Jade Lads of the Western Numinous reside upon the Terrace of Enduring Cold, attending and guarding the *Jade Registers of the Eightfold Radiance*.

The *Arrayed Records of the Later Sagely Lord* says: The Turtle Mother wielded the brush, and the Jade Lads bound the compilation, naming it the *Upper Scripture of the Purple Writings of the Numinous Book*.

The *Inner Sounds of the Three August Ones* says: When inscribing the talismanic characters of these inner sounds, use a yellow brush to form the script in seal, clerical, or tadpole characters, recording the origins of creation and the beginnings of human relations.

The *Writ of the Northern Emperor from the Six Palaces of Fengdu* states: The life and death of humans are carved by the Jade Emperor in hidden inscriptions upon stone, recorded on the northern walls of the Six Palaces to restrain and govern malevolent forces. It further says: The hidden stone inscriptions are transcribed onto a three-foot length of green silk before being worn, whereupon the myriad spirits pay homage—this is the Way of remote antiquity. It also says: Within the caverns of Mount Fengdu, the Jade Emperor’s hidden inscriptions comprise ninety-one words, carved upon stone and recorded in the Six Palaces of the Grotto-Heaven of Mount Fengdu. The northern walls of the Six Palaces are the numinous abode of the myriad spirits. It further says: The *Hidden Writ of the Cavern Radiance of Golden Mystery* from the Jade Clarity is carved in hidden stone inscriptions, its sounds emerging from the chapters of spontaneity. The Jade Chapters of the Nine Heavens are profound and recondite, beyond the comprehension of beginners or ordinary mortals, nor may their mysteries be fully expounded save by the descent of the Great Emperor.

The *Scripture of the Golden Root* also states: Those who cultivate the Golden Mystery must wear the hidden inscriptions. The *Mysterious Record of the Seven Sages of the Jade Emperor* says: Those whose names are inscribed in the Upper Clarity are all recorded in the *Dark Garden*, thereby attaining the perfection of Great Peace. Thus, the Most High’s proclamations are inscribed in jade script, not to be conveyed by bamboo slips, brush, or ink.

The *Hidden Writ of the Jade Clarity* says: The Dark Feather Jade Lad bestowed the *Dark Feather Supreme Jade Scripture* upon the guests of the Highest Jade Worthies of the Three Primordials of Grand Simplicity. It further says: The Radiant Jade Lads reside in the Gates of Numinous Radiance and the Chambers of Rosy Mist, attending and guarding the hidden writings of the Jade Grace of the August Highest and the Jade Clarity.

Here ends the Fourteenth Section of the Daoist Canon. Latter Part of the Immortal Scriptures.

The *Seven Sages’ Mysterious Record of the Jade Emperor* states: The ancient texts comprise one hundred thousand jade words, which none but the highest sages can fathom in intent. They are inscribed in the Hall of Kunlun and the Source of the Northern Grotto. It further says: Within the Chamber of Kunlun and the Perfected of the Northern Grotto, the source winds through the Nine Yi Celestial Nights, where white slips and azure records reside.

The *Scripture of Fundamental Conduct* says: Above the Nine Capitals, golden tablets and jade writings jointly inscribe the names of those who attain the Dao, enduring through kalpas. It further says: Within the Purple Orchid Terrace, the jade script of purple characters lies.

The *Bright Statutes of the Four Poles* states: The Western Chamber of Tortoise Mountain and the Southern Grotto of Wangwu Mountain contain the complete celestial scriptures. It further says: The Three Qi of the Jade Clarity’s Grotto-Chambers are sealed with golden chapters within the Purple Gates of the Jade Capital. It further says: The jade registers and treasured writings are concealed within the nine gates of the Purple Chamber.

The *Feminine One Scripture of the Great Grotto* says: There is a Dark-Lin Jade Palace where the Five Elders guard the Upper Scripture Repository within. It further says: The *Bright Statutes of the Four Poles* are sealed in the Golden Portal and Purple Terrace. It further says: The *Scripture of Radiant Perfection* is secretly kept in the Palace of Great Possession above the Nine Heavens, upon the Seven-Treasured Terrace of Golden Radiance. There is also the Three Treasures Mystic Terrace, wherein the *Hidden Writ of the Upper Clarity* is concealed.

The *Concealed Instructions for Ascending Perfection* states: Within the Upper Clarity’s Immortal Terrace, the golden script resides; within the Ninefold Mystic Terrace of the Grand Ultimate, the jade-slip writings lie; within the Bright Hall of the Mystic Tortoise Terrace of the August Perfected, the *Mystic Perfected Scripture* is kept. It further says: The Jasper Terrace of Kunlun, the Palace of the Queen Mother of the West—this is the Upper Jasper Terrace where the celestial perfected’s secret writings are preserved.

The *Golden Script and Jade Characters Upper Scripture* says: Within the Western Mystic Terrace, the *Golden Script Grotto-Chamber Scripture* is held. It further says: The destiny of one’s bones is already determined in the Mystic Pavilion’s green characters, for those whose names are inscribed in the immortal registers are predestined.

The *Cavernous Mystery Scripture* states: There is a Primordial Yang Terrace within the Heaven of Ruan Le, where the Inner Sound Writings are kept. It further says: A three-tiered jade terrace stands above the Nine Heavenly Gates, upon which rest three hundred volumes of the *Treasure Scripture of the Grand Clarity* and the registers of perfected ones learning immortality, overseen by the Jade Controller of the Celestial Thearch’s Perfected Oversight. It further says: The Jasper Terrace, where the Highest Thearch conceals the Golden Mystic Feather Chapters, holds the hidden sounds of the myriad spirits within its purple writings.

The *Golden Root Scripture* says: All who study must diligently uphold arduous resolve, whereupon the Jade Emperor of the Three Primordials and the Supreme of Eastern Florescence shall dispatch perfected ones to bestow upon them the true scriptures. None among the later sages and perfected ones fail first to present golden slips to Eastern Florescence and submit jade tablets to the Upper Clarity before receiving the *True Scripture of the Great Grotto*. Yet if the Azure Palace lacks the register of golden slips and the jade tablets bear no name in the mystic records, then even the divine scriptures cannot be bestowed.

The *Golden Root Scripture* says: Unfolding the cloud-phoenix’s brocade and the purple-silk pouch, one reveals the purple-written true instructions and jade chapters.

The *Scripture of Great Possession* states: The Imperial Minister holds the *True Scripture of the Great Grotto*, encased in a purple jade casket. It further says: The Lord of the Grand One holds the *Mysterious Scripture of the Cavernous Mystery and Great Possession*, encased in a yellow jade casket. It further says: The *Scripture of Great Possession* is written in gold-threaded jade characters to illuminate its chapters. It further says: The wondrous *Scripture of Great Possession* and the nine perfected statutes are examined and sealed within the golden repository and jade coffer.

The *Catalogue of the Feminine One of the Great Grotto* says: The *True Scripture of the Great Grotto* resides above the Nine Heavens, in the Great Possession Palace’s Terrace of the Grand Mystic. It further says: Within the Flowery Jade Hall, the Golden Elixir of the Immortal Mother lies, chasing the two luminaries of sun and moon.

The *Hidden Writ* states: Beneath the Western Mystic Mountain, within the Terrace of the Flowery Tower, lies the *Scripture of Yu Yi’s Neighboring Knots*. The Central Void of Wangwu Mountain also holds this scripture, though incomplete. Only in the High Terrace of the Supreme Thearch’s Mystic Palace and the Northern Chamber of Penglai Prefecture, where golden pillars and jade walls are inscribed, is it fully preserved.

The *Eight Simplicities Scripture* says: The Supreme Thearch declares: All perfected ones who receive the *Eight Simplicities Scripture of the Mystic Clarity* possess the catalogue of the Supreme Thearch. Only those destined to become perfected ones, as recorded in the jade slips of the Western Florescence Palace’s aquatic writings, may obtain this text. It further says: Upon the Western Tortoise Mountain, above the Dark Garden and north of the Accumulated Stones, the *True Scripture of the Eight Simplicities* is kept.

The *Primordial Record of Tortoise Mountain* states: The Crimson August Flying Mystic Purple Writ of Tortoise Mountain is treasured and concealed by the Queen Mother of the West. Its purport is profoundly recondite, and none without an immortal name may approach its catalogue. Those who obtain it have their names inscribed in the celestial registers of Tortoise Mountain. It further says: Within the Jade Flower Chamber, the Crimson Radiance Jade Writ lies.

The *Flying Feather Scripture* says: Within the Golden Terrace Chamber of Mount Emei, the *Flying Mystic Feather Scripture* is concealed. It further says: The Supreme Thearch’s *Flying Scripture* is hidden in the Sevenfold Radiant Purple Terrace of the Upper Clarity’s Upper Palace.

The *Five Treasures Scripture* states: The *Purple Writ of the Numinous Treasure* is secretly kept above the Nine Heavens, in the Terrace of the Grand Mystic. It further says: The *Seven Revolutions Dancing Heaven Scripture of the Divine Continent* is concealed in the Primordial Terrace of the Purple Heaven.

The *Jade Registers of the Three Primordials* says: Within the gates of the Three Passes of the Nine Heavens, the *Nine Heavenly Dragon Writ*, the *Three Primordials Cavernous Jade Registers*, and the *Flying Mystic Writ* are inscribed. It further says: Within the Three Mysteries Terrace, the *Jade Registers of Purple Writ* and the *Nine Heavenly True Writings* reside. It further says: Within the Western Sand Square Terrace, the registers of the Three Primordials’ perfected ones lie. It further says: Within the Terrace of the Morning Lamp, the *Flying Heavenly Register Writ* is kept, illuminating the heights of the Nine Heavens. It further says: Within the Golden Casement Terrace, the *Three Primordials Jade Registers* are inscribed. It further says: Within the Phoenix-Born Terrace, the *Golden Writ of the Supreme Perfected* lies.

The *Golden Slips and Jade Characters Scripture* says: There is a Yang Terrace of the Cavernous Heavens, wherein the *Jade Pendants and Golden Earrings Scripture* is kept.

The *Cavernous Radiance Golden Mystery Scripture* states: None but those whose names are recorded in the celestial charts and jade registers of the Thearch may hear or behold this scripture. Those who do so ascend as flying immortals of the Upper Clarity.

The *Dharma Wheel Scripture* says: The Supreme One Perfected of the Grand Mystic declared: In the past, I received the *Eight Gates Scripture of the Supreme Thearch of the Boundless* from the Lord of the Grand Dao of the Supreme Ultimate. After attaining the Dao, my rank was elevated to that of a perfected one.

Here the text unfolds in sacred continuity with the primordial:

This scripture shares its birth with the Primordial Beginning, enfolding heaven and earth, enduring through kalpas uncounted. None but those bearing the immortal’s seal may transmit it without transgression.

The *Celestial Terrestrial Compendium Scripture* states: The Supreme Jade Scriptures and Hidden Writings are all enshrined in separate caskets.

The *Roadside Scripture* says: Within the Eastern Well’s Flowery Grove Hall of the Cavernous Heavens, the *Inner Tone Jade Scripture* rests above.

The *Great Possession Scripture* declares: The Supreme Mystery Numinous Terrace holds the *Nine Perfected Luminous Regulations of the Mystic Capital* within.

The *Flying Dragon Hidden Instructions* records: The *Feathered Flight Scripture* is sealed in the Golden Chamber of Mount Emei’s summit.

The *Transmission of Daoist Learning* recounts: Within the cavernous chamber stand a golden city and jade mansion, where the true writ resides.

The *Inner Instructions of the Nine Perfected of the Upper Clarity* reveals: The Supreme Palace’s Loftiest Terrace bears the *Supreme Jade Dawn’s Yuyi Pounding Mortar Red Jade Writ* and the *Supreme Jade Dawn’s Jielin Pounding Moon Yellow Radiance Jade Chapter*—these two scriptures inscribed upon jade slips in golden characters.

The *Inner Tone Jade Character Scripture* states: The *Inner Tone* is sealed within the stone coffer of the Southern River’s cavernous chamber.

The *Five Talismans Scripture* says: The *Nine Heavens’ Numinous Writ* is sealed in a stone coffer.

The *Jade Instructions Scripture* records: The Southern Garden’s Cinnabar Fire River holds a cavernous chamber of the Three Origins, where jade coffers bear sealed inscriptions.

The *Demon-Dispelling Scripture* notes: A cache of immortal scriptures lies hidden in a desolate mountain, testing the hearts of the common.

The *Heaven-and-Earth Likeness Chapter* recounts: During the reign of Emperor Shun of the Later Han, a hundred fascicles of divine immortal scriptures were discovered above the springs of Quyang. Seventy fascicles within were inscribed on white silk with vermilion borders and azure headings in cinnabar script, titled *The Azure Dao’s Hidden Practice of the Supreme Peace*.

The Solar Orbital Generation Lord Sima Sheng bestowed upon Wu Commandery’s Shen Xi a text inscribed on white jade tablets with azure jade borders in cinnabar jade characters.

It further states: The *Upper Clarity* is written in cinnabar-gold script, demarcated with purple gold.

The *Three Origins Perfected Unity Scripture* says: The Chamber of Jasper Radiance holds the esoteric methods of the Three Origins’ Perfected Unity within.

The *Jade Radiance Eight Effulgences Scripture* declares: The Golden Splendor Purple Palace enshrines the *Golden Perfected Jade Radiance Eight Effulgences Scripture* within.

The *Upper Clarity Scripture* states: The Southern Culmen conceals the *Upper Clarity Scripture* upon its Jasper Terrace.

The *Biography of Lord Mao* recounts: The Golden Terrace seals the *Inner Scripture of the Supreme Perfected* within.

The *Three Daoist Sequences Scripture* says: The Southern Cavern’s chamber holds the *Three Daoist Scriptures* sealed by Lord Wang within.

The *Mystic Perfection Scripture* proclaims: The wondrous Dao of the Lofty Mystery and the secret chapters of the Jade Clarity are all bestowed upon those of golden names and jade characters—lofty immortals.

The *Nine Perfected Central Scripture* reveals: The Way of Racing Sun and Moon, the *Supreme Upper Clarity*, the *Great Ultimate Nine August Ones*, and the treasured secrets of the Four Bureau Perfected Ones are the jade chapters of the Mystic Origin Lord. None but those bearing golden watchtower jade names or Eastern Florescence purple characters may hear or behold them. These are the titles of the two chapters: *Yuyi Racing the Sun* and *Jielin Racing the Moon*.

The *Three Origins’ Dispensation Scripture* states: The *Supreme Treasure-Sealed Jade Slips of the Southern Culmen* remain unseen by those without mystic names or imperial charts, who cannot glimpse their fascicles.

The *Golden Feather Mystic Chapter Scripture*—this text remains hidden, untransmitted in the world. None but those bearing Orchid Terrace cinnabar characters may see or hear it.

The *Numinous Guest Perfected Unity Instructions* says: The *Cavernous Mystery Natural Scripture*, whose original text issues from the Supreme Dao, is boundless in its subtle intricacy, formless in its wondrous subtlety.

*Laozi* declares: Nothing in the world is more supple and weak than qi; nothing is more supple and weak than the Dao. That by which the Dao is supple and weak enfolds heaven, earth, and the myriad things. For the supple gives birth to the firm, and the weak gives birth to the strong—yet none in the world know the root from which they arise. Thus, being arises from non-being as its mother; non-being arises from emptiness as its mother; emptiness arises from the Dao as its mother. The natural is the root of the Dao. If one can take the natural as the true Dao, then the Dao may be attained and penetrated.

The *Supreme Scripture* states: The Dao is truly formless, hidden as the root of transformation. Scriptures possess written words, manifest as the beginnings of teaching. Masters possess embodied speech, whose comings and goings become the method. Speech and silence follow the moment—this is preservation at its finest. The goal is to reach the Dao through the white scriptures and the master. Master, scripture, and Dao are called the Three Treasures.

It further says: The root of transformation has three: the Dao, the scripture, and the master. The Great Dao is formless; scriptures serve as its steps. The scriptural texts are profound and wondrous, beyond the ken of the common. The sagely descend as masters to reveal the essential instructions to humanity.

*Laozi* says: The Dao is the mystery of the myriad things, the treasure of the good. The worthy obtain it and regard it as their true treasure; the foolish obtain it yet dare not lose the Dao. The Dao has no constant technique; virtue has no constant method. The spirit has no constant form; harmony has no constant appearance. The Dao is the central master, befriending stillness.

It further states: The *Nine-Writ Dragon Radiance* and *Purple Phoenix Vermilion Script* of ancient texts are stored within the Supreme Six Harmonies’ Purple Chamber, attended by heaven’s people.

The *Supreme Tenuity Yellow Writ Scripture* says: The Heavenly Perfected Three August Ones concealed the *Eightfold Assemblage* texts upon Mount Wei Yu, while the Supreme Tenuity Heavenly Thearch concealed one copy upon Mount Gui. These numinous writings of the Eightfold Assemblage possess no fixed character forms; their profundities are exhaustively pursued yet difficult to fathom in detail. They are called heavenly scriptures, naturally and utterly true. The qi of these Eightfold Assemblages harmonizes the fivefold tones—none but the most profound can fully comprehend them. The Heavenly Perfected August Person exhausted his vision to annotate their meaning. The Eightfold Assemblages’ many texts establish heaven and earth, inaugurate the transformation of humans and spirits, serve as the root of the myriad things, and govern the summoning of the Nine Heavens. The Celestial Thearch verifies and settles the charts and registers of divine immortals, administers the heavens’ divisions, pacifies states and quiets the people, restrains and commands Dengdu, subdues demons and vanquishes ghosts, commands the Water Thearch of kalpic destiny, and summons dragons to ascend the clouds. They discuss the kalpic cycles of heaven and earth, distinguish the names and clans of sagely perfected ones, and govern the manifold affairs of city towers and terraces. Their principles are broadly proclaimed, distinguishing the five directions’ primordial essences, the methods of ingesting and employing them to seek immortality and transform the body—all expounded through the wondrous subtlety of the natural, the emptiness of the correct and true, whose marvelous purport is luminous and complete.

Moreover, there are the *Jade Instructions*, wherein the Perfected of Heavenly Truth expound and elucidate the celestial script of the Eightfold Assemblies, establishing them as the correct intonation.

There are also the *Numinous Charts*, through which the Mysterious Sages manifest transformations, revealing numinous metamorphoses and depicting forms to expound principles, thereby rendering things easily comprehended.

The *Jade Emperor’s Registers of Lineage* record the names and clans of the sagely lords, tracing the ancestral origins, hereditary succession, and the ranks of divine officials.

The *Canons of Sincerity and Discipline* were established by the Mysterious Sages to measure the gravity of transgressions and blessings, setting forth statutes and ordinances to prevent and examine faults.

The *Scripture of Natural Dignity and Propriety* fully demonstrates the observances of purification and abstinence, the postures of reverence in ritual, the forms of advancement and withdrawal, and the norms and measures of conduct.

The *Methods* comprise the esoteric essentials of elixirs and medicines, divine herbs and numinous fungi, malleable gold, flowing water, and jade—all pertaining to the Dao of self-cultivation.

The *Arts and Numerologies* clarify the discernment of spirit through contemplation, the preservation of truth through mindfulness of the Dao, the purification of the heart and emptying of intent, wandering through emptiness and flying steps, ingesting and absorbing primordial harmony, guiding and conducting the Three Luminaries—these are the methods of immortal transcendence.

The *Records and Biographies* document the studies, attainments, and realizations of the Perfected, as well as the traces of those who have verified their fruits.

The *Scripture of Ascending Mystery* states: The *Inner Teachings of the Numinous Treasure* may be transmitted only to those who universally inspire faith among the people. One must uphold the precepts completely, harbor no inner defilements, relieve the orphaned and weak, shun evil and cultivate goodness, seek neither fame nor reputation, and regard praise and blame as equal. In secluded and remote places, one must diligently practice the Dao so that others may trust it. Like the four seasons, one must be unwavering; when discussing with the worthy, one must not cling obstinately to one’s own views—only then may the teachings be transmitted. Furthermore, one who ardently seeks superior methods, follows goodness as water flows downward, delights in drawing near to the wise and sagacious, and acts without suspicion or doubt; who is discerning and able to distinguish truth from falsehood, cautious in speech and measured in conduct; who is gentle and without transgression, able to honor teachers superior to oneself without arrogance or disrespect, and values their teachings as a pauper values treasure; who reveres and serves their masters without shirking toil, and whose desire for instruction remains unwavering day and night—only such a one may be entrusted with the scriptures.

The text further states: Those who obtain the *Arrayed Chronicles of Supreme Purity* may become Perfected of the Great Ultimate. If one can recite them, one may ascend to become a Lord of Supreme Purity. Those who possess the *Hidden Writings of Jade Purity* shall attain true immortality in a single day and night, discoursing on the Dao and expounding its wonders. Those who hold the *Bright Statutes of the Four Poles* shall have the Jade Emperor dispatch the divine soldiers of the Five Directions, with the Three Officials of Left and Right supervising and regulating the numinous texts.

The *Scripture of the Numinous Treasure* states: The *Five Chapters of True Writ in Vermilion Script of the Primordial Commencement’s Cavernous Mystery and Numinous Treasure* existed prior to the Primordial Commencement, within the emptiness of the Cavernous Void, before heaven and earth took root, before the sun and moon shone, in the profound obscurity where there was neither ancestor nor clan. The numinous writ flickered in and out of existence, ethereal and elusive. The Two Modes awaited it to divide the Great Yang; they awaited it to bring forth illumination. The numinous charts evolved with the turning of the cosmos, the celestial images shifted with the reckoning of time, and in response to the moment and in accord with destiny, it came into being. Heaven and earth, receiving it, became distinct; the Three Luminaries, receiving it, radiated light. The numinous writ flourished in splendor, illuminating the Supreme Purity with its resplendence. It emerged from the Celestial Realm of Primordial Azure, its hues unbounded by fixed directions, its branches and configurations intricate beyond all tracing or inquiry. First refined in the Hall of Cavernous Yang, tempered in the Court of Flying Fire, its true writ was clarified, its radiance gleaming brilliantly. As the qi of Cavernous Yang is vermilion, it is called the Vermilion Script. Heaven treasures it to bring about ascent; earth conceals it to ensure stability. The Five Thearchs reward it, thereby securing the governance of the Three Luminaries and ascending to lofty brilliance. The Supreme Sages uphold it to attain truth; the Five Marchmounts follow it to gain numinosity. The Son of Heaven obtains it to achieve good governance; the state enjoys it to attain great peace. The wondrous power of the imperial numinous writ marks the mysterious root of heaven and earth. Its majestic numinosity expands boundlessly, universally bestowing infinite blessings. Vast and transformative, it is the ancestor of divine luminosity. Its measure is unfathomable, towering as the great void. It gives birth to heaven and establishes earth, inaugurating the transformations of divine luminosity. Above, it is called the *Numinous Bestowal that Pacifies the Five Marchmounts and Preserves the State for Eternity*; below, it is called the *Numinous Treasure’s Mysterious Wonder, the Most Exalted of All Things*.

It further states: The *Eightfold Might of the Supreme* now follows the *Five Talismans of the Numinous Treasure*. There is a talisman named the *Supreme’s Eightfold Might* for subduing tigers, leopards, and mountain spirits. The *Scripture of the Golden Truth and Jade Radiance of the Supreme’s Hidden Writ* is the transmission of the Jade Dawn of the Supreme. The *Mysterious and Profound Scripture of the Great Existence* is the transmission of the Queen Mother of the West. The *Jade Pendants and Golden Earrings of the Golden Writ of the Great Ultimate* is the transmission of the Great Lord Emperor of Fusang. The *Scripture of Feathered Flight* is the transmission of the Yellow Venerable Lord of the Center. The *Hidden Writ of the Great Night’s Jade Chapters* is the transmission of the Supreme Thearch. All these transmissions possess true scriptures, though some may hold high rank yet practice inferior methods, or bear heavy responsibilities yet occupy humble positions. These transmissions, though containing new methods, take the *Inner Scripture of the Yellow Court* as their foundation, which is the *Scripture of the Great Ultimate*. The *Scripture of Vermilion Cinnabar, Golden Essence, Stone Radiance, and Water Mother* resembles the *Purple Writ Method of Ingesting Solar Essence*, the *Celestial August Symbol Talismans* for harmonizing primordial qi, and the *Yellow Writ and Vermilion Realm*—the essentials of longevity.

The *Scripture of the Cavernous Mystery of the Perfected* states: The *Golden Pavilion of the Great One*, the *Hidden Registers of the Five Stars*, the *Seven Talismans of Later Sages*, the *Stone Casket of Hollow Mountain*, the *Vermilion Terrace’s Mysterious Yellow Chapters*, and the *Embracing Chart of the Heavenly Mother of the Five Phases*—none may hear or behold the supreme Dao.

The *Scripture of the Cavernous Perfection* states: The *Jade Chamber* contains the *Thirty-Nine Plain Words*, the *Supreme Transformation of the Mysterious Elixir*, and the *Dao of the Three Perfected and Cavernous Primordial*—all concealed within. It further states: The *Supreme Conceals the Three Primordials’ Jade Regulations*, and within its secluded chamber, the *Three Primordials’ Scripture* is arrayed. This is the secret repository of the *Nine Elixirs’ Writ of the Supreme Immortals*, guarded by the Lord Emperor of the Celestial Microcosm. The Five Elders of the Primordial Commencement further conceal the *Five Chapters of True Writ* within.

It further states: Within the Jade Leather Green Palace of the Azure Lad of the Eastern Sea’s Lesser Florescence, in the eastern hall’s shelves, there are three hundred volumes of precious scriptures and nine thousand chapters of jade instructions. These govern the registers of those who study immortality and are bestowed upon those destined to become Perfected. They are overseen by the Jade Dawn’s Supervisor of Immortal Attendants. It further states: The *Five Elders’ Precious Scripture of the Mysterious Numinous Terrace* and the *Three Perfected’s Scripture of the Cavernous Primordial of the Golden Terrace of the Eight Gates of the Mysterious Mother* are concealed within.

It further states: Upon the Nine Heavens’ Pass Terrace, there are the jade names of the Supreme August Great Perfected High Emperor and the registers of the Later Sage Perfected, overseen by the Great Abiding Jade Dawn’s Supervisor.

The *Jade Scripture of the Great Cavern* states: The Jade Dawn extends its golden-flowered hall, while the Supreme Writs are inscribed upon luminous jade tablets.

It further states: Dragon Mountain is the name of a high terrace within the Jade Purity Heaven, wherein the Heavenly Emperor’s jade name resides.

It further states: The Ten Thousand Flowered Palace holds the Supreme Emperor’s precious scriptures and the Jade Purity’s hidden writings.

The *Scripture of the Great Cavern* states: There is a Dark Cloud Feather Chamber, wherein the Yellow and Old Primordial Lord’s sealed scriptures are kept.

It further states: The Yellow and Old Primordial Lord’s sealed scriptures reside within the Plain Jade Terrace and the Northern Frigid Golden Terrace.

It further states: There is the Hearing-the-Wind Jade Terrace, which governs the registers of those who study the Dao and attain immortality.

It further states: The Feminine One’s jade tally is concealed above the Nine Heavens, within the Great Existence, named the Supreme Mystery Numinous Terrace.

It further states: There is a Pristine Jade Hall, wherein the *Perfect Scripture of the Great Cavern* is kept.

It further states: The *Perfect Scripture of the Great Cavern* comprises the secret signs of the Three and Five, the utmost essence of the true Dao, the supreme chapters of the Three Ones, together with the Jade Purity’s forbidden instructions and the Highest’s secret scrolls.

The *Supreme Nine Perfected Luminous Regulations Scripture* further states: The *Perfect Scripture of the Great Cavern*, the *Feminine One’s Precious Scripture*, and the *Plain Numinous Wondrous Scripture*—the three marvelous chapters—are the Supreme Jade Emperor’s precious scrolls, concealed above the Nine Heavens, within the Great Existence’s palace, in the Jade Chamber of the Supreme Mystery Numinous Terrace.

The Three Registers are the origins of all scriptures: the Golden Register, the Yellow Register, and the Jade Register.

As for the *Scriptures of the Numinous Treasure*, there are inner and outer teachings. The outer teachings include miscellaneous doctrines, expounded according to each person’s understanding, not necessarily exhaustively, but to guide the learner toward enlightenment. The inner teachings are the wondrous arts of the True One, arising from the innermost heart; through virtuous practice, one attains the Dao, which does not come from without. If the Dao could be obtained externally, it would be bestowed upon the utterly true, unchanging, and eternally abiding.

The Three August Scriptures are: the *Jade Purity Cavern-Real*, the *Highest Purity Cavern-Mystery*, and the *Supreme Purity Cavern-Spirit*.

The *Supreme Ultimate Hidden Annotations of Precious Instructions Scripture* further states: When receiving the Three Cavern Scriptures, one must renounce worldly affairs to practice them.

The Three Caverns are collectively named the *Supreme Cavern-One*, the highest of scriptures.

The *Perfect Scripture of the Great Cavern* is also called the *Supreme Perfected Dao Scripture* or the *Supreme Purity’s Highest Dao Observing Heaven Scripture*. It contains the Highest Purity’s loftiest principles, the subtlest words of the utmost truth, and the wondrous scriptures of flying immortals.

The *Scriptures of the Numinous Treasure* are also called the *Cavern-Mystery* or the *Supreme*, as the *Ascending Mystery Scripture* states: They are the highest grade of transcendent immortals, the utmost truth of emptiness and non-being, and the profound praise of the Great Dao.

The Three August Heavenly Writs are also called the *Cavern-Spirit*, the *Cavern-Immortal*, or the *Supreme Jade Strategies*.

These Three Cavern Scriptures are the guiding principles of the Dao’s talismans, the mysterious lineage of the Great Void, and the foremost scriptures of the Highest Perfected. How could they be known to middling immortals?

The *Golden Register Simplified Writ Scripture* further states: The Three Cavern Precious Scriptures are the natural celestial writings.

The *Supreme Supreme Perfected Regulations Scripture* further states: When the great transformation first arose and human customs were pure, the Three Treasures saved the three grades of people. The *Cavern-Spirit* is named the Dao of the Immortal Treasure, corresponding to the era of the Three August Ones. The *Cavern-Mystery* is named the Dao of the Numinous Treasure, illuminating the Three Powers and saving the era of the Five Emperors. The *Cavern-Real* is named the Dao of the Heavenly Treasure, recording the methods of purity and rectitude to aid the eras after the Three Dynasties.

The *Supreme Granary of Primordial Qi Scripture* further states: The Three Cavern Scriptures are the *Cavern-Real of the Highest Purity*, the *Cavern-Mystery of the Numinous Treasure*, and the *Cavern-Spirit of the Three August Ones*.

The *Numinous Writ Scripture* further states: In the Dragon-Han era, the Primordial Commencement composed the Ten Division Scriptures and told the Queen Mother of the West: Within the Supreme Purple Tenuity Palace, the golden tally and jade writings of the *Numinous Treasure True Writs* contain wondrous scriptures.
