Their titles are now revealed, all inscribed in gold upon jade slips, with their chapter headings displayed at the southern pavilion of the Purple Tenuity Palace. The Jade Capital Mountain of the Supreme Mystery Capital also records their texts in full.

The *Arrayed Records of the Dao Lord* states: If within the Three Primordial Palaces there are pearl tablets with azure writings, then the northern celestial physiognomy of a purple brain and brocade tongue marks one as an immortal.

The Fifteenth Division of the Dao concludes.
The Sixteenth Division of the Dao begins.

Here follows the translation:

---

The *Principles and Locations*
The *Chart of the Five Sacred Mountains’ Names* states: The affiliations of nature, life, soul, and spirit all possess their proper principles and locations.

The *Classic of Divine Marvels* says: On Kunlun stands a bronze pillar, towering into the clouds—this is the so-called Pillar of Heaven. Its circumference spans three thousand *li*, perfectly round as if carved. Below it lie the nine bureaus of the immortal courts. It further states: Kunlun has three peaks. One peak faces due north, aligned with the celestial stem *chen*, and is named *Hearing-the-Wind Summit*. Another faces due west, called *Mystic Garden Terrace*. The third faces due east, named *Kunlun Palace*. Above it stand twelve jade towers, where radiant clouds reflect the sun and crimson auroras glow with ninefold brilliance. This is the seat of the Queen Mother of the West, the revered abode of true officials and transcendents.

The *Hidden Instructions for Ascending to Perfection* states: The realm of Supreme Purity is the gateway of the Nine Heavens. The Supreme August Emperor and the Jade Sovereign gather the host of spirits therein to determine the karmic fortunes of all under heaven. It further says: The Western Florescence Hall lies in Supreme Purity, where the Queen Mother resides. It further says: The Hall of Cultivated Virtue is the dwelling of Zhang Shu-yin. It further says: The Eight Radiance City lies in Supreme Purity, where the Jade Dawn Dao dwells. It further says: The Crimson City of Great Primordiality is the abode of perfected persons. It further says: In Supreme Purity stands the Yang Liao Palace, where the Supreme August Emperor and Jade Sovereign assemble the host of perfected beings. It further says: The Hall of Rare Forest stands atop the Eight Stilling Mountains in the Eastern Sea of Supreme Purity, where the Supreme Emperor dwells. It further says: The Jasper Palace lies within the Golden Portals of Supreme Purity, where the Sage Sovereign resides. It further says: Within the realm of Supreme Purity stands the Cinnabar City and Purple Terrace, where the Supreme August Emperor and Jade Sovereign convene. It further says: The Sevenfold Numinous Terrace lies in the realm of Supreme Purity, where the Jade Dawn Dao Lord dwells. It further says: The Terrace of Illuminated Perfection stands atop the Eight Stilling Great Mountain in the Eastern Sea of Supreme Purity, where the Emperor resides. It further says: The Terrace of Na-fu lies on the Eastern Florescence Mountain of the Square Cauldron within the realm of Supreme Purity, where the Azure Lad dwells. It further says: Within the realm of Supreme Purity stands the Terrace of Rare Forest, where the Supreme Emperor and Dao Lord reside.

Dongfang Shuo’s *Record of the Ten Continents* says: There is the Hall of Radiant Jasper, where the Queen Mother of the West resides.

The *Three-Nine Simplex Sayings* states: The Orchid Terrace Palace is the dwelling of the Jade Maiden of Red Cassia. The Jade Chamber Palace is the dwelling of the daughter of the Yellow Emperor.

The *Record of the Ten Continents* says: On the Canglang Sea Island stands the Chamber of Accumulated Stones, filled with stone elephants and the eight varieties of stone: *nao*-stone, cinnabar-stone, and osmanthus-essence. It further says: The Purple Stone Palace is the seat of governance for the Nine Elder Transcendents. It further says: Kunlun Mountain is also called Kunling Mountain or Mystic Garden Terrace. Atop it lie the Garden of Accumulated Stones and the Great Smelting Well, where the Queen Mother holds her banquets. It further says: On Kunlun stands the Jasper Flower Chamber, where the Queen Mother of the West resides. It further says: The Dark Continent lies in the northern sea at the *hai* direction, where the Lord of the True Countenance of Supreme Mystery holds governance. It further says: The Gathered Casket Continent lies in the Western Sea, bordering Kunlun to the north. Many true transcendents and officials dwell there, and among its creatures are the *bi-xie* and celestial deer. On the continent grows a great tree resembling the maple, its fragrant blossoms detectable for *li* around. It further says: On the Island of Divine Transcendents stand purple stone palaces, the seat of governance for the Nine Elder Transcendents, where tens of thousands of immortal officials reside. It further says: Fangzhang lies in the Eastern Sea, where the Three Heavenly Controllers of Destiny dwell, and all transcendents come and go upon it.

The *Perfect Scripture of the Great Cavern* says: On the Three Primordial Mountains of Supreme Simplicity stands the Palace of the Central Yellow and Grand Unity, the abode of the Supreme Emperor. It further says: The Great Dao Lord of the Jade Dawn governs the Jeweled Conch Shell Portals. It further says: The Jade Sovereign Dao Lord resides in the Azure Cloud City, with jade steps and patterned terraces. It further says: The Jade Countenance Hall is the leisurely abode of the Void-and-Nothingness Perfected, as well as the Hall of Radiance of true *qi*. It further says: The Jade Countenance Hall is the Hall of Radiance of the Supreme, the repository of talismans and registers of those who attain the Dao. It further says: The Myriad Florescence Palace lies in the Heaven of Jade Perfection of Lesser Existence, where the Master of Lesser Existence holds governance. It further says: The Palace of Absolute Emptiness lies north of the Dark Continent, where the Nine Perfected Transcendent Lords and the Celestial Controller of Prohibitions convene with the host of transcendents. It further says: The Round Florescence Palace is the dwelling of the Yellow and the Old. It further says: Within the Great Auroras dwells the Primordial Lady of the Great Void. It further says: On Mount Flourishing Splendor, the Perfected of the Great Ultimate calls it the Round Brightness Cinnabar Chamber, where the Five Numinous Lords reside. It further says: The Azure Essence Lord ascends the Purple Void Mountain and transforms within the Jade Chamber. It further says: On Kunlun Mountain stands the Hall of Flowing Clouds of Golden Elixir, reaching upward to the turning pivot of the celestial mechanism and downward into the Great Chamber, where the Queen Mother of the West holds governance and the female transcendents reside. It further says: The Jade Chamber is the dwelling of the Azure Essence Lord. It further says: The Three Primordial Lords of Flourishing Splendor dwell in the Chamber of Flowing Leisure. It further says: In the Great Void stands the Chamber of Great Auroras, its halls built upon the convergence of ninefold clouds, where the Primordial Lady of the Great Void resides. It further says: The Azure Florescence Chamber is where the Azure Lad rides a jade-carved chariot, guiding the orb of round pearl-*qi* into the mountain chamber. It further says: The Chamber of the Great Elder lies among the Eight August Ones of Supreme Purity, where the Old Lord rides a broad jade carriage to enter. It further says: Atop Flowing Rigidity Mountain stands the Chamber of Radiant Scenery, the seat of governance of the Queen Mother of the West.

The *Scripture of the Golden Root* says: The Imperial Lord of the Azure Essentials resides in the Jade Mound Kingdom, within a palace of yellow gold and purple, where the Imperial Lord of the Azure Essentials dwells. It further says: The eight-gated celestial beings scatter incense between them, and above the gates stands a golden terrace. On the nine-tiered terrace, the Jade Dawn Guardian Lord ascends to dwell. There is a palace of golden radiance and purple, the Golden Portals of the Later Sage, where the Imperial Lord resides.

The *Scripture of Supreme Purity* says: The Jade Terrace and Cinnabar Numinous Palace of the Southern Culmen Controller of Destiny for Long Life in Supreme Purity also lie in the Orchid Court and Cloud Terrace, and ascend into the Purple Jasper Terrace of Absolute Emptiness. It further says: In the center stands the Purple Tenuity and Mystic Jasper Palace, where the Yellow and the Old Lord reside.

---

It further states: The Chamber of Layered Birth within the Hall of Void Concord is the leisurely dwelling of the Supreme Great Dao Lord. It also says: The Primordial Origin resides at the Purple Cloud Gates, with Azure Radiance forming its walls. It further says: There is the Chamber of the Yellow Chamber, the Hall of Single-Stone Jade Countenance, where the True Dawn Dao Lord governs within. The Lofty Terrace of Mystic Reverence is where the Heavenly Master pays homage. It also says: There is the Chamber of the Swallow Immortals, where the Heavenly Master instructs and transforms.

The *Southern Perfected Sayings* states: The Queen Mother of the West’s daughter, named Female Charm with the style Shenlin, governs Canglang Mountain and receives scriptures to become the Cloud Forest Lady. It further says: Li Qingbin’s daughter, a disciple of the Northern Primordial Central Mystery Dao Lord, receives scriptures to become the Spirit Illuminating Literary Person of the Eastern Palace, governing within the Thirteenth Vermilion Pavilion of Fangzhang Terrace. It also says: Langye is the prefecture of Langfeng. Above Kunlun lie the Nine Prefectures, which are the Nine Palaces of the Great Ultimate, serving as the abodes of the Great Palace’s various immortals—all officials of the Nine Palaces. As for Perfected Persons, they are the dukes and ministers of the Nine Palaces. It further says: The various palaces of the Great Square are the constant governing places of the Azure Lord; those above are all celestial perfected and lofty immortals, the dukes and ministers of the Great Ultimate, and the dwelling places of the various Controllers of Destiny. There is a method of ingesting the radiance of the sun and moon; though they have already attained the Dao and become perfected, they still practice it. Huoshan and Chicheng are also prefectures of the Controllers of Destiny, where only the Supreme Primordial Perfected Person, the Lady of the Southern Marchmount, resides. Li Zhongfu is in the West, Han Zhong in the South, and the remaining thirty-two Controllers of Destiny should all be in Donghua. The Azure Lad of Eastern Florescence is the Grand Controller of Destiny who oversees all. Yang Jun also departed to serve in the Eastern Hub, though it is unknown which rank he holds.

It further says: On Mount Juqu, the Three Lords Mao of Han govern above, each riding a white crane to gather at their dwelling. At times, people have seen the mountain produce gold. During the reign of Emperor Ling of Han, an imperial edict commanded commanderies and counties to mine gold from Juqu to fill the armories. By the time of Sun Quan, he again dispatched guardsmen to mine gold, which was regularly delivered to the court.

It further says: Northwest of Fangzhang lies the great Yin Cheng Mountain, and southwest of Canglang lies the great Yang Chang Mountain. Many true immortals dwell upon these mountains, which mark the signs of the Ninefold Calamities and Sixfold Destructions. On Xiuhua Mountain stands the Jade Hall, where the Five Numinous Perfected Lords reside. It also says: Above Golden Florescence Mountain lie the Five Palaces, where the Great One dwells. It further says: Above the Dark Continent stands the Chamber of Scenic Radiance, the governing place of the Queen Mother of the West.

The *Scripture of the Seven Transformations and Seven Changes of the Divine Continent* states: By the banks of the Western Ridge’s Mengfan, within the Purple Tenuity Jade Hall, is where the Queen Mother requested the numinous and plain chapters. The *Hidden Formula of the Flying Dragon* says: The Northern Ultimate Perfected Lord governs within the Northern Ultimate’s Vast Void Chamber. The *Feminine One Chapter of the Great Cavern* states: The Three Primordial Lords reside in the Chamber of Primordial Void.

The *Preface of the Primordial Origin* says: The Cinnabar Numinous Vermilion Hall stands in the Great Clarity’s Supreme Mystery, where the King Metropolis Dao Lord requested the Perfected Writings. There is also the Hall of Jade Treasure, where the August Honored One dwells. The *Inner Transmission of Lord Wang* states: The Purple Clarity and Great Simplicity, the Jasper Gate and Great Simplicity, are where the Three Primordial Dao Lords govern. The *Scripture of the Cavern Mystery* says: The Purple Jade Gates of the Great Ultimate are where the Great Ultimate Primordial Perfected Lord governs. Since the inception of heaven and earth, the registers of human life and death have been kept within.

The *Jade Clarity Writings* state: The Jade Door and Jasper Gate are where the Nine August Supreme Perfected Ones reside. The *Inner Transmission of Lord Mao* says: Within the Heaven of Jade Clarity stands the Scattered Blossoms Terrace, where the Four Dipper and Seven Dawn Dao Lords govern. The *Accounts of the Arrayed Immortals* states: The Jade Terrace of the Great Void is where the Great Peace Dao Lord resides. The *Eight Effulgences Flying Scripture of Supreme Clarity* says: The Jade Treasure Terrace is where the Three Primordial Lords ascend. The *Scripture of the Three Primordial Perfected Ones* states: The Yellow Gates and Purple Doors of the Chamber of Dark Essence are where the Three Ones, the Venerable Lords within the body, constantly abide.

The *Scripture of Divine Invocations* says: The Supreme Mystery Hall is where the celestial beings reside. The *Scripture of Fundamental Conduct* states: There are the Cavern Chambers of the Three Primordials, where the Wondrous Perfected dwell. The *Transmissions of Daoist Learning* says: At the Swallow’s Mouth of Mount Mao, the female Daoist adept Qian ascended the altar as a Wondrous Perfected. The *Scripture of Fixed Resolve* states: The Heavenly Honored One’s tranquil dwelling is the Seven Treasures Purple Tenuity Palace of the Primordial Yang of the Mystic Capital. The *Scripture of the Great One’s Cavern Perfection* says: There is the Palace of the Purple Chamber of the Great Ultimate, where the Heavenly Emperor’s Treasure Spirits reside. The *Scripture of Jade Clarity* states: The Jade Clarity Palace is where the Lofty Perfected and Jade Emperor come and go.

The *Records of the Cavern Unseen* says: The Lofty Hall of Yidu stands in the Sea of Purple Mud, where Dongfang Shuo rested and feasted. The *Scripture of the Cavern Perfection* states: The Great Elder’s Repose Hall is where the Eight August Elder Lords reside. The *Scripture of the Three Primordials’ Jade Tallies* says: The Hall of Vast Numinosity is where the Great Simplicity Three Primordial Lords reside, within the Heaven of Supreme Clarity. The *Scripture of the Eight Gates of the Mystic Mother* states: The Hall of the Five Penetrations is where the Five Penetrations Emperor Lords reside within. It further says: The Scattered Blossoms Jade Chamber is where the Three Simplicity Primordial Lords reside.

The *Hidden Writings of Jade Clarity* says: The Jasper Grove Hall is where the Supreme August Jade Emperor rests and feasts. The *Transmissions of Daoist Learning* states: Within the cavern chamber lies the Hall of Great Yin, where the Dragon Might Elder saw the Perfected Writings. The *Primordial Records of Mount Gui* says: The Writings Cavern Chamber is where the Upper Primordial Lord sits. Ge Hong’s *Traditions of Divine Transcendents* states: On Golden Florescence Mountain stands a stone chamber, the hermitage of Huang Chuping of Danxi. The *Inner Transmission of the Perfected Lord Wang of Pure Emptiness* says: The cavern of Mount Weiyu extends ten thousand *li* in circumference, named Great Existence and Luminous Void, where the Heavenly Marshal Ji Zhu resides. It further says: The cavern of the Jade Mountain in the Western Regions extends three thousand *li* in circumference, named Supreme Mystery, where the Celestial Controller of Destiny of the Assembly of Perfected Ones resides.

*The Record of Famous Mountains* states: To the southwest of Yizhou lies Mount Qingcheng, also called Mount Qingchengjun, its shape resembling a walled city. Within the mountain are cliff dwellings, the place where Celestial Master Zhang of the Red Wall conducted his teachings. To the south, it connects with Mount Emei, whose distant peaks appear as two verdant ridges, like the brows of a silkworm moth. There are also cavern-heavens where sacred scriptures are stored, though it is unknown which numbered cavern-heaven this is. It further states: The cavern of Red City and Cinnabar Mountain extends three hundred *li* in circumference, named the Upper Clarity Jade Level Heaven. Beneath this mountain lies a terrace spanning two hundred *li*, the residence of the Celestial Controller of Destiny.

*The Scripture of the Jade Capital* says: On the Jade Capital Mountain of the Dark Metropolis stands a Seven Treasures City, where the Supreme Non-Ultimate Great Dao and the Void Sovereign Lord hold court, the Dark Metropolis of the Lofty Transcendents.

*The Scripture of Great Existence* says: The Grand Clarity’s Ultimate Mystery Palace lies above the Primordial Radiance, where the Supreme Lord resides.

*The Scripture of the Three Primordials’ Cloth* says: Within the Upper Clarity Jade Radiance Palace dwell those who wear the Three Primordials’ Cloth.

*The Scripture of the Dao’s Proximity* says: The Luminous Flower Jade Hall is where the Five Numinous Perfected Ones reside. It further says: The Cavern Perfection Hall is where the Celestial Venerable of Primordial Beginning, the Supreme Sage Lord, expounded the Great Precepts of Observing the Body.

*The Scripture of Ascending Mystery* says: The Jade Clarity Terrace is where transcendents and sages wander and delight.

*The Scripture of the Seven Stars’ Shifting Degrees* says: The Imperial Lord ascends the Jade Terrace of the Great Ultimate.

*The Scripture of the Upper Origin* says: The Immortal Duke Mei Zhu resides on Mount Nanyue.

*The Scripture of the Five Talismans* says: The August Person dwells on Mount Emei’s northern side, beneath sheer cliffs in a dwelling of azure jade.

*The Primordial Records of Mount Gui* says: In the Western Florescence Purple Pavilion reside the Jade Maidens.

*The Scripture of Divine Invocations* says: Within the Chamber of Ninefold Union dwells the Supreme Lord.

*The Scripture of Wang Chen’s Bright Mirror* says: There is the Chamber of Great Mystery, Jade Dawn, and Golden Florescence, where the Three Primordial Ladies of the Plain reside.

*The Declarations of the Perfected* says: To the southwest of Great Mount Mao lies Fourfold Level Mountain, commonly called Square Mountain. Beneath it is a cavern chamber named the Square Terrace Cavern, connected with Huayang and known as a separate abode of secluded halls, where those who attain the Dao reside. It further says: Beneath Square Lateral Mountain lies a cavern chamber named the Square Source Lodge, where recluses dwell. It further says: Beneath Mount Bao lies a stone chamber with silver doors, a hundred *li* in circumference. It further says: There is the Altar of the Celestial Market, where Fan Qiulin received oral instructions. It further says: Within the Preserved Square Terrace, the transcendent Cai Tiansheng secluded himself. It further says: The Pure Emptiness Palace is where Sima Jizhu concealed himself. It further says: The Accumulated Stone Terrace is where the Young Master Zhu resided. It further says: The Chamber of Tranquil Repose is where Master Juan dwelled. It further says: The Transcendent Duke of Penglai, Luo Guangxiu, governed Mount Penglai. It further says: Xu Yufu dwelled in the cavern of Square Mountain, serving as the Transcendent Duke of Upper Clarity. It further says: Xianmen now resides in the Golden Court of Mount Meng’s great cavern, having received scriptures to become the Middle Primordial Transcendent Minister. It further says: Ninety *li* east of Mianzhu County in Guanghan Prefecture lies a mountain where Han Zhong once attained transcendence. A great copper stone marks the site, corresponding to the Winnowing Basket constellation. It further says: One hundred fifty *li* from Chengdu in Xindu County of Guanghan Prefecture stands a mountain with divine mushrooms and sacred herbs. Before it lies a pond with five spirit fish. Here, Wang Fangping once met the Supreme Lord, corresponding to the Dipper constellation. It further says: In Nadu County of Yuejun Prefecture lies a lesser mountain, with the greater one named Mount Mengzhi, whose height is unmatched. Yi Yin studied the Dao here. Above grow golden-fluid mushrooms and herbs of immortality; consuming them transcends the world, corresponding to the Straddler constellation. It further says: On Cloud Terrace Mountain grows a single peach tree, flowering once every three years and fruiting once every five, suspended above a bottomless ravine. Only Zhao Sheng dared cast himself down to retrieve the peach, while others could not, corresponding to the Stomach constellation. It further says: On Heavenly Pillar Mountain, a Jade Maiden rides a white crane, and transcendents ride white deer before the Cloud Terrace. Two steles stand there. It further says: The Jade Bureau Precinct lies south of Chengdu. In the first month of the first year of Yongshou, on the seventh day, the Supreme Lord rode a white deer, and Celestial Master Zhang rode a white crane to this place, where they established the bureau’s foundation. Its jade-like appearance gave it the name Jade Bureau, corresponding to the Ghost constellation. It further says: Mount Zhong lies beyond the Weak River in the land of the Northern Sea’s waters. There, divine herbs grow spontaneously, and transcendents cultivate mushrooms, measuring fields by *qing* and *mu* like rice paddies. Above a jade spring stands the Palace of the Nine Sources Elder, who governs the water spirits of the world. It further says: Fusang lies in the Azure Sea, the palace of the Great Emperor, where the Supreme Perfected Eastern King holds court. It further says: Atop Mount Penglai stands the Nine Heavens Perfected Palace, the dwelling of the Supreme Perfected Transcendents.

*The Scripture of the Jade-Frost Transcendent Mountains* says: The Square Reservoir Palace is governed by the Azure Lad; the Great Cinnabar Palace by the Southern Culmen Primordial Lord; the White Mountain Palace by the Supreme Plain Perfected Lord; and the Western City Palace by the Controller of All Perfected Ones.

*The Regulations of the Supreme Perfected* says: Within the Boundless Palace dwells the Loftiest Supreme Perfected.

*The Primordial Records of Mount Gui* says: The Golden Florescence Palace is where the Western Florescence Jade Maiden resides.

*The Scripture of Upper Clarity* says: The Opening Gold Palace is where the Jade Treasure Ninefold Heavens Elder dwells; the Sevenfold Radiance Palace, where the Purple Radiance Ninefold Heavens Perfected One dwells; the Jade Clarity Primordial Treasure Palace, where the Loftiest Void Sovereign Lord resides; the Golden Numinous Palace, where the Purple Void Loftiest Primordial August Dao Lord dwells; the Vermilion Numinous Palace, where the Supreme August Void Lord resides; the Cavern Cloud Palace, where the August Thearch Lord dwells; the Golden Splendor Palace, where the Purple August Lord resides; the Numinous Radiance Palace, where the Lofty Pavilion Lord dwells; the Transformation Palace, where the Jade August Master resides; the Jade Treasure Palace, where the Purple Essence Lord dwells; the Flying Mystery Palace, where the Mystery One Lord dwells; and the Mystery Supreme Palace, where the Jade August Master resides.

The Transformation Cloud Palace, where the Grand Thearch Lord dwells; the Golden Gate Palace, where the August Thearch Lord resides; the Yang Brightness Palace, where the Cavern Perfected Lord dwells; the Primordial Radiance Palace, where the Grand Simplicity Lord resides; the Purple Jade Palace, where the Northern Mystery Lord dwells; the Spirit-Receiving Palace, where the Southern Vermilion Lord dwells; the Sound-and-Light Palace, where the Western Florescence Lord dwells; the Numinous Gold Palace, where the Central Primordial Lord dwells; the Purple Tenuity Palace, where the Eastern Brilliance Lord dwells; the Phoenix-Born Palace, where the Loftiest Lord dwells; the Luminous Model Palace, where the Primordial Stellar Lord dwells; the Sevenfold Jade Palace, where the Ninefold Primordial Lord dwells; the Luxuriant Forest Palace, where the Grand Brilliance Lord dwells; the Cloudy Forest Palace, where the Primordial Numinous Lord dwells; the Cavern Empyrean Palace, where the Threefold Primordial Lord dwells; the Returning Fragrance Palace, where the Primordial Illumination Lord resides; the Longevity Palace, where the Grand Ultimate Primordial Lord dwells; the Lofty Void Palace, where the Purple Primordial Lord dwells; the Flying Mystery Palace, where the Supreme Perfected Most Ancient Lord resides; the Jasper Countenance Palace, where the Cavern Radiance Lord dwells; the Radiant Jasper Palace, where the Grand Yang Lord dwells; the Illuminated Perfection Palace, where the Radiance Primordial Lord dwells; the Purple Brilliance Palace, where the Director of Destinies Lord dwells; the Penetrating Mystery Palace, where the Heavenly Thearch Lord dwells; the Golden Florescence Palace, where the Yellow Chamber Lord dwells; the Heavenly Thearch Palace, where the Grand Unity Lord dwells.

The Leisurely Clarity Mansion, where the Ninefold Heavens Venerable One dwells. There is also the Cinnabar Mansion, where the Three Heavens Jade Lads reside; the Dark Profundity Mansion, where the Jade Treasure Ninefold Empyrean Venerable One dwells; the Phoenix-Born Mansion, where the Ninefold Empyrean Perfected One dwells; the Gold Mansion, where the Numinous August Lord dwells; the Cinnabar Spirit Mansion, where the Supreme August Primordial Dao Lord dwells; the Life-and-Perfection Mansion, where the Jade Void Lord dwells; the Gold Soul Mansion, where the Myriad Beginnings Master dwells; the Task-of-Void Mansion, where the August Thearch Lord dwells; the Purple Brilliance Mansion, where the Purple August Lord dwells; the Divine Transformation Mansion, where the Central Primordial Lord dwells; the Ninefold Union Mansion, where the Jade August Master dwells.

It is also said: there is the Chamber of Generative Layers, where the Jade Dawn Dao Lord resides. It is also said: the Green Canopy Chamber, where the Grand Primordial Perfected One resides.

The *Inner Transmission of Han Emperor Wu* states: there is the Purple Cassia Palace, where the Most Ancient Venerable One dwells.

*Daoist Canon, Section Sixteen* concludes.
*Daoist Canon, Section Seventeen* begins.

*The Declarations of the Perfected* states: There was an elder clad in an embroidered robe, wearing a hibiscus crown and leaning upon a nine-jointed crimson staff. The hibiscus crown resembles the ceremonial *juebian* cap, though roughly so; yet it remains unknown what material the Perfected Ones use to fashion it. None but those who have attained Perfection may don this crown.

It is also said: the *Yuanyou* crown is worn by the Perfected One of Mount Tongbai. Female Perfected Ones who have attained the "Smiling" stage also wear crowns, save for the Queen Mother of the West, who wears a jade *sheng* upon her head. Female Perfected Ones who have not yet reached the reckoning stage coil their hair into three loops, or weave it into soaring clouds, letting the rest hang down to their shoulders and waists.

The *Dragon Crown*, *Golden Essence Kerchief*, *Tiger Kerchief*, *Azure Kerchief*, *Tiger-Patterned Kerchief*, and *Golden Kerchief*—these are the names of celestial Perfected Ones’ crowns and headscarves, though their designs remain undescribed.

It is further said: male Perfected Ones wear the *True Crown*, all with soaring celestial knots.

*The Traditions of Daoist Scholarship* states: Two jade maidens attending the Queen Mother ascended the hall, wearing the *Grand Perfection Dawn Tassel Crown* and black phoenix-embroidered shoes of dark jasper.

It is also said: Meng Jingyi, styled Fuming, during the Yi Jia rebellion, rushed through the night to answer the summons. While traveling, he lost his way. At that moment, a figure in yellow robes and a yellow crown appeared before him, leading the way.

Once having attained the Dao, he vanished without a trace.

*The Scripture of Sea and Void* states: Perfected Immortals and Daoist adepts all wear the *Mystic Crown* and drape themselves in kingfisher-feather capes.

*The Regulations of the Supreme Perfection* says: When doffing the common robe, one dons the *Crimson Mist Garment*; when removing the headscarf, one wears the *Far-Wandering Crown*.

It is further said: The Human Sovereign wore the *Seven-Jewel Pearl Crown*.

*The Scripture of Supreme Purity* states: The Primordial August Lord of the Uppermost Zhang wore the *Purple Radiance Crown* and girded himself with the *Nine-Colored Spontaneous Sash*.

It is also said: The Lofty Numinous One of the Nine Heavens wore the *Golden Flower Seven Luminaries Crown*.

It is further said: Wang Zhen, the Nine Heavens Zhang Person, wore the *Flying Essence Hundred-Transformations Crown* and carried the *Nine Origins Dao Perfection Talisman*.

It is also said: The Jade Lads of the Three Upper Heavens wore the *Three-Flower Treasure Radiance Grotto-Heaven Jade Crown*.

*The Regulations of the Four Clarities* states: On the day of reciting the *Scriptures of Supreme Purity* and the *True Scriptures of the Great Grotto*, one must don the ritual crown and vestments.

It is further said: When women study the methods of Supreme Purity, receive the precious scriptures and jade instructions, and cultivate the Great Grotto, they attain the rank of *Primordial Sovereign Lady*. On the day of recitation, they must wear the robes of the Primordial Sovereign, gird themselves with the sashes of the Ten Thousand Perfected, and be attended by twenty Jade Lads and twenty Jade Maidens. Those who oversee the ritual vestments must ensure that without these garments, one may not ascend to Supreme Purity.

*The Scripture of the Grotto Spirit* says: Those who receive the Dao all wear the *Mystic Crown* and straw sandals.

*The Scripture of Transmission* states: When Laozi departed Zhou, Zuo Ci in Wei both wore hemp headscarves and single-layered skirts, eschewing the common robe.

It is also said: Master Lu explained: "Facing both high and low is called the *Posture of Bowing and Uprightness*—these are the two garments of the coarse robe." He further said: "The crown embodies the Two Modes; the robe covers the Four Symbols—thus they are called ritual vestments."

*The Traditions of Daoist Scholarship* states: The Queen Mother of the West bound her hair into the *Great Flower Coiffure*, wore the *Supreme Perfection Dawn Tassel Crown*, and donned dark jasper shoes embroidered with phoenixes.

*The Scripture of Supreme Purity Transformations* says: The *Purple-Shining Jade Radiance True Jade Crown* is fastened with *Interlocking Gold Hooks*.

It is further said: The August Jade Numinous Sovereign wore the *Seven Luminaries Flower Crown* and girded himself with the *Boat-Patterned Purple Sash*.

It is also said: The August Thearch wore the *Seven-Colored Vermilion Essence Flower Crown*.

It is further said: The Supreme Simplicity Lofty Void Uppermost Purple August One wore the *Seven-Treasure Crown* and girded himself with the *Divine Essence Intertwining Serpent Sash*.

It is also said: The Void Brightness Purple Orchid Middle Origin Lofty Graceful One wore the *Three-Flower Crown* and girded herself with the *Flowing Gold Purple Insignia*.

It is further said: The Supreme Simplicity Perfected Sovereign wore the *Purple Dawn Kerchief* and rode a *Green Dragon* beneath a *Purple Feather Canopy*.

*The Scripture of Jade Pendants and Golden Earrings* states: The Primordial Heavenly King wore the *Nine-Colored Parted Silk Cape* and the *Treasure Crown*.

It is further said: The Supreme Thearch wore the *Seven Qi Vermilion Crown*.

It is also said: The Supreme Peak Lord wore the *Three-Treasure Nine-Light Night Crown*.

It is further said: The Hua Mountain Lord wore the *Six Origins Penetrating Spirit Flying Crown* and girded himself with the *Intertwining Numinous Sash*.

It is also said: The Song Heights Lord wore the *Middle Origin Yellow Dawn Jade Crown* and girded himself with the *Yellow Spirit Central August Insignia*.

It is further said: The Jade Pendant Thearch wore the *Purple Crown*.

*The Declarations of the Perfected* states: The Upper Primordial Lady wore a *Crimson Frost Robe*, draped herself in a *Blue Fur Brocade Cloak*, bound her hair into a *Three-Pointed Coiffure* with tresses flowing to her waist, wore the *Primordial Dawn Night Moon Crown*, girded herself with the *Six Mountains Fire Jade Pendants*, fastened a *Phoenix-Patterned Jasper Grand Sash* at her waist, and wielded the *Flowing Yellow Radiant Essence Sword*.

*The Scripture of Supreme Purity Transformations* says: The Supreme Primordial Perfected wore the *Lotus Crown*.

*The Supreme Purity Primordial Thread* states: The Nine Heavens Primordial Father wore the *Treasure Heaven Crown*.

*The Supreme Lord of the Five Thearchs’ Inner Perfection Scripture* says: The Green Thearch wore the *Nine Heavens Penetrating Heaven Crown*.

It is further said: The Red Thearch wore the *Three Qi Mystic Beam Treasure Crown*.

It is also said: The White Thearch wore the *Seven Qi Bright Radiance Treasure Crown*.

It is further said: The Black Thearch wore the *Five Qi Mystic Dawn Crown*.

It is also said: The Yellow Thearch wore the *Yellow Dawn Penetrating Heaven Crown*, carried the *Yellow Dawn Transcendent Origin Talisman*, and girded himself with the *Numinous Flying Purple Sash*.

*The Supreme Lord’s Scripture of Flying Feathers* states: The Nine Dawn Lords wore the *Flying Essence Jade Crown* and the *Nine-Colored Phoenix Cape*.

It is further said: The Primordial Dawn Lord wore the *Flying Heaven Jade Crown* and the *Nine Dragons Heavenly Robe*.

It is also said: The Canopy Dawn Lord wore the *Three Dawn Treasure Crown* and the *Cinnabar Brocade Flying Skirt*.

It is further said: The Upper Dawn Lord wore the *Mystic Essence Jade Crown* and the *Mystic Feather Flying Skirt*.

It is also said: The Flower Dawn Lord wore the *Flying Dawn Treasure Crown* and the *Azure Feather Flying Skirt*.

*The Supreme Lord’s Scripture of Flying Feathers* says: The Numinous Consort Primordial August Lady wore the *Dawn Tassel Treasure Crown*.

*The Scripture of Ascending Mystery* states: The immortal Ding Ziming wore a *Yellow Coarse Robe* and a *Mystic Kerchief*.

*The Jade Instructions of the Great Grotto* says: The Primordial August Purple Origin Heavenly Center Perfected wore the *Vermilion Brocade Robe* and the *Verdant Radiance Crown*.

*The Classic of the Western Mountains* states: The Jade Maiden wore the *White Crown*.

*The Scripture of the Grotto Spirit* says: The Heavenly Sovereign wore the *Nine Origins Crown*; the Earthly Sovereign wore the *Two Dawn Jade Crown* and carried the *Primordial August Register-Stabilizing Talisman*. The Human Sovereign wore the *Seven-Colored Crown* and carried the *Upper August Life-Protecting Jade Talisman*.

It is further said: The Supreme Purity Jade Perfected of the Southern Culmen and the Red Thearch wore the *Progressing Worthies Crown*.

It is also said: The Jade Perfected of the Northern Culmen and the Black Thearch wore the *Mystic Treasure Crown*; the Jade Perfected of the Western Culmen and the White Thearch wore the *Penetrating Heaven Treasure Crown*; the Jade Perfected of the Central Culmen and the Yellow Thearch wore the *Penetrating Origin Five Qi Crown*.

*The Jade Essence Perfected Instructions* states: The Nine Numinous Perfected of the East wore the *Nine Qi Crown*; the Perfected of the Southern Culmen wore the *Progressing Worthies Crown* and the *Crimson Insignia Robe*. The White Numinous Perfected of the West wore the *Three-Treasure Mystic Crown*; the Mystic Numinous Perfected of the North wore the *Mystic Crown*; the Central Total Primordial Three Numinous Perfected wore the *Yellow Dawn Jade Crown*.

*The Scripture of Jade Radiance and Eight Effulgences* says: The Eastern Origin Radiance Dao Lord wore the *Seven-Colored Shining Heaven Jade Crown* and the *Nine-Colored Shoes*.

*The Scripture of the Golden Root* states: The Nine Heavens Primordial Father wore the *Seven-Colored Vermilion Jade Accumulation* and the *Boundless Progressing Worthies Crown*.

The text further states: The Mysterious Mother of the Nine Heavens wore the *Azure Treasure Divine Radiance Brocade Frosted Gauze Nine-Colored Sash* and the *Purple Primordial Mysterious Yellow Treasure Crown*.

*The Scripture of Great Possession* says: The Mother of Jade Purity wore the *Sevenfold Divine Vermilion Jade Coiffure*, the *Boundless Progressing Worthies Crown* as her headscarf, and the *Mysterious Yellow Unadorned Numinous Sash*, residing in the *Vermilion Palace of the Great Ultimate*. It further states: The Perfected Maiden of the Nine Heavens wore the *Mysterious Yellow Seven* and the *Progressing Worthies Crown*. It also says: The Perfected Maiden of Supreme Purity wore the *Jade Crown* and the *Nine-Colored Sash*, dwelling in the *Palace of Great Seclusion*. It further states: The Empress of the Great Ultimate wore the *Boundless Progressing Worthies Crown* and the *Five-Colored Phoenix-Patterned Sash*, residing in the *Palace of Great Purity and Ultimate Mystery*. It also says: The Supreme Lord wore the *Three-Treasure Jade Crown* and the *Nine-Colored Sash*, dwelling in the *Palace of the Boundless Perfected*. It further states: The Celestial Lord of Dawn wore the *Azure Essence Progressing Dawn Jade Crown*.

*The Scripture of the Great One’s Mysterious Perfection* says: The Three Simplicities Venerable Lords wore brocade robes and the *Dragon-Tiger Crown*. It further states: The Great One, the Noble Son, White Prime, Director of Destinies, and Peach Lord—these five all wore vermilion robes and crimson headscarves, overseeing talismans and registers in the *Purple Chamber Palace of the Grand Tenuity*.

*The Hidden Instructions for Ascending Perfection* says: The Jade Maiden of the Supreme Vermilion Clouds of Great Mystery wore the *Purple Headscarf*, as well as the *Purple Floral Hibiscus Headscarf*, the *Gold Essence Headscarf*, the *Flying Headscarf*, the *Tiger-Patterned Headscarf*, and the *Gold Headscarf*.

*The Primordial Register of Mount Tortoise* says: The Supreme Elder of the Primordial Beginning wore the *Nine Qi Purple Radiance Crown* and the *Nine-Light Brocade Robe*, girded with the *Nine-Colored Seamless Natural Sash* and the *Six-Mountain Fire Jade Belt*, residing above Supreme Purity. He also bore the *Nine Heavens Immortal-Refining Sword*, wore the *Nine-Colored Mottled Robe*, and constantly rode twelve flying unicorns, girded with the *Gold Tiger Phoenix-Patterned Sash*.

*The Scripture of Golden Perfection and Jade Radiance* says: The Dao Lord of Primordial Radiance trailed the *Mysterious Yellow Sash* and wore the *Seven-Colored Jade Crown*. It further states: The Dao Lord of Primordial Radiance wore the *Cinnabar Brocade Sash* and the *Progressing Worthies Jade Crown*, riding the *Mysterious Radiance Chariot* drawn by phoenixes. In the *Purple Tenuity Palace of the Supreme Yang Upper Prefecture*, the Dao Lord trailed the *Crimson Brocade Vermilion Sash*, wore the *Jade Crown* and the *Nine-Colored Shoes*, and held the *Demon-Quelling Seal*. The Supreme Unity Lord of Primordial Radiance trailed the *Mysterious Yellow Unadorned Sash*, wore the *Seven-Treasure Crown*, held the *Life-Spirit Tally*, rode the *Jade Chariot* with a *Five-Colored Canopy*, the *Purple Cloud Carriage*, and was drawn by six dragons.

*The Scripture of the Most High and Unadorned Numinous* says: The Perfected Man Wang Ziqiao of Mount Tongbai was very young and exceptionally refined, wearing the *Hibiscus Crown* and a vermilion robe, with white pearls adorning the seams, girded with a sword. He often discoursed on matters of the Golden Court Mountain to the assembled Perfected.

*The Scripture of the Supreme Unadorned Numinous* says: The Supreme Divine Immortals wore the *Flying Dawn Treasure Crown*, the *Azure Essence Morning Jade Crown*, the *Cloud-Traversing Treasure Crown*, the *Jade Essence Treasure Crown*, the *Heaven-Connecting Jade Treasure Crown*, and the *Three Mysteries Treasure Crown*. The Perfected Lords of Supreme Purity all wore the *Great Crown of Supporting Floral Dark Radiance*, while the Dao Lords wore the *Nine Virtues Crown*.

The *Daily Observances of the Left Perfected Lord of the Great Ultimate* notes: The Supreme Three Heavens bestowed upon the Perfected Lord the *Hibiscus Dawn Crown*.

*The Scripture of the Six Jia of Numinous Flight* says: The Jade Perfected of the Eastern Culmen in the Jade Palace of Supreme Purity wore the *Nine Qi Communicating Essence Crown*; the Perfected of the Jade Capital wore the *Communicating Yang Jade Dawn Crown*; the Lesser Yang Perfected wore the *Communicating Radiance Crown*; the Three Primordials of Great Simplicity wore the *Precious Jade-Floriate Dawn Feather Crown*; the Primordial Lady of Purple Simplicity wore the *Great Perfected Dawn Tassel Crown*, with three coiled buns and hair flowing loose to the waist.

*The Golden Book of the Great Ultimate* says: The Primordial Beginning wore the *Cave Heaven Crown*; the Supreme Lord wore the *Azure Essence Heavenly Jade Crown*; the Venerable Perfected wore the *Three-Treasure Jade Crown*; the Three Heavenly Lads wore the *Three-Floral Treasure Radiance Cave Heaven Jade Crown*.

*The Jade Scripture of the Great Cavern* states: The Perfected Man of Purple Prime wore the *Vermilion Brocade Robe* and the *Green Radiance Crown*.

*The True Forms of the Five Marchmounts* says: The Great Marchmount of the Eastern Peak, Mount Tai, wore the *Sevenfold Azure Jasper Crown*; the Southern Marchmount, Mount Heng, wore the *Nine Cinnabar Solar Essence Crown*; the Central Marchmount, Mount Song, wore the *Yellow Jade Supreme Mystery Crown*; the Western Marchmount, Mount Hua, wore the *Great Beginning Nine Streams Crown*; the Northern Marchmount, Mount Heng, wore the *Great Obscurity Numinous Yin Crown*; the Venerable Man of Mount Qingcheng wore the *Heaven-Covering Crown*.

*The Scripture of Ascending Mystery* says: In ancient times, the immortal Dou Ziming wore the *Yellow-Brown Mysterious Headscarf*.

The *Purple Book of the Golden Root* says: The Primordial Father of the Nine Heavens wore the *Sevenfold Pearl-Jade Headband*.

*The Scripture of Ritual Arrangement* says: The Orthodox Unity Attendant wore the *Vermilion Yang Headband*.

The *Golden Book of the Great Ultimate* says: The Celestial Emperor of the Primordial Beginning wore the *Nine-Colored Gauze Robe with Cinnabar and Crimson Hem*, and the *Pearl-Embroidered Radiance Robe*.

The *Daily Observances of the Left Perfected Lord of the Great Ultimate* notes: The Supreme Three Heavens bestowed upon the Perfected Lord the *Cinnabar Brocade Robe*.

*The Scripture of the Purple Text of the Numinous Writ* says: The Great Lord of the Azure Lad wore the *Flying Azure Kingfisher Feather Robe*.

*The Scripture of the Feminine One and the Five Venerables* says: The Three Primordials of Great Simplicity wore the *Purple Qi Floating Cloud Brocade Robe*, the *Purple Embroidered Feather Robe*, and the *Phoenix-Patterned Brocade Robe*.

*The Inner Transmission of the Supreme Perfected* says: The *Nine-Colored Brocade Robe with Floral Patterns*.

*The Inner Transmission of Lord Mao, the Perfected of Great Simplicity* says: The *Embroidered Feather Purple Robe*.

*The Central Scripture of the Nine Perfected* states: *Azure Jade*, *Brocade Robe*, *Crimson Jade*, *Unadorned Jade*, *Mysterious Jade*, *Yellow Jade*, and *Brocade Robe*. It further states: *Azure Floral Cinnabar Pistil Jade White Fluorite*, the *Four-Emerging Dragon Robe*, the *Mysterious Jade Nine Paths*, the *Cloud Brocade Yellow Robe*, and the *Cloud Mountain Patterned Brocade Robe*.

The *Scripture of the Perfected Lord’s Inquiry* says: The Perfected of the Great Ultimate said: Those who study the Dao must wear clean and cool clothing, prepare proper headscarves and brown robes, which are called the *Dharma Robes of the Way*.

*The Oral Instructions of the Numinous Treasure’s Spontaneous Unity* says: Those who have attained the Way wear the *Seven-Colored Dharma Robe of Nine Lights*.

*The Scripture of the Six Jia of Numinous Flight* states: The Jade Perfected of the Southern Culmen wears a crimson gauze Dharma robe.

*The Purple Palace Scripture of the Highest Clarity* says: Those who cultivate the Way of the Seven Transformations are granted by the August Lord of the Supreme the *Dharma Robe of Flying Immortals with Feathered Chapters*, and are further crowned with the *Purple Origin Flying Frost Crown of Seven Colors*.

**Sashes**
*The Scripture of the Highest Clarity* says: The Most High Jade Emperor wears a robe adorned with *jade-script radiant light*, and a sash of *flying bud jade*.

*The Yuan Record of Mount Tortoise* says: The Mysterious Mother of the Nine Heavens wears a *frost-gauze sash of nine colors*, and also a *blue-gauze sash*.

*The True Forms of the Five Marchmounts* says: The envoys of the Five Marchmounts wear *crimson sashes*.

*The Scripture of the Three Primes* says: The Purple Prime Lady wears a *purple brocade sash with embroidered edges*. The Solar Prime Lady wears a *white brocade sash of radiant light*.

*The Yuan Register of Mount Tortoise* says: the *nine-colored flying cloud brocade sash*; the *nine-colored sash of spontaneous unfolding*; the *jade-script radiant light flying brocade sash*; the *nine-colored pearl-crimson cloud-light brocade sash*; the *cinnabar brocade sash of seven-colored patterned light*.

**Robes**
*The Golden Book of the Great Ultimate* says: The Primordial Beginning wears a *frost-pearl robe*.

*The Scripture of the Highest Clarity* says: The Jade Lads of the Three Heavens wear *blue-yellow brocade robes*.

*The True Forms of the Five Marchmounts* says: The Lord of the Eastern Marchmount wears a *vermilion radiance robe*.

*The Yuan Register of Mount Tortoise* says: the *radiant light flying brocade pearl robe*, the *five-colored cloud-gauze robe*, the *seven-colored phoenix-cloud robe*, the *nine-colored mottled feather robe*.

*The Inner Transmission of Lord Mao* says: the *crimson frost robe*.

**Fur Garments**
*The Jade Scripture of the Great Cavern* says: The True Earl of Prohibitions rides the *cakes of sun and moon* and wears a *tiger-patterned fur*.

*The Scripture of the Eight Limits* says: The White Prime Lady wears a *yellow-green luminous cloud-patterned fur*.

*The Scripture of the Inner Perfected of the Five Thearchs* says: the *mysterious-script radiant light fur* and the *nine-colored mottled fur*.

*The Yuan Register of Mount Tortoise* says: the *cloud-patterned cinnabar brocade fur*.

**Garments**
*The Scripture of the Three Ways in Harmonious Progression* says: The Jade Scenery Perfected wears a *mysterious bud jade brocade garment*.

*The Central Scripture of Laozi’s Successive Treasuries* says: The Eastern Father, the *qi* of pure yang and forerunner of the ten thousand spirits, wears a *five-colored garment*.

*The Yuan Register of Mount Tortoise* says: the *radiant light brocade nine-vermilion flying-script Dharma garment*, the *three-prime flying-script brocade garment*, the *five-colored mottled garment*, the *nine-colored dragon garment*. Also the *blue-yellow-purple three-colored feather garment*, the *nine-colored phoenix garment*, and the *Nine Heavens phoenix garment*.

**Pendants**
*The Scripture of the Great Precepts* says: The Perfected of the Great Ultimate said: Those who reverently attend to Dharma robes must wear *crowns, tiaras, and jade pendants*.

*The Scripture of the Three Primes* says: the *jade pendants of the Six Great Marchmounts*.

**Sashes (for Seals)**
*The Scripture of the Eight Primes* says: The Prime Lady of Great Simplicity wears a *flowing-light cloud-patterned sash*; the Prime Lady of Original Simplicity wears a *purple-light cloud-patterned plain sash*; the Prime Lady of Mysterious Simplicity wears a *flying-cloud nine-transformation sash*; the Purple Prime Lady wears a *mysterious-yellow nine-colored plain gauze sash*; the Nine Yellow Prime Lords wear a *flying-cloud plain brocade sash*.

*The Scripture of the Three Primes* says: The Purple Prime Lady wears the *interlaced Great Sash of Numinous Flight*; the White Prime Lady wears the *patterned jade-blossom sash*.

*The Scripture of the Flying Feathered Wings* says: the *nine-bell sash*, the *flying numinous purple sash*, the *flying dawn sash of the Six Marchmounts*, the *nine-light sash*.

*The Scripture of Golden Perfection and Jade Radiance* says: the *purple-blue sash*, the *cinnabar brocade sash*, the *crimson-cinnabar sash*, the *mysterious-yellow plain sash*, the *white-script plain numinous sash*, the *mysterious-numinous five-colored sash*.

*The Scripture of the Primordial Beginning* says: The Mysterious Mother of the Nine Heavens wears a *flowing-tassel purple sash*. It further says: the *nine-origin light-extending purple sash*, the *numinous flight purple sash*, the *interlaced numinous plain sash*, the *nine-colored sash of spontaneity*, the *golden-tiger phoenix-script sash*. It further says: The Most High wears the *nine-qi life-numinous insignia* and the *kingfisher-feather script numinous sash*.

**Tablets**
*The Scripture of Ascending to the Mysterious* says: The Most High said: The Realized Officials of the Five Thearchs, the messengers bearing talismans, and the heralds announcing audiences in the ten directions all wear *crowns with hanging tassels*, hold *jade tablets* in unison, and array their *processional regalia* before, behind, and beside me.

**Handled Tablets**
*The Scripture of Ascending to the Mysterious* says: The Most High instructed the Inspector of Lingyang, who bowed and rose, holding his *handled tablet* to his chest and standing facing west.

**Skirt-Panels**
*The Scripture of the Flying Feathered Wings* says: The Highest Lord wears a *phoenix garment with mottled tiger skirt-panel*.

*The Scripture of the Plain and Numinous* says: The Most High and the divine immortals wear *blue brocade single skirts*, *blue damask skirts*, *cloud brocade crimson-chapter cinnabar skirts*, *crimson garments with flying hems*, and *yellow cloud brocade skirts*.

*The Scripture of the Three Primes* says: The Three Prime Ladies of Great Simplicity wear *nine-colored dragon brocade feather skirts*; the Purple Prime Lady wears a *flying frost gauze skirt*.

*The Daily Record of the Left Immortal Duke of the Great Ultimate* notes: The Most High of the Three Heavens bestowed upon the Immortal Duke a *knot-tied gauze skirt*.

*The Yuan Register of Mount Tortoise* says: the *cinnabar brocade flying skirt* and the *nine-colored dragon brocade feather skirt*.

*The Scripture of the Flying Feathered Wings* says: the *seven-colored night-luminous cloud brocade skirt*.

*The Central Scripture of the Nine Perfected* says: the *azure-flower flying feather skirt*, the *cinnabar-flower flying feather skirt*, the *white feather flying flower skirt*, and also the *black feather yellow feather flying flower skirt*. It further says: the *kingfisher dragon-flower flying feather hem*, the *vermilion-flower phoenix-broom*, the *plain feather inscribed-chapter skirt*, the *black feather dragon-script skirt*, the *green feather phoenix-flower embroidered skirt*.

**Bells**
*The Scripture of Transference* says: The True August Lord of the Southern Realm wears *numinous frost phoenix-flower pendants*, a *dragon bell tiger-script sash*, the *mystery-dawn crown*, a *flying blue brocade robe*, and rides a *cinnabar cloud vermilion chariot*.

*The Yuan Register of Mount Tortoise* says: the *jade bell* and the *morning-light bright-moon bell*.

*The Biographies of the Immortals* says: The Lady of Numinous Radiance, daughter of Li Qingbin, the Middle Mystery Lord of the Northern Prime, wears a *purple brocade robe with a divine tiger talisman*, holds a *flowing gold bell*, and is attended by two maidservants, each about twenty years of age, while the Lady herself appears to be thirteen or fourteen.

Hearing the call, one maidservant was named Hidden Radiance. The maidservants all wore azure damask robes and bore two crimson jade caskets, bound with azure cords and sealed with white jade tablets, one inscribed *Supreme Petition*, the other *Supreme Script*. The Lady of the Writ, Supreme Script, wore an azure jade-colored sash in the manner of an official’s petition pouch, the hidden writ measuring some five *zhang* in length and three to four *chi* in width.

It is further said: Within the Supreme Ultimate dwell four Perfected Ones. The Central Yellow Lord stands to its left, bearing the talisman of the divine tiger, girded with flowing gold bells, grasping the purple-fleeced tally, and crowned with a golden essence kerchief.

It is also said: Among the Dao of immortals are purple embroidered feathered cloaks, cinnabar-and-indigo flying skirts, kingfisher-feather patterned robes, gold bells with azure sashes, and curved-dawn flying canopies—when mounted, they soar of their own accord.

**Staffs**
*The Yuan Register of Mount Tortoise* says: In the three months of winter, the Jade Lads of the Three Heavens transform into an old man, holding a nine-jointed golden staff that illumines the Jade Clarity with radiant splendor.

*The Scripture of the Sacred Record* says: An old man grasped a green bamboo staff and discoursed with Lord Lao on the reckonings of heaven and earth.

*The Upper Scripture of the Red Writ and Jade Formulas* says: One should take bamboo from the sunlit side of the numinous mountain, measuring one *zhang* and seven joints in length, to fashion a divine staff, ensuring it is perfectly straight from top to bottom. Sweet bamboo is best. Imprint it with the seal of the Primordial Beginning; in motion and stillness, rising and sitting, keep it ever at hand. The staff is attended by the true talismanic officials of the Five Thearchs, who assist the Perfected of the Highest Clarity.

*The Traditions of Lord Mao* says: The Vermilion Palace Messenger bore a green-tasseled staff with a jade shaft and feathered streamers.

It is further said: The Perfected of the Supreme Simplicity grasped the Eight Radiance Flying Staff and the Nine-Colored Tally, ascending and descending the Highest Clarity.

The Jade Lads of the Three Heavens wore three-cornered yellow kerchiefs bound at the brow and held nine-jointed golden staffs.

**Tallies**
*The Biographies of the Immortals* says: The Perfected of the Supreme Prime leaned upon a purple-fleeced tally as the Lady of the Purple Tenuity and a divine maiden descended together. The divine maiden wore a cloud-brocade sash, crimson above and azure below, their patterns interluminous. At her waist hung a green embroidered belt, from which were suspended over ten small bells, alternating in azure and yellow. To her left hung a jade pendant, resembling the pendants of the mortal world but slightly smaller. Her robes shimmered with sudden light, casting a radiance within the chamber like sunlight through mica.

The hair and temples were arranged with unparalleled refinement. A topknot sat at the crown, while the remaining tresses cascaded to the waist. Gold rings adorned the fingers, and white pearls encircled the arms, making her appear no older than thirteen or fourteen. Flanking her were two attendant maidens: one wore crimson robes and bore a green talismanic pouch, her hands also holding a brocade satchel over a foot in length, containing more than ten scrolls. The white jade clasp atop the satchel bore the inscription *Jade Clarity Divine Tiger, Inner Perfected Purple Prime Cinnabar Script*. The other maiden, clad in azure, carried a white casket bound with crimson cords, its form resembling an ivory box. Both attendants, around seventeen or eighteen, were adorned with extraordinary elegance.

It is further said: The attendants of Perfected Pei bore a tally of azure fur, one youth carrying an embroidered pouch; the attendants of Lord Zhou bore a tally of yellow fur, without pouches. Each of the two lords had six youths in attendance.

It is also said: The Eastern Minister of State descended with seven attendants—one bearing a purple-furred tally, another holding a *hua-shen* (also called the *Tenfold Wondrous Scepter*), one wearing a green talismanic pouch, three carrying ivory caskets, and one grasping a flowing-gold bell. All attendants wore crimson robes. The Eastern Minister appeared far younger than his two brothers, who were dressed in azure brocade skirts, purple-furred kerchiefs, and *lotus-petal crowns*. The two brothers stood side by side until the Eastern Minister bade them sit, and they conversed at length.

This occurred in the *yichou* year, the third year of the Xingning reign of the Jin dynasty, on the fourth day of the seventh month, descending at the home of Master Yang.

**Footwear**
It is further said: To bestow upon the immortals.

The earlier Dao possessed thirty-seven varieties of colored tallies.

The *Central Scripture of the Nine Perfected* states: "For all who study the Dao, let none violate the taboo of sandals. In walking the Dao, prohibitions abound."

The *Scripture of Golden Perfection and Jade Radiance* speaks of five-colored and nine-colored lion sandals.

The *Eight Radiant Luminaires of Jade Light* records: "In the Eastern North’s Palace of Primordial Yang, Niu Yuanjing’s feet tread upon five-colored sandals."

**Shoes**
The *Original Register of Mount Turtle* states: "The Sovereign of the Immortals’ Realm, bearing the mandate of the Primordial Beginning, is bestowed with a jade crown of morning-twilight tassels and phoenix-cloud shoes, granted to the Supreme Perfected and Celestial Mothers." There are also *divine-thunder phoenix shoes*.

The *Biographies of the Immortals* recounts: "Master Anqi sold medicines by the sea, known to his time as the Millennial Elder. The First Emperor of Qin summoned him and spoke with him for three days. That evening, he was gifted gold and jade worth thousands of millions, left at the Pavilion of Restful Village. There, he placed a letter of departure and left behind a pair of crimson jade shoes, one of which he used to measure the other, saying: 'Seek me beneath Mount Penglai a thousand years hence.' The First Emperor dispatched envoys into the sea, but before they reached Penglai, winds and waves drove them back."

The *Original Register of the Supreme Perfected* states: "The Primordial Father of the Nine Heavens trails cloud-phoenix shoes of divine mist, girded with a sash of plain clouds."

**Curtains and Canopies**
The *Divine Continent Scripture* says: "The Emperor Lord of the Nine Rivers sits within a jade grove, surrounded by five-colored curtains and canopies, their inner and outer light resplendent, with a thousand strands of jade pendants."

**Seats**
The *Scripture of Jade Pendants and Golden Earrings* records: "The immortal Zheng Duan sits upon a seat of jade blossoms."

Section Seventeen of the Daoist Canon concludes.
Section Eighteen of the Daoist Canon begins.

**Bamboo Slips and Jade Tablets**

The *Seven Sages’ Mysterious Record of the Jade Emperor* states: "The Seven Sages determine the bamboo slips; the Five Emperors record the names."

The *Concealed Instructions for Ascending to Perfection* says: "The Heavenly King of Lesser Existence, the Perfected of Great Simplicity and Pure Emptiness, ascends White Void Mountain to visit the Three Primordial Ladies of Purple Emptiness. There, he receives the Flowing Gold Fire Bell, the Seven Primordials of the Vast Expanse, the Eight Radiant Flying Dawn Talismans, and the Jade Seal." It further states: "The Great One possesses a jade seal, golden elixir, and tiger tally."

The *Hidden Writ of Jade Clarity* records: "There exists the *Flying Nine Dawns Jade Scripture* with inner texts inscribed on golden bamboo slips." It also says: "Within are the jade seal, phoenix case, golden perfection, jade radiance, purple script, and single-section tablets."

The *Scripture of the Nine Dark Realms* declares: "The Emperor Lord resides in the Three Primordial Palace, overseeing the collation of charts and registers." It further states: "Meritorious deeds are inscribed in the Yellow Register; golden frames and jade tablets are arrayed before the Three Clarities and Four Poles."

The *Scripture of Luminous Regulations* says: "If one possesses the Purple Tablets of the Emperor’s Chart with green characters, it may be transmitted after a thousand years." It also states: "The Five Elders’ Treasured Scripture is written in azure and green characters to compose its sections." And: "The *Eight Simplicities Perfected Scripture* is the hidden writ of the Supreme. The Lord Emperor of the Golden Watchtower inscribed it with eight-hued brushes as the method of attaining perfection, bestowing it upon the Perfected of Great Emptiness. The Red Pine Master of the Southern Marchmount was sent to transmit it below to those studying the Dao. Those with prior destiny bear golden and jade characters carved in the Golden Pavilion. Those who are to become Perfected must not transmit it beyond Earthbound Immortals." It further records: "The *Five Talismans Scripture*—a single passage of unobstructed writ—is sealed in a cinnabar-silk pouch with a case of golden blossoms, stamped with the seal of the Dark Capital, and entrusted to the Lord of the Shocking Waters Grotto-Chamber." And: "The *Scripture of the Perfected and Spontaneously Real*—when the host of Perfected wear this scripture, it is inscribed in cinnabar upon yellow brocade, and the Dao’s true essence is eternally enjoyed without end."

The words spoken by the Primordial Beginning in the midst of expounding the scriptures are all the hidden sounds of the inner names of the Heavenly Thearchs, not the common speech of the world. It further states: "The *Five Treasures Scripture of the Feminine One* is secretly kept above the Nine Heavens, within the Jade Chamber of the Great Existence Palace and the Terrace of the Great Mystery Numinous Treasure. Its texts are composed on purple-gold silk, with azure and green characters forming its sections." And: "There is a wondrous scripture carved on jade slips, transmitted to the Heavenly Emperor Lord."

The *Eight Simplicities Perfected Scripture of the Supreme* says: "The Registrar of Destinies records in the register: jade tablets with cinnabar script, bound with golden threads and wrapped in azure silk, enduring for ten billion myriad years without doubt." It further states: "On an auspicious day of the Supreme, the sections of the Three Primordials are stamped with the seal of the Great Mystery, the seal of the August Sovereign, and the seal of the Central Yellow." And: "In the Western Florescence Palace, there are jade slips with blossoming script."

It also says: "The Supreme inscribes with cinnabar upon white jade slips, also using azure, dark jade, and yellow gold for the writ." The *Eight Simplicities Scripture* states: "The mysterious text of the *Eight Simplicities Perfected Scripture* arises within the Great Emptiness, appearing on the Western Tortoise Mountain, above the Dark Garden, and beneath the Shaded Accumulated Stones. The High Mystery Feathered Chapters are celebrated by the host of Perfected in the Upper Clarity."

The *Scripture of the Upper Clarity* says: "The Jade Lads of the Three Heavens wear the vermilion essence-seal of the Heavenly Prohibition. The High Jade Sovereign bears the cinnabar sovereign jade seal." It further states: "The purple radiance of the Nine Empyreans holds the true jade seal of the Golden Phoenix." And: "The Three Primordial Ladies of Great Simplicity possess cloud-jade tablets with nine-transforming tiger script." And: "The Nine Sovereigns of High Numinosity wear the purple sash of primordial radiance and the flowing essence flying-jade seal." And: "The Jade Lads of the Three Heavens wear the seal of the Nine Heavens." And: "The Supreme Sovereign Lord of Emptiness bears the cinnabar sovereign jade seal." And: "The Jade Perfected Venerable of the Nine Heavens wears the nine-primordial penetrating-perfection jade tally." And: "The Purple Numinous August Upper Primordial Sovereign bears the jade tally for summoning the sealed numina, wearing the flowing radiance phoenix seal." And: "The Jade Void Lord of the August Supreme bears the cinnabar-script purple sash." And: "The Three Primordial Great Luminous August Supreme Sovereign wears the divine tiger purple seal." And: "The August Supreme Lord of Myriad Beginnings bears the golden tiger phoenix script, wearing the cinnabar sovereign purple seal." And: "The August Emperor Lord wears the divine tiger jade seal." And: "The Supreme Purple August Lord of the Highest wears the six-mountain jade belt with the intertwining divine essence serpent seal-sash."

The *Luminous Writ of the Great Empyrean* says: "The Heavenly Emperor Lord of the Grand Tenuity binds the *Purple Measure Scripture* with purple slips for its chapter headings." It further states: "There is the seal of the Emperor’s sections." And: "The jade-text Emperor’s sections should be carved on jujube-wood and received within the abyss of sheer cliffs." And: "The *Luminous Writ of the Great Empyrean* is the flying-empyrean canon of the Nine Heavens; the jade-text Emperor’s sections are its supreme writ. Both arise from the Primordial Beginning within the spontaneous emptiness, received by the Numinous Sovereign Jade Emperor from the Nine Mysteries. Cast in gold as slips and carved in jade to form chapters, with golden threads and jade characters, they illuminate the treasured texts secretly kept above the Nine Heavens."

The *Scripture of the Cavernous Spirit* states: "There are the Three Capitals Seal, the Three Sovereigns Seal, and the Nine Heavens Seal, vast beneath the heavens." It further says: "There are the Three Sovereigns’ Jade Contracts, also called golden tallies." And: "To receive the Three Sovereigns’ method, one must use jade slips, one foot and two inches long, one inch wide, and three-tenths of an inch thick. If unavailable, hibiscus or paulownia wood may serve as substitutes." And: "The slips for petitioning the Three Sovereigns are made of azure jade with characters in red gold."

The *Scripture of the Golden Root* says: "Golden slips and jade tablets emerge from the Palace of the Supreme Numinous Capital, inscribed in vermilion script and bound with vermilion cords." It further states: "There is the place where the Perfected of the Divine Flower Jade Gate present golden slips." And: "The Jade Gentlemen Who Lead Immortals carry golden slips and purple registers to the Eastern Florescence Azure Palace to verify jade names." And: "The Jade Emperor carves and bestows cinnabar essence, jade mushrooms, golden seals, and phoenix seals." Within the Azure Palace’s Jade Treasury, there are golden seals and phoenix tallies. And: "In the northern hall of the Azure Palace, there are golden seals and phoenix tallies, which the Perfected obtain." And: "Within the northern hall of the Azure Palace, there is a golden frame for immortal records, upon which are the ledgers of those studying immortality, their mysterious names, and the depth of their years and months."

The golden slips and jade tablets number one hundred thousand scrolls, forming the canon of the Jade Gentlemen Who Lead Immortals. It further states: "Without the registers of golden slips in the Azure Palace, the jade ledgers lack the names of the mysterious compilations, and the divine scriptures cannot be perused." The *Great Cavern Jade Scripture* says: "Those who recite the *Mysterious Unity Cavern Scripture* have their names inscribed on the slips of Fortune’s Link in the Terrace of Spirits." The golden slips and jade tablets of the Most High are called the *Book of Fortune’s Link*. It further states: "True Yang is the name of a palace in the Upper Clarity, where the slips of Fortune’s Link are inscribed within."

The *Scripture of the Five Talismans* says: "True Unity consumes the celestial patterns of the Five Sprouts." And: "In the Western Florescence Palace, there are jade slips and flower-script." And: "The Most High uses white jade for slips and cinnabar-jade writing, also employing azure-green mysterious jade and yellow gold for them."

The *Scripture of the Eight Simplicities* says: "The mysterious text of the *Eight Simplicities True Scripture* arises within the Great Void, appearing on the Western Tortoise Mountain, above the Mysterious Orchard, and beneath the Shade of Accumulated Stones. The lofty and mysterious feathered chapters are celebrated by the assembled perfected in the Upper Clarity." The *Upper Clarity Scripture* says: "The Jade Lads of the Three Heavens bear the vermilion-essence-sealed celestial chapters. The Lofty Jade Emperor wears the cinnabar-jade imperial seal." And: "The purple radiance of the Nine Empyreans is matched with true jade pendants and golden phoenix seals." And: "The Three Primordials of the Great Simplicity have cloud-jade tablets and nine-transformation tiger-script." And: "The Nine Sovereigns of the Lofty Numinous wear the purple sashes of primordial radiance and the flying-jade chapters of flowing essence." And: "The Jade Lads of the Three Heavens bear the chapters of the Nine Heavens." And: "The Lofty Void Emperor wears the cinnabar-jade imperial seal." And: "The Nine Heavens Venerable of Jade Truth bears the nine-primordials-pervading-true jade tally." And: "The Purple Numinous August Supreme Primordial wears the jade tally of sealed-numinous-summoning-true and the phoenix chapters of flowing radiance." And: "The Supreme Jade Void Lord wears the cinnabar-script purple sash." And: "The Three Primordials Great Brilliance Supreme August Lord bears the purple chapters of the divine tiger." And: "The August Supreme Lord of Myriad Beginnings wears the phoenix-script of the golden tiger and the purple chapters of the cinnabar emperor." And: "The August Thearch wears the jade chapters of the divine tiger." And: "The Supreme Lofty Purple August Lord wears the jade belt of the Six Mountains and the intertwined-serpent chapters and sash of divine essence."

The *Azure Jade Scripture of the Grand Empyrean* says: "The Celestial Thearch of the Grand Tenuity binds the purple slips to compile the *Purple-Measure Scripture*." And: "There is the seal of the imperial chapters." And: "The jade-script imperial chapters should be carved on jujube-wood and received within the secluded cliffs." And: "The *Azure Jade Scripture of the Grand Empyrean* is the canon of the flying empyrean of the Nine Heavens, while the imperial chapters of jade-script are the supreme texts. Both originate from the spontaneous emptiness of the Primordial Beginning, received by the Numinous August Jade Emperor from the Nine Mysteries. Gold is cast into slips, jade is carved into bound scrolls, with golden threads and jade characters to illuminate the treasured scriptures hidden above the Nine Heavens."

The *Cavern Spirit Scripture* says: "There are the Three Capitals Seal, the Three Augusts Seal, and the Nine Heavens Seal, which govern the world below." And: "There are the Three Augusts’ jade vouchers, also called golden contracts." And: "To receive the methods of the Three Augusts, one must use jade slips, one foot and two inches in length, one inch in width, and three *fen* in thickness. If unavailable, *hibiscus* or paulownia wood may serve as substitutes." And: "The slips for petitioning the Three Augusts are made of azure jade with characters in red gold."

The *Golden Root Scripture* says: "The golden slips and jade tablets emerge from the Palace of the Numinous Capital of the Most High, written in vermilion script and bound with vermilion cords." And: "There is the place where the Perfected of the Divine Flower Jade Gate present golden slips." And: "The Jade Gentlemen Who Lead Immortals carry golden slips and purple registers to the Eastern Florescence Azure Palace to verify jade names." And: "The Jade Emperor carves and bestows cinnabar essence, jade mushrooms, golden seals, and phoenix seals." Within the Azure Palace’s Jade Treasury, there are golden seals and phoenix tallies. And: "In the northern hall of the Azure Palace, there are golden seals and phoenix tallies, which the Perfected obtain." And: "Within the northern hall of the Azure Palace, there is a golden frame for immortal records, upon which are the ledgers of those studying immortality, their mysterious names, and the depth of their years and months."

The golden slips and jade tablets number one hundred thousand scrolls, forming the canon of the Jade Gentlemen Who Lead Immortals. It further states: "Without the registers of golden slips in the Azure Palace, the jade ledgers lack the names of the mysterious compilations, and the divine scriptures cannot be perused." The *Great Cavern Jade Scripture* says: "Those who recite the *Mysterious Unity Cavern Scripture* have their names inscribed on the slips of Fortune’s Link in the Terrace of Spirits." The golden slips and jade tablets of the Most High are called the *Book of Fortune’s Link*. It further states: "True Yang is the name of a palace in the Upper Clarity, where the slips of Fortune’s Link are inscribed within."

The *Scripture of the Five Talismans* says: "True Unity consumes the celestial patterns of the Five Sprouts. The Queen Mother of the West carves them on yellow-gold tablets, seals them with cinnabar mushrooms and luminous herbs, and stamps them with the central seal of the Most High." The *Inner Transmission of Lord Mao* says: "When Mao Ying was within Mount Heng, he dreamed of the Jade Maiden of the Great Mystery holding jade tablets and leading him." And: "The Dao Lord of Heaven possesses a jade chariot and phoenix seals." And: "The True Person of the Great Primordial has one attendant bearing a register-chapter satchel, another bearing an embroidered-chapter satchel, and another bearing a brocade satchel of scriptures."

The *Scripture of Golden Truth and Jade Radiance* says: "There are the chapters of luminous revelation and the jade seals of life-preservation." And: "This scripture is lofty and wondrous, the most venerable of all scriptures. It governs the myriad perfected and rectifies the host of immortals. Its mysterious talismans flow and reflect, illuminating the purple dawn. Hidden within the palaces of the Nine Heavens, gold is cast into slips to compile the numinous texts, and jade is carved with cinnabar writing to clarify its scrolls." The *Scripture of the Numinous Treasure’s Spontaneity* says: "The Most High and the various perfected immortals use yellow gold for slips and write upon them with cinnabar jade." The *Canons of the Great Perfected* use jade tablets and golden script, with the Seven Treasures serving as slips for the Jade Emperor.

The *Mysterious Record of the Seven Sages* says: "They are carved on white-silver slips and bound with flying azure script." And: "Within the Hall of Vast Numinosity, the Nine Empyreans of the Turning Heavens are inscribed on white slips with azure threads." The *Canons of the Great Perfected* say: "The cinnabar slips are vermilion-lacquered slips that establish the yang with luminous fire."

The *Ink Registers* are texts written in ink to clarify that water governs the yin, and those who study longevity are thus named *Cinnabar Slips* and *Ink Registers*—these are secret and not recklessly transmitted.

It is also said: The Heavenly Sovereign holds the *Jade Writs of Flying Immortals*; the Human Sovereign holds the *Jade Writs of the Supreme Sovereign for Life Preservation*; the Earthly Sovereign holds the *Writs of the Primordial Sovereign for Registering Destinies*.

The *Inner Scripture of the Three Flowers’ Treasure Radiance* states: Within the Hall of the Numinous Capital of the Supreme Emperor, there are 240,000 perfected immortals of the highest rank, all of whom cast gold into slips, bound with white silver, and inscribed with purple-flower script, reciting and chanting these chapters.

The *Orthodox Dharma of the Three Heavens* says: The *Great Numinous Register of the Nine Subtleties of the Three Heavens* is secreted within the Palace of the Numinous Capital of the Most High, carved on slips of purple jade with golden script, and entrusted to the Five Elders and the Left Duke of the Perfected Immortals of the Capital of the Immortals. It is sealed in a purple-stamen jade box and encased in a cloud-brocade bag.

The *Inner Biography of the Lady of the Southern Marchmount* states: White slips with plain threads, using white jade for slips and azure jade for characters, are thus called *White Slips and Azure Registers*, all recording the names of those who attain the Dao.

The *Traditions of Daoist Learning* says: The golden slips bear the calligraphy of Wang Yuan’gui.

The *Supreme Plain Scripture* states: For all who receive the *Yellow Plain Scripture of the Most High*, the transmission covenant employs one jade tablet, one foot and five parts in length, one inch and four parts in width.

It also says: There are the *Elegant Slips of the Three Primes*.

The *Authentic Declarations* says: The Perfected Person of Pure Emptiness visited the Lords of the Three Primes to receive the *Jade Seal and Golden Perfection*.

The *Primordial Register of Mount Tortoise* states: Cinnabar script and purple stanzas, divine tiger jade seals, the stanzas of the Seven Primes’ intersecting radiance, flowing-gold purple stanzas, the stanzas of the Most High’s command to the spirits, night-shining treasure stanzas, and the nine-colored stanzas of the Departed Net.

The *Scripture of the Numinous Writs in Purple Script* says: The *Upper Scripture of the Numinous Writs in Purple Script* is carved on slips of purple jade with azure-gold script.

The *Scripture of the Yellow Register Slips* states: One golden dragon is offered, and a cinnabar-written jade tablet is bound with azure silk. To seal the pledge of the Five Thearchs for ascension and deliverance, it is placed within an abyssal cliff, following the old method as before.

It also says: A cinnabar-written jade tablet and one golden dragon are struck against stone and sunk into the Three Rivers to seal the pledge of the Water Thearch for ascension and deliverance, following the old text of the jade instructions.

The *Jade Scripture of the Great Cavern* says: The jade tablets of the scriptures of the Most High are called the *Books of Blessing Continuity*.
