It also says: When the Most High writes on tablets of vermilion jade, the Hall of Jade Radiance becomes visible, and the Gates of the Four Luminaries may be entered.

The *Arrayed Records of the Later Sage Dao Lord* states: Carved on slips of purple jade with azure-gold script, the Tortoise Mother holds the brush, the Perfected Youth sweeps the mat, and the Jade Youth binds the slips—this is named the *Numinous Writ*.

The *Hidden Instructions of the Flying Dragon’s Plain Silk* says: The Lord Emperor of the Supreme Tenuity commands the Feathered Immortal Attendant Gentleman to hold the golden tablet and request the *Flying Feathered Stanzas*.

The *Mysterious Scripture of the Supreme Oneness’ Cavern Perfection* states: The Five White Primes who oversee destiny, clad in vermilion robes and crimson headscarves, each hold a white jade tray bearing the slips they govern.

The *Scripture of the Purple Radiance of Blazing Light* says: The Tortoise Mother holds the brush, the Supreme Oneness sweeps the mat, the Heavenly Consort attends with incense, and the Jade Brush binds the threads, using white jade for slips and golden script for the *Upper Talismans of the Perfected Immortals of the Capital of the Immortals*. The Left Duke seals it in a jade box with a cloud-brocade bag.

The *Scripture of Transformations* says: The *Golden Light Standing-in-Emptiness Tablet* states: The brocade bag seals the *Nine Crimson-Spotted Talismans* within the Primordial Mystery, which the Lord of Longevity and Destiny of the Southern Culmen obtained.

The *Upper Scripture of Jade Pendants and Golden Earrings* states: The Nine Elder Immortals of the Capital of the Immortals hold the *Golden Essence Standing-in-Emptiness Tablet* to request the treasure texts and bestow them upon the assembled perfected.

The *Scripture of the Numinous Stanzas of the Cavern Emptiness* says: *White Slips* deliver ranks, and *Azure Registers* determine immortality.

The *Supreme Scripture of the Supreme Prime* states: Without the *Jade Registers* inscribed with names on slips for the Three Clarities, one cannot obtain the *Inner Talismans of the Golden Tiger*.

The *Scripture of the Numinous Writs* says: The *Stanzas of the Numinous Treasure for Delivering Life from the Nine Qi of the Eastern Heaven* emerged from the Azure Youth of the Primordial Beginning’s Eastern Flower, sealed within a treasure casket of azure jade and stamped with the *Nine Qi Seal of the Primordial Beginning*.

The *Central Scripture of the Divine Immortals* states: When Laozi transmitted the *Pass*, he wrote the *Five Thousand Words* for Yin Xi, explaining its fifty-five chapters—this was in his own hand. Those who practice this Dao know the primordial qi, the parents, and what precedes heaven and earth; those who do not know this labor in vain.

The Lord Emperor of the Supreme Tenuity inscribed the *Scripture of the Purple Radiance of Blazing Light*’s chapter titles on purple slips, wrote its main text on golden slips, wherein the mysterious stanzas reside.

The *Registers of the Jade Emperor* says: The lofty assembly of perfected beings binds the *Stanzas of Spontaneity*.

The *Scripture of the Golden Mystery Feathered Stanzas* states: The *Hidden Writ of the Eight Effulgences of the Jade Clarity* and the *Inner Text of the Golden Mystery* arose before the Primordial Beginning—this is the *Scripture of Heaven*, which overawes the hundred spirits and all heavens.

The *Scripture of Inner Sounds* says: Heaven possesses the *Flying Mystery’s Spontaneous Qi*, which harmonizes the five tones to form the *Boundless Cavern Stanzas of Heaven*.

The *Upper Jade Instructions of the Vermilion Writ* states: The *Beginningless Numinous Treasure* informed the Water Thearch to erase the slips of transgressions, which were then transmitted to the Nine Heavens via the *Golden Dragon Courier* on silverwood slips written in vermilion, to be cast into the abyss of the Three Rivers. Initially, nine pairs of golden knobs were used to link the slips and sink them into the limpid springs, burying them at the peaks of one’s natal destiny. The Three Offices and Nine Bureaus record people’s merits and demerits—this principle is most clear.

The *Scripture of the Hidden Mystery’s Inner Text* says: The Azure Youth invited the myriad emperors to the winding chamber to expound the wondrous instructions of the treasure texts.

The *Scripture of the Cavern Perfection* states: The six-tiered jade terrace stands above the *Chart of the Nine Heavens*, upon which lie golden slips, jade tablets, and 100,000 *Purple Phoenix Cinnabar Stanzas*. The Jade Gentleman of the Most High’s Perfected Writs oversees them.

The *Scripture of the Eight Effulgences of Jade Light* says: The *Stanzas of the Jade Treasure Terrace of the Great Emptiness* are sealed within.

The *Scripture of the Flying Feathers* states: The *Ninefold Reverted Dao of the Supreme Sovereign* is written on crimson slips in purple script, secreted within the *Primordial Terrace of the Purple Heaven*.

The *Chart of the Twenty-Four Lives* states: Unfurling the Ninefold Radiance of Jade Essence, one reveals the three divisions of golden-script, purple-character jade texts and cinnabar stanzas—the *Eight Effulgences and Twenty-Four Lives Chart*—and places them upon a white jade table.

The *Hidden Writs of the Numinous Treasure* says: "Jade Birth" is the name of the tenth capital of the Tanyuan Heaven. Above it shine the stanzas of the Great Cavern, purple-script jade characters, resplendent in the Highest Clarity.

The *Mount Jade Capital Retreat* states: The many lofty immortals and perfected ones gather in the Mystic Capital of the Most High, unfurling the stanzas of the Empty Cavern.

The *Scripture of the Numinous Writs* says: In the Nine Qi Heaven of the East, the *Numinous Writs for Delivering Life* emerge from the Primordial Origin. The Eastern Florescence Azure Palace and the Azure Youth seal them within a green jade treasure casket, stamped with the seal of the Primordial Nine Qi.

Moreover, in the Three Qi Cinnabar Heaven of the South, the *Numinous Writs for Delivering Life* in jade stanzas emerge from the Primordial Origin. The Vermilion Mound Upper Palace and the Upper Prime of the Southern Culmen seal them within a red jade treasure casket, stamped with the seal of the Great Cinnabar Three Qi.

Furthermore, in the Seven Qi Heaven of the West, the *Numinous Writs for Delivering Life* in jade stanzas emerge from the Primordial Origin. The Golden Mother of the Western Florescence seals them within a white jade treasure casket, stamped with the seal of the Great Simplicity Seven Qi.

It is also said that in the Five Qi Heaven of the North, the *Numinous Writs for Delivering Life* in jade stanzas emerge from the Primordial Origin. The Jade Dawn Lord of the Northern Upper Palace seals them within a dark jade casket, stamped with the seal of the Great Mystery Five Qi.

The *Scripture of the Three Primes’ Distribution* says: The *Highest Three Primes Scripture* is the true writ of the Three Clarities. The Upper Perfected inspect the *Flying Cavern Stanzas*; the Upper Prime inspects the *Celestial Great Register*; the Middle Prime inspects the *Perfected Immortals’ Writs*; the Lower Prime inspects the *Earthly Jade Texts*. All such treasured stanzas and highest scriptures are engraved in cinnabar script on gold, stored in natural cloud-brocade satchels, sealed with the seals of the Three Primes’ numinous powers, and concealed in the Palace of Great Possession atop the Nine Heavens, within golden terraces and jade chambers, the ninefold winding cinnabar chambers.

The *Cinnabar Writs of the Numinous Treasure* states: The Primordial Origin commanded the Great Perfected to wield the brush, the Jade Consort to sweep the mat. Gold was cast into slips, jade carved into stanzas. The Five Elders bestowed the registers, which were secreted in the Numinous Capital Palace of the Nine Heavens.

The *Scripture of the Nine Heavens’ Return to Heaven* says: Thereupon the Great Unity swept the mat, the Heavenly Consort attended with incense, the Jade Efflorescence held the towel. Cinnabar-script purple characters were engraved upon white gold, their numinous countenances embossed, bound into jade stanzas, titled with the green register of those who attain the Dao, adorned with the ninefold dragon radiance.

The *Scripture of the Purple Phoenix and Cinnabar Writs* says: The Most High commanded the Perfected of the Supreme Ultimate to transmit the jade slips and golden script of the *Treasure Cavern, Flying Empyrean, and Utmost Mystery Stanzas*.

The *Mysterious Record of the Jade Emperor* states: In the first year of the Central August, on the seventh day of the ninth month, the Seven Sages fasted in the Luminous Clarity Long Palace and recorded the stanzas of their attainment. These were engraved on silver slips, stored in cloud-brocade satchels, sealed with the *Seal of Life’s Summons*, and entrusted to the Five Elders’ Immortal Capital, where the Left Duke oversees their registry in the Jasper Palace.

It also says: Within the Ancient Cavern Emptiness lies the *Supreme Writ of Heaven’s Return*, preserved by the Four Offices, expounded by the Five Emperors, its slips determined by the Seven Sages, its forms aligned with the primordial.

The *Scripture of Great Possession* says: The Most High’s jade stanzas, carved on jade slips, govern the myriad perfected.

The *True Scripture* says: The Year Star of the East, the Azure Emperor Goumang, bears the *Seal of Pervading Radiance*; the Sparkling Deluder of the South, the Vermilion Emperor Taihao, bears the *Seal of the Great Yang*; the Grand White of the West, the White Emperor Shaohao, bears the *Seal of Pervading Yin*; the Chronographic Star of the North, the Dark Emperor Zhuanxu, bears the *Seal of Pervading Spirit*; the Quelling Star of the Center, the Great Emperor Wenchang, bears the *Seal of the Square Spirit*.

The *Scripture of the Primordial Boundary* says: There are the twelve dharma seals.

The *Golden Root Scripture of the Purple Writs* says: There is the *Azure Essence Jade Seal*.

The *Upper Scripture of the Golden Chamber* says: Within the numinous divine capital of the Great Emperor’s palace lies the *Golden Chamber Formula for Delivering Life and Prolonging Years*. It is cast in gold slips, bound in silver threads, its text inscribed in purple ink.

The *Scripture for Dispelling Demons* says: One opens the vermilion coffer of the Nine Heavens and gazes upon the jasper slips of the Highest Clarity. Once the mysterious writ is engraved upon jade stanzas, the crimson names are first inscribed upon the numinous watchtower.

The *True Scripture of the Great Cavern* says: The *Eight Effulgences Jade Register* is concealed in the Jade Terrace of Great Simplicity, the Feathered Chamber of Mystic Clouds, sealed within the dense forest casket with the seals of the Jade Clarity’s Three Primes.

The *Catalogue of Slips and Tablets* says: The Azure Youth is called the *Lord of Azure Slips*. If there is no gold slip, silver or wood may suffice. If there is no jade tablet, paulownia wood may suffice, provided it is refined and fine. The true principle admits no gaps; one must take the tablets from the cloud-brocade satchel. These are the supreme titles of the Highest Perfected, the numinous stanzas of the Jade Emperor.

The *Inner Instructions of the Upper Clarity’s Nine Perfected Central Scripture* contains the *Jade Stanzas of the Mystic Numinous Primordial Lord, Treasured and Secret, Racing the Sun and Moon*.

The *Scripture of the Seven Transformations of the Divine Continent* says: The Great Yin Jade Dawn, the Nine Heavens’ Perfected Consort, the Purple Dawn Lord, receives the *Treasure Stanzas of Flowing Essence and Flying Radiance*.

The *Central Scripture of the Great Clarity* says: There is the *Celestial One’s Seal of the Eight Poles*.

The *Primordial Precepts of Mount Tortoise* says: There is the *Seal of the Flowing Gold Phoenix*. It also says: The Heavenly August Great Emperor dispatched the embroidered-robed messenger Leng Guangzi Qi to bestow upon Mao Ying the *Divine Seal, Jade Stanzas, and Golden Watchtower*. The Sage Lord commanded the Perfected of the Supreme Ultimate to send the *Orthodox Unity’s Upper Mystery Jade Gentleman*, Wang Zhong, Bao Bing, and others to confer the seal upon Mao Ying.

The *Scripture of the Flying Feathers of the Most High* says: The Great Perfected Venerable wears the *Nine-Colored Flying Clouds’ Radiant Feather Stanzas*.

The *Scripture of the Six Jia of the Numinous Flight* says: The Jade Perfected Azure Lord bears the *Seal of the Flowing Gold Phoenix* and the *Ninefold Vermilion Mottled Talisman of the Most High*.

The *Inner True Scripture of the Five Emperors* says: There are the *Seals for Sealing Spirits and Controlling Demons* and the *Seal of the Yellow Spirit and Central August*.

The *Scripture of the Three Sovereigns* says: The natural texts of the Three Sovereigns all employ gold and jade. The Heavenly Sovereign’s bestowal uses dark jade for slips and azure jade for text; the Earthly Sovereign’s bestowal uses yellow jade for slips and white jade for text, bound with golden hooks, linked with golden clasps, placed upon a jade table, covered with a pearl kerchief, a treasure canopy, and a forest of jewels. It is enshrined in the Azure Palace, sealed in the Purple Chamber, perfumed with the five fragrances, and attended by the ten blossoms.

*The Scripture of the Seven Transformations and Seven Changes* states: The *Flowing Gold Phoenix Seal of the Purple Chamber* was worn by the *Supreme August One, the First Master*.

*The Preface to the Three Sovereigns* states: The *Seal Script of the Nine Heavens* is used to summon the *Nine Heavenly Investigators*.

*The Upper Clarity Scripture of Transformations* states: The *Most High Void Sovereign Lord* wears the *Cinnabar August Jade Seal*. It further says: The *Great Illuminator of the Three Origins, Supreme August Lord* bears the *Divine Tiger Purple Seal*. There is also the *August Lord of the Supreme Thearch*, who wears the *Golden Tiger Phoenix Script* and bears the *Divine Tiger Jade Seal*. It further states: The *True Jade of the Nine Empyreans* is paired with the *Golden Phoenix Seal*.

*The Scripture of the Hidden Calendar* states: The *Heavenly King Marquis* wears a *purple sash with a golden seal*.

*The True Charts of the Five Peaks* states: The *Lord of Mount Tai* wears the *Seal of Pervading Yang and Great Illumination*; the *Lord of Mount Heng* wears the *Seal of Night-Shining Heavenly Perfection*; the *Lord of Mount Song* wears the *Seal of Divine Ancestry and Yang Harmony*; the *Lord of Mount Hua* wears the *Seal of Opening Heaven and Communing with Perfection*; the *Lord of Mount Heng* wears the *Seal of the Long Ford and Awakening to Perfection*; the *Elder of Mount Qingcheng* wears the *Seal of the Three Courts*.

*The Arrayed Records of the Later Sage* states: The *Purple Tenuity*, the *Upper Perfected*, the *Heavenly Thearch*, and the *Jade Clarity Lord* dispatched the *Eight Radiance Jasper Chariot* to welcome the *Sage Lord*, ascending to the *Upper Clarity Palace*, bestowing upon him the *Jeweled Cinnabar Phoenix Seal*.

*The Arrayed Records of the Nine Mysteries Dao Lord of the Later Sage* states: The *Great Yin Method* encompasses life and death, with *black registers and white ledgers*, *vermilion and azure jade-bound slips*, recording the sequence of prior and subsequent births.

*The Arrayed Records of the Dao Lord of the Later Sage* states: The *Jade Clarity Lord* bestowed upon the *Dao Lord* the *Jade Phoenix Seal*.

*The Scripture of Flying Through the Three Realms* states: Below is the *Golden Seal of the Great One with Purple Sash*, the *Faith Seal of the Majestic Joy Heavenly Thearch*. Cultivating the *Dao of Flying Through the Three Realms of the Numinous Treasure*, it is worn by the *Perfected*.

*The Upper Scripture of the Five Invocation Talismans* states: The *Seal of Communing with the Five Stars’ Spirits* imprints the *Five Stars’ Numinous Talismans*.

*The Traditions of Daoist Learning* states: King Helü of Wu obtained the *True Writ* but could not comprehend it. He sealed it with *golden seals* and stamped it with the *Jade August Seal*, then inquired of Confucius, the Grand Master of Lu. It further states: Yu sealed the *Five Talismans* in a *golden essence casket*, secured with the *Seal of the Dark Capital*.

*The Biographies of Divine Transcendents* states: Wei Shuqing said to his son, Du Shi: "You may retrieve my *immortality formula* from beneath the cassia tree in the northwest of the chamber. Follow it and ingest it to attain longevity." Du Shi grasped the *jade casket*, sealed with the *Flying Transcendent’s Seal*, and took it to ingest the *Five-Colored Numinous Mother*, thereafter ascending as a transcendent.

*The Scripture of the Northern Thearch* states: The *Secret Seal of Mount Dengdu* is employed to *save the world and inquire*, subjugating and controlling ghosts and spirits.

*The Register of Assembled Transcendents* states: Du Lanxiang was a female transcendent who descended upon the household of Zhang Shuo at Mount Bao by Dongting Lake. Zhang Shuo was one who cultivated the Dao. She transmitted to him the *Dao of Flying Transformation*, leaving behind a *jade slip* and a *jade spittoon*. She also bestowed upon him a *feathered robe of yellow unicorn*, a garment worn by *upper transcendents*, not found within *grotto-heavens*.

*Section Eighteen of the Daoist Canon concludes. Section Nineteen of the Daoist Canon.*

Few and Tables

*The Record of the Ten Continents* states: Within the Golden Peak Abbey on Yingzhou, there stands a *blue-luminous jade table*, draped with a plain cloth woven of *cloud-grasping* silk, its legs carved from *water-jade* into inverted dragon-pigs.

*The Scripture of the Eight Radiant Lights of Jade* states: When the assembled perfected ones gather in ritual, the Great Thearch humbles himself before the table.

*The Supreme Mystery Scripture of the Great One* states: Within the Purple Chamber of the Grand Tenuity, there is a youth named *Jingjing*, styled *Huiyuan*. Before the Lord Emperor, he bears a *crimson jade table*, upon which rests the register of destinies under his charge. It further states: The Five—*Great One, Noble Scion, White Prime, Controller of Fates,* and *Peach Lord*—each clad in vermilion robes and crimson kerchiefs, hold aloft a *white jade table*, upon which rests the register each oversees.

*The Hidden Writ of Jade Purity* states: The Lord Emperor of the Grand Tenuity advances to bow before the table of the August Thearch. It further states: The Supreme Lord Emperor then pushed aside his table, reclining in chant, gazing emptily into the vast sky, reciting the *Hidden Writ of Jade Purity*, singing the *Numinous Stanzas of the Primordial Radiance*, his voice soaring amid the clouds, pure and subtle as the root of jade.

*The Scripture of the Great Cavern* states: The Five Registers of the Minor Youths of the Grand Tenuity bear *jade tables*, which the Lord Emperor attends, governing the communication of all spirits.

*The Scripture of Transformations* states: There is a *golden-luminous table standing in the void*. It further states: The *Primordial Beginning* struck the table, chanting aloud into the vast sky.

*The Upper Scripture of Jade Pendants and Golden Earrings* states: The Nine Elder Transcendents of the Transcendent Capital bear *tables of golden essence*, upon which they present sacred texts to the assembled perfected ones.

*The Scripture of the Cavernous Spirit* states: One brushes and wipes the table, placing the scripture before it.

*The Scripture of Images and Names* states: The Eastern Supreme Honored One rests upon a *curved table of seven treasures adorned with phoenix patterns*, unfolding the essential true scriptures of the Dao.

*The Scripture of Dharma Offerings* states: The Three Perfected Ones stand beside a *table suspended in the void*, with seven treasures hanging to cover the scripture above.

*The Scripture of Many Chapters* states: The Primordial Beginning, Supreme Honored One, in profound contemplation, strikes the table and raises his voice, summoning the Five Thearchs to deliberate and settle the workings of yin and yang, reckon the cycles of kalpas, adjust the courses of the celestial rivers, and inspect the registers of heavenly measures.

*The Scripture of the Cavernous Spirit* states: There is a *table with framed legs* for placing scriptures and talismans.

*The Yellow Plain Scripture of the Supreme* states: Whenever one receives the *True Scripture of the Great Cavern* or a single esoteric text, one must always place the scripture upon a table in a clean and pure location.

*The Scripture of the Nine Dark Realms* states: The August Honored One resides in the *Three Primordials Palace* within the *Wondrous Realm of the Nine Purities*, presiding over the *flowering treasure of the Three Qi*, seated upon a *cloud-jade throne* to review the charts and registers, delivering all from suffering.

*The Twenty-Four Images of Life* states: One unfolds the *Nine Radiant Jade Wrappings*, revealing the *Three Sections*—golden script, purple characters, jade texts, and cinnabar stanzas.

*The Twenty-Four Images of Life of the Eight Radiances* are contained within a *white jade table standing in the void*, amid nine-colored clouds, with a *flying-script brocade canopy* suspended above the scripture.

*The Hidden Instructions of the Dragon-Flying Plain Silk* states: The Lord Emperor of the Grand Tenuity commands the *Feathered Transcendent Attendant* to bear a *golden table* to present the *feathered scriptures of flight*.

*The Audience Text of the True Writ of the King of the Upper Clarity* states: There are twelve *flowing-luminous great numinous jade tables* held by attendants.

*The Inner Transmission of the Primordial Beginning* states: The heavens each present *lotus thrones* covered by jeweled canopies.

*The Biographies of Divine Transcendents* states: The *Yellow and Old* dispatched transcendent officials and jade maidens bearing a *golden table and jade cup*, filled with medicine to bestow upon Shen Xi. It further states: The King of Huainan provided the *Eight Masters* with a *table of gold and jade*, observing the rites of a disciple at the gate.

*The Regulations of the Four Poles* states: For all sacred scriptures, the tables and cloths must not be casually lent to others.

*The Scripture of the Great Mystery* states: When *Laozi* transmitted the scriptures, precepts, registers, rituals, and esoteric instructions, he used a *small table with framed legs*, placing the scripture upon it and covering it with a colored cloth.

*The Scripture of the Supreme Mystery of the Great One* states: The *Supreme Mystery Scripture of the Great One* is separately stored in a *satchel*, sealed with a precious vessel, and placed upon a table.

*The Scripture of the Immeasurable* states: The seat of the Supreme One is three *zhang* high, and within the *Palace of the Purple Terrace*, a high seat of six *chi* is arranged.

*The Scripture of Golden Perfection and Jade Radiance* states: The Emperors of the Nine Heavens present *jade tables* and *golden lungs*.

*The Classic of Mountains and Seas* states: The Queen Mother of the West leans upon a table, wearing sheng-ornaments as a support. *Sheng* refers to the jade sheng-ornaments she wears. Other accounts that describe the Queen Mother of the West as having a head resembling a sheng-bird are greatly mistaken.

*The Scripture of the Origin* states: The Primordial Beginning, Supreme Honored One, resides in the *Jeweled-Adorned High Seat* of the *Hall of Eternal Joy*. Though the seat has form, it does not obstruct things, and people may come and go without hindrance. There are also small *lapis lazuli seats*, arranged in rows on both sides, each five *chi* high.

*The Inner Transmission of Lord Mao* states: The *White Jade Tortoise Mountain* connects to the *Jade Grove Canopy*, where the Queen Mother of the West resides.

*The Yellow Plain Methods of the Supreme* states: The *Azure Essence* resides on *Purple Shaman Mountain*, transforming into the chamber of the King of Wang, within which there is a *jade table*.

*The Seven Sages’ Mysterious Record of the Cavernous Perfection* states: The Left Transcendent submits memorials beneath the tables of the Seven Sages, the Nine Heavenly Emperors.

*The Scripture of Feathered Flight* states: In practicing the *Dao of the Three Ones*, one sits upon a *golden-shaped jade table*, with a *golden censer and jade spoon*.

*The Poems of the Supreme Perfected* state: The Grand Tenuity opens the *jade table*.

*The Biographies of the Arrayed Transcendents* state: Within the *Great Chamber Mountain*, there is an *earth transcendent* named *Na Shu*, who reclines upon a *table*.

*The Declarations of the Perfected* state: Within *Deer Track Mountain*, there is a deep ravine, within which there are naturally formed *stone groves, stone couches,* and *curved screens*.

---

Vehicles and Entourages

*The Feathered Scripture of Flight of the Supreme* states: The High Perfected Ones of the Jade Purity are the High Spirits of the Upper Clarity; the High Spirits of the Upper Clarity are the High Numinous Ones of the Grand Clarity; the High Numinous Ones of the Grand Clarity are the High Transcendents of the Flying Transcendents. For all who practice the Dao of the Jade Purity, when they depart, the various heavens provide escort, erecting *seven-colored standards*, driving a *purple cloud chariot* with *twelve jade wheels*, the *Six Masters* clearing the path, *flying dragons* flanking the shafts. For the Dao of the Upper Clarity, when one departs, the Five Thearchs provide escort, erecting *purple-feathered standards*, driving a *flying cloud cinnabar carriage*, aligned with the Upper Clarity, with *transcendent ministers* to the left and right. For the Dao of the Grand Clarity, when one departs, the Five Thearchs provide escort, erecting *five-colored standards*, driving a *dragon carriage and white hornless dragon*, the *Grand Ultimate* clearing the path with a *triple canopy*.

It further states: Wang Zongzhen became Mao Ying, summoning two *Crimson-Crowned Envoys* who rode a *flowing-light chariot*. Azure serpents grasped green standards, wielding jade staves adorned with feathered banners, while crimson clouds veiled the sun as a transverse canopy. The envoys, clad in embroidered robes and lotus crowns, each bore a *purple-silk writ* of a hundred characters, which they delivered to Mao Ying’s two younger brothers, Gu and Zhong. Thus, Gu was granted the title of *Earthly Perfected Upper Immortal and Register-Fixing Divine Lord*, while Zhong received the rank of *Life-Preserving Immortal Lord of the Three Offices*, each dispatched to their appointed divine palaces and upper bureaus in accordance with the *purple-silk mandate*, with resources duly allocated to both lords.

In the second year of *Yuanshou* during the reign of Emperor Ping of Han, on the *jiyou* day of the eighth month, the *Perfected of the Southern Marchmount*, the *Lord of Western Citadel*, the *Queen Mother of Tortoise Mountain*, and the *Azure Lad of Fangzhu* all rode *verdant-light chariots*, driving *divine-tiger carriages*, and together visited Mao Ying at the northern slope of Golden Altar Peak on Mount Juqu.

It further states: The esoteric Dao of the Flying Transcendents summons the dawn of the Five Celestial Bodies, and those who constantly practice it shall, after fifteen years, be welcomed thus: the *Old Man of the Southern Culmen* and the *Upper Perfected of Cinnabar Mound* in a *verdant-cloud chariot*; the *Old Man of the Western Culmen* and *Master of Pristine Numinosity* in a *yellow-silk carriage*; the *Old Man of the Northern Culmen* and the *Mystic Upper Immortal Sovereign* in a *mystic-light dragon*; the *Old Man of the Eastern Culmen* and the *Duke of Supporting Yang* in a *green-tiger carriage*; and the *Old Man of the Central Origin* and *Master of Upper Mysteries* beneath a *curved-dawn canopy*. When the Five Elders convene, they ascend together to the *Purple Void*—these Five Elders are the Perfected of the Five Stars, not to be confused with the *Five Thearchs’ official documents* of Master Pei among the stars, nor with the methods of the *Five Directions’ Elder Scholars* of *Cloudfang*. Those who follow this path become Flying Transcendents.

It further states: The *Eight Esoteric Sayings of the Dao* comprise eight principles, their words lofty and wondrous. In a serene chamber, with mind at ease and emptiness made true, one may behold the *cinnabar-light qi*, the *Three Pristine flying clouds*, the *eight chariots and crimson carriages*, the *purple auroras and jade wheels*, the *Upper Clarity’s tranquil paths* where reins are turned, the *Three Origins’ High Sovereigns* bearing standards, *divine lads* grasping shafts, the *Grand Pristine* holding canopies, and the *Southern Culmen* approaching the chariot. Then, as radiance shines outward and images illuminate the void, the *Master of the Grand Void* may perceive them without effort—like *congealed frost washing blossoms*, they are the *mystic marrow and golden elixir*.

The first of the *Eight Esoteric Sayings* states: On the eight solar terms, at dawn, face north in the early morning (slightly earlier than daybreak). If *purple, green, and white clouds* appear, they are the *Three Origins Lords’ Three Pristine flying clouds*. At that time, the *Three Origins Lords* ride the *eight chariots* to ascend and pay homage to the *Jade Clarity Lord of the Heavenly Thearch*.

When you witness this, bow twice and declare your plea to attend the wheel-hub.

The second of the *Eight Esoteric Sayings* states: On the eight solar terms, at midnight, face northeast. If *dark azure and yellow clouds* appear, they are the *Grand Culmen Heavenly Thearch Lord* riding the *Eight Radiant Chariots* to ascend and pay homage to the *Highest Jade Sovereign*.

The third of the *Eight Esoteric Sayings* states: On the *jiazi* decade’s *wuchen* and *jisi* days at dawn, face northwest. If *purple, azure, and yellow clouds* appear, they are the *Grand Culmen Perfected Lord’s Three Pristine Clouds*. At that time, the *Grand Culmen Perfected Lord* and the *Highest Perfected Ones* ride the *Mysterious Radiance Green Chariot* to ascend to the *Purple Tenuity Palace*.

The fourth of the *Eight Esoteric Sayings* states: On the *jiaxu* decade’s *wuyin* and *jimao* days at dawn, face southeast. If *crimson, white, and azure clouds* appear, they are the *Fusang Grand Thearch Lord’s Three Pristine Clouds*. At that time, the *Fusang Grand Thearch Lord* rides the *Luminous Eightfold Path Chariot* to ascend to the *Purple Tenuity Palace*.

The fifth of the *Eight Esoteric Sayings* states: On the *jiashen* decade’s *wuzi* and *jichou* days at dawn, face due west. If *white, crimson, and purple clouds* appear, they are the *Grand Pristine Highest Perfected White Thearch Lord’s Three Pristine Clouds*. At that time, the *Grand Pristine Highest Perfected Ones* and the *White Thearch Lord* ride the *Jade Ornament Chariot* to ascend to the *Jade Heaven’s Mysterious Sovereign Highest Perfected Ones*.

The sixth of the *Eight Esoteric Sayings* states: On the *jiawu* decade’s *wuxu* and *jihai* days at dawn, face due south. If *azure, crimson, and yellow clouds* appear, they are the *Southern Culmen Highest Perfected Red Thearch Lord*. At that time, he rides the *Crimson Jade Green Chariot* to ascend to the *Lofty Breeze Terrace*.

The seventh of the *Eight Esoteric Sayings* states: On the *jiachen* decade’s *wushen* and *yiyou* days at dawn, face southwest. If *green, purple, and azure clouds* appear, they are the *Highest Clarity Perfected Ones*. At that time, they ride the *Mysterious Radiance Eightfold Crimson Chariot* to ascend to the *Highest Heavenly Thearch*.

The eighth of the *Eight Esoteric Sayings* states: On the *jiayin* decade’s *wuwu* and *jiwei* days at dawn, face due east. If *vermilion, jade-green, and yellow clouds* appear, they are the *Grand Void’s Highest Perfected Ones*. At that time, they ride the *Jade Meandering Chariot* to ascend to the *Grand Thearch Lord*.

On the eight solar terms, when the *Three Pristine Clouds* appear, the *purple clouds* are above, the *green clouds* follow, and the *white clouds* are below, all overlapping one another. Observe them with care.

The *Scripture of Transference* states: The *Perfected Sovereign* joins the *yellow auroras*, traversing the four directions; the *flying canopy and green plow* ascend to the *Golden Palace*.

The *Red Writ of the Numinous Treasure* states: The *Perfected Ones of Heaven* ride the *jade chariot of azure auroras*.

The *Perfect Scripture of the Grand Grotto* states: The *Most High* rides the *One Radiance Chariot*, receiving the *Ninefold Splendor of the Grand Dawn’s Hidden Talisman*.

The *Dragon Script of the Hidden Writ of Highest Clarity* states: The *Queen Mother* rides the *Nine-Canopied Floral Chariot*, with all the *Perfected Ones* in attendance.

The *Scripture of Purple Writ* states: The *Eastern Sea’s Azure Lad, Lord of the Square Reservoir*, fasts within the *Crimson Palace’s Yellow Chamber* for three years before riding the *azure cloud chariot*.

The *Biography of the Grand Prime Perfected* states: There is the *spotted dragon chariot*.

The *Scripture of Golden Perfection and Jade Radiance* states: There is the *jade chariot*; also, in the *Highest Clarity’s Three Heavens’ Arrayed Records*, there is the *purple chariot*.

The *Jade Scripture of the Grand Grotto* states: The *Azure Lad* rides the *carved jade chariot*; the *Perfected Warden of Prohibitions* rides the *sun-and-moon chariot*. It further states: The *Grand Culmen Primordial Lady* rides the *feathered chariot*.

The *Scripture of the Most High* states: There is the *white simurgh chariot*.

The *Inner Biography of Lord Mao* states: The *Eastern Sea’s Azure Lad* rides the *carriage of jade inlay*. It further states: Within the *stone chamber of Crane-Crying Mountain*, a *natural seat* is set, with a *golden floral canopy*. It also states: The *Five Thearch Perfected Ones* all ride the *Eight Radiance Jade Chariot*.

The *Scripture of the Twenty-Four Lives’ Diagrams* states: The *Later Sage, Lord Li*, roamed the *Western River*, surveying the eight directions. He encountered the *Primordial Commencement* riding the *Eight Radiance Jade Chariot*, driving *mysterious dragons*, and came forth. Lord Li inquired about the *celestial script’s jade characters*, yet their wondrous passages remained unmastered. The *Primordial Commencement* then commanded the *Ultimate Dao’s Perfected Ones*, whereupon he disgorged the *Grand Mystery’s Inner Vision Jade Talisman* to bestow upon him.

The *Scripture of Transformations* states: The *radiant chariot, crimson plow, purple carriage*—these are what the *Nine Heavenly Thearch Kings* ride.

The *Highest Clarity’s Oral Instructions* state: The *Mysterious Mother* rides the *Three Pristine Chariot*. It further states: The *Primordial Father* controls the *crimson-feathered flying carriage*, with a *crimson simurgh* harnessed to the left and a *purple phoenix* to the right.

The *Oral Instructions on the Corpse and the Unrefined* state: The *Heavenly Thearch Lord of the Grand Tenuity* mounts the *white simurgh chariot*, driving the *black-feathered phoenix*, and roams the *azure waters’ realm*.

The *Jade Scripture of the Grand Grotto* states: The *August Thearch* rides the *luminous jade wheel*, turning to feast within the *sun’s midst*.

The *Inner Biography of Lord Mao* states: The *Supreme Dao Lord* was granted the *Eight Radiance Jade Chariot*, the *phoenix-sealed golden perfection*, and the *curved dawn’s flying canopy*. It further states: The *Azure Florescence Lad, Dao Lord* rides the *azure aurora chariot*. It also states: The *Highest Perfected Lord, Red Thearch* rides the *crimson jade green chariot*. It further states: The *Grand Clarity Perfected Lord* rides the *azure dragon and purple feathered canopy*. It also states: The *Grand Prime Perfected* wields the *purple cloud’s staff*, rides the *spotted dragon chariot* and the *white tiger plow*, and bears the *curved dawn’s treasure canopy*. It further states: The *Grand Pristine Perfected Lord* rides the *tiger-flag tiger chariot*, with a *golden canopy and jade wheel*, wielding the *nine-colored staff*, entering and exiting the *Grand Clarity*.

The *Scripture of Golden Perfection and Highest Radiance* states: The *Most High Great Dao Lord* rides the *jade chariot and azure carriage*; the *Harmonious Grand Dao Lord* rides the *white cloud chariot*. It further states: The *Mysterious Harmony Dao Lord* drives the *mysterious dragon’s bannered carriage*.

The *Jade Scripture of the Grand Grotto* states: The *Eight August Elder Lords* ride the *yellow langgan chariot*, grasping the *purple phoenix’s staff*, and enter the *Grand Elder’s Chamber*. The *Lord of Myriad Floras* rides the *Three Pristine’s radiant feathered chariot*, reposing in the *Chamber of Ten Thousand Chariots*.

The *Eight Pristine Chapters* state: The *Four Elders* turn the *brocade chariot*, and the *ten thousand immortals* pay homage to the *Thearch’s chamber*.

The *Inner Biography of Lord Mao* states: The *Vermilion Palace’s Messenger* drives the *dark steed*, grasping the *green staff*.

The *Declarations of the Perfected* state: The *Purple Primordial Lady* rides the *feathered treasure cloud chariot*, driving *nine dragons*, with *nine thousand female riders*, clad in *brocade robes* and *azure feathered skirts*.

The *Scripture of Spontaneity* states: The dragon-reins rise high, the cloud-canopy towers majestically; immortal youths and jade maidens ascend the dragon with me.

The *Supreme Perfected Scripture* states: The Eastern Blue Thearch rides the *nine-dragon cloud chariot*.

The *Scripture of the Cavernous Void* states: The *Celestial Venerable of Primordial Beginning* and the hosts of heaven together ride the *jade palanquin and jasper wheels*.

The *Preface to the Five Elders’ Red Writ of the Jade Chapters of Primordial Beginning* states: The *Supreme Dao Lord* and the perfected beings of the ten directions ride the *five-colored jade wheels* and *nine-colored dragons*; the *Perfected of Wondrous Conduct* rides the *elephant-cloud jade palanquin*, ascending to the *Jade Capital*; the *Perfected of the Central Ultimate* constantly rides the *elephant-wheel chariot*; the *Perfected of High Flight* constantly rides the *nine-colored dragons*, roaming the *Jade Purity* clouds; the *flying celestial spirits* ride the *azure mist palanquin*, wandering the heavens of *Jade Exaltation*; the *Black Thearch Lord* rides the *four-scene chariot*.

The *Scripture of the Three Primes’ Distribution* states: The *Supreme Venerable of Primordial Beginning* rides the *purple palanquin*.

The *Inner Biography of Lord Mao* states: *Lord Wang* rides the *nine-canopied palanquin*.

The *Scripture of Grotto Heavens* states: The *Spirit Radiance Dao Lord* rides the *crimson cloud chariot*.

The *Supreme Scripture of Flying Feathered Flight* states: The perfected of *Central Harmony* drive the *brocade chariot*.

The *Inner Biography of Lord Mao* states: The *Queen Mother* rides the *green radiance chariot*.

The *Scripture of the Eight Radiant Jades of Jade Light* states: The *Dao Lord of Eastern Primordial Radiance* rides the *azure cloud chariot*, driving *blue-green dragons*. It further states: The *Dao Lord of Southern Mystic Radiance* rides the *five-colored cloud chariot*, driving *phoenixes*. And: The *Dao Lord of Southern Spirit Radiance* rides the *crimson cloud chariot*; the *Dao Lord of Southwestern Primordial Radiance* rides the *purple cloud chariot*, driving *six dragons*; the *Dao Lord of Western Bright Radiance* rides the *white cloud chariot*, driving *white tigers*; the *Dao Lord of Northern Mystic Harmony* rides the *pearl-jade chariot*.

The *Scripture of the Golden Root* states: The *Jade Thearch Lord* rides the *azure mist nine-phoenix flying chariot*.

The *Hidden Writ of Jade Purity* states: The *Lord of the Grand Tenuity* ascends the *eight-jewel flying celestial palanquin*, tilting the canopy over the *radiant city*. It further states: The *Dao Lord of the Northeast*, *Ge Xian*, rides the *eight-chariot flying tortoise vehicle*, descending to govern the *mud-pill palace* of humanity.

The *Hidden Instructions for Ascending Perfection* states: The *Perfected of Great Primordiality* rides the *white tiger chariot*, with *eight-colored cloud chariots*.

The *Declarations of the Perfected* states: The immortal *Xu Yufu* rides a *new green calf chariot*. It further states: *Wang Meishou’s* younger sister, the *Lady Attendant of the Central Candidate*, rides the *white ox chariot*.

The *Inner Instructions of the Central Scripture of the Nine Perfected* states: The *Southern Culmen Elder* and the *Cinnabar Mound Supreme Perfected* welcome with the *green cloud chariot-canopy*; the *Western Culmen Elder* and the *White Spirit of Yu Si* welcome with the *yellow chariot*; the *Human Prime Elder* and the *Central Supreme of Primordiality* welcome with the *curved dawn chariot*; the *Five Elders* unite and ascend together to the *Purple Spirit*.

The *Biography of Lord Wang* states: *Lord Wang* rides the *tiger palanquin*, with *golden canopy and jade wheels*, entering and exiting *Supreme Purity*, attending to affairs in *Grand Simplicity*.

The *Biography of the Wei Lady of Southern Marchmount* states: The Lady rides the *tiger palanquin*, the *jade chariot*, and the *hidden axle vehicle*.

The *Declarations of the Perfected* states: The *Lady of Southern Marchmount* drives the *nine-canopied chariot*.

The *Records of Searching for Spirits* states: The jade maiden *Cheng Zhiqiong* drives the *covered chariot*, accompanied by eight maidservants.

The *Scripture of the Five Talismans* states: At *Zhong Zhi’s* summit stands the *seven-jeweled golden terrace*, the abode of the *Primordial Qi’s* purple watchtower, where the *Heavenly Thearch Lord* resides.

The *Jade Scripture of the Grand Cavern* states: *Great Brilliance* is the name of the central hall in the *Jade Purity Heaven*, where the *Supreme August King Perfected* roams.

The *Scripture of Great Peace* states: The *Grand Void Jasper Terrace* is the hall of *Cavernous Perfection*, within the *Golden Flower*, where the *hosts of perfected attendants* reside.

The *Upper Scripture of the Purple Writ of Numinous Books* states: There is the *Grand Void Jasper Terrace*, the *cinnabar palace hall*.

The *Red Writ of the Numinous Treasure* states: The *Perfected of Wondrous Conduct* approaches the *Primordial Beginning* to receive the *Five Chapters of the Red Writ of Perfected Script*. Thereupon, the *Primordial Beginning* commands the hosts of perfected to enter the *Golden Terrace of Grand Stillness*, the *Jade Treasure Hall*, and the *Nine Radiant Flower Chambers*.

The *Golden Root Scripture of the Purple Writ* states: There is the *golden hall*.

The *Inner Chapters of the Mysterious Wondrous* state: There is the *seven-jeweled hall*.

The *Jade Scripture of the Grand Cavern* states: There is the *Feather Radiance Hall*, within the *Courtyard of Grand Nothingness*. *Jade Countenance* is the *Bright Hall of the Supreme*.

The *Golden Mystery Scripture of Cavernous Radiance* states: The *Jade Thearch* commands the *Heavenly Thearch Lord of the Grand Tenuity* to seat the *Myriad Spirits* in the *veranda chambers*, scattering *flower incense* in the *jade eaves*, lingering in the *Eight-Jewel Chambers*, feasting in the *Nine-Jewel Halls*.

The *Scripture of the Foreign Release of Karma* states: There is the *Radiant Jasper Hall*.

The *Instructions on the Jade Scripture of the Grand Cavern* state: The *Jasper Terrace of the Western Fields* is where the *Great Thearch* resides, and there is the *Jade Purity Terrace*. There is also the *Flower-Scattering Terrace*.

The *Scripture of the Jade Capital of the Supreme* states: The *Jade Capital* has the *Seven-Jeweled Palace*, and the palace has the *seven jewels*. The *Mystic Terrace* is the *Supreme’s* seat of governance, and there is also the *Heavenly Treasure Terrace*.

The *Scripture of Supreme Purity* states: There is the *Purple Jasper Mystic Terrace*.

The *Perfect Scripture of the Grand Cavern* states: The *Perfected of Supreme Purity*, the *Marshal of the Hosts of Immortals*, and the *Master of Longevity Techniques* ascend the *Tai Chang Cang Lang Mountain’s* *Shuang Terrace*, within the *twin jade caves*, drinking deeply of the *purple luminous mushroom nectar*.

The *Declarations of the Perfected* states: There is the *Jade Flower Chamber*, where the *Stone-Inscribed Perfected* resides.

The *Five Victorious Writings* state: Drive the *flying dragon* to the *Western Florescence Terrace* to pay homage to the *Imperial Perfected of the Red Writ*.

The *Instructions on the Jade Scripture* state: The *Perfected of Great Primordiality of the Supreme Mystery Palace* regularly, on the *Spring Equinox*, convenes the *hosts of immortal officials* at the *Kunlun Jasper Terrace* to collate and verify the *Numinous Treasure Perfected Scriptures*. It further states: The *Perfected of the Sunlit Terrace* regularly, on the *Beginning of Winter*, convenes the *hosts of immortal officials and jade maidens* atop the *Numinous Treasure Sunlit Terrace* to collate and verify the *registers of Dao learners*.

The *Scripture of Fundamental Conduct* states: There is the *Jade Terrace for Seeking the Perfected*.

The *Scriptures of the Hosts of Chapters* state: The *Thearch Lord* leads the *hosts of perfected* to assemble within the *Golden Terrace of the Grand Void’s* inner chamber.

The *Scripture of Jade Characters* states: The *nine-tiered terrace* stands upon the *Jade Capital Mountain*, resplendent above the *Mystic Capital*, bearing the *Supreme Perfected Jade Seal*.

It further states: The *Fragrant Radiance Heavenly Center* is another name for the *Jade Capital Mystic Terrace*, where the *Western Numinous Perfected* regularly recites the *Boundless Grotto Chapters*, wandering and roaming above it.

The *Great Grotto Jade Scripture* states: Above the *Nine Heavens* stands the *Luminous Perfected Terrace*.

The *Inner Transmission of Lord Mao* states: The *Perfected of the Hour of Chen* bears the *Ting-Sheng Talisman* upon the *Azure Wave Terrace*.

The *Scripture of Guiding and Absorbing the Three Luminaries* states: The *Perfected of Fixed Light* resides within the *Absolute Contemplation Terrace* of the *August Tenuity Heaven*, guiding and absorbing the *primordial qi*. It further states: The *Ninefold Transformed Perfected* resides within the *Proclamation of Yang Terrace of No Utterance* in the *Jade Perfection Heaven*. It further states: The *Guiding Immortal Perfected* resides within the *Cloud-Shaded Flowery Grove Terrace* of the *Harmonious Youth Heaven*. It further states: The *Cloud-Flower Perfected* resides within the *Mystic Chant Treasure-Canopy Terrace* of the *Level Nurturing Heaven*. It further states: The *Yang King Perfected* resides within the *Grand Perfected Terrace*. It further states: The *Dharma Qi Perfected* resides within the *Flying Terrace*. It further states: The *Ze-Ying Perfected* resides within the *Boundless Contemplation Terrace* of the *Crossing Balance Heaven*.

The *Declarations of the Perfected* states: The *White Jade Tortoise Terrace* is sealed by the *Ninefold Numinous Grand Perfected Sovereign*.

The *Scriptures of the Three Sovereigns* states: The *Celestial Writ of the August Script* received by the *Human Sovereign* was inscribed on *cinnabar jade tablets* with *yellow jade characters*, placed within the *Azure Palace* and sealed within the *Purple Chamber*.

The *Great Grotto Perfected Scripture* states: All those of *heaven-endowed immortal talent* have their names inscribed upon the *Golden Chamber*.

The *Golden Mystery Feathered Chapters* states: Beneath the *Purple Chamber*, affairs are administered within the *Ninefold Jade Chamber of Jade Purity*, the *Yellow Chamber*, and the *Azure Chamber*.

The *Central Scripture of the Calendar Storehouse* states: The *Kunlun Mountain* possesses *ninefold golden walls* and *twelve jade towers*, the domain of *divine immortals*.

The *Primordial Register of Tortoise Mountain* states: Atop *Tortoise Mountain* stand *twelve jade towers*, resplendent with radiant brilliance. Within the *Grand Clarity* is the *Golden Flower Tower*, where the *jade registers of all perfected immortals* are kept within the *golden tower*.

The *Numinous Writ Scripture* states: There is the *Grotto Numinous Observation*, its four sides inscribed with *golden characters*. There is also the *Ninefold Numinous Observation* and the *Purple Yang Observation*. Within the *Purple Tenuity Upper Palace* is the *Yang-Penetrating Observation*, which governs the *weight of merits* of those who attain deliverance.

The *Scripture of the Three Primes’ Precepts* states: When the *nine qi* first congealed and the *three luminaries* shone forth, they wove together the *azure, yellow, and white qi* to establish the *Three Palaces of the Upper Prime*.

The *Great Grotto Jade Scripture* states: In the *Grand Beginning* were the *Flowery Yang Palace* and the *Assembly of Directions Palace*. Within the *Lesser Existence Perfected Heaven* is the *Myriad Flower Palace*, the seat of the *Jade Lord’s* governance. Within the *Jade Dawn Palace* is the *Jade Reflection Palace*. There are also the *Six Abysms Palace of the Primal Sovereign*, the *Yellow Elder Round Flower Palace*, the *Upper Clarity Perfected Yang Palace*, and the *Grand Ultimate Upper Palace*, which presides over the *hymns and chants of all immortals*.

The *Great Grotto Jade Scripture* states: Within the *Grand Radiance* is the *White Cloud Chamber*, the dwelling of the *Grand Void Primal Sovereign*.

The *Scriptures of the Three Sovereigns* states: In the *stone chamber* west of *Mount Emei* in *Shu Commandery* was once kept the *Writ of the Three Sovereigns*. This writ is not like the common texts of the world; among a million people, not one has obtained it.

The *Primordial Register of Tortoise Mountain* states: There is the *Jasper Jade Chamber*.

The *Scripture of the Released Grades of Foreign Lands* states: There is the *Jasper Flower Chamber*.

The *Golden Mystery Scripture of Grotto Radiance* states: The *Eight Jasper Chamber*.

The *Upper Scripture of the Three Flowered Treasure Radiance* states: The *Jade Chamber of the Upper Clarity Scriptures* contains the *Azure Chamber*.

The *Great Grotto Jade Scripture* states: The *Three-Flowered City* is the name of a *chamber* in *Jade Purity*, situated within the *Jade City*, the dwelling of the *Yang Peace Primal Sovereign*.

The *Inner Transmission of the Supreme Perfected* states: There is the *Nine-Colored Flowing Cloud Chamber*.

The *Inner Transmission of the Immortal Duke* states: Atop *Kunlun Mountain* is the *Piled Stone Jasper Chamber*.

The *Purple Writ of the Supreme* states: The *White Jade Mother* entered the *Tortoise Mountain Kingly Gate* and dwelled within the *Vermilion Purple Chamber* of the *Azure Jade Palace*.

The *Numinous Treasure Red Writ* states: There is the *Ninefold Radiant Flower Chamber*.

The *Scripture of the Released Grades of Foreign Lands* states: The *Purple Jasper Vermilion Chamber*.

The *Daoist Canon* states: That which purifies the *Dao* in the present is my *abode*. The *Dao* purifies itself in accordance with *Heaven’s* clarity, stills itself in accordance with *Earth’s* tranquility, illuminates itself in accordance with the *light of the sun and moon*, rectifies itself in accordance with the *movements of the stars and constellations*, and harmonizes the *natures of the myriad things* through their *growth and decline*. Among the myriad things, humans are the most noble, capable of rendering the *form* untroubled and the *spirit* formless, thereby employing *clarity* to achieve the *intent of non-action*—this is the *abode of the Dao*.

The *Scripture of the Inner Sounds of the Heavens* states: The *Heavenly Perfected August Person* opens the *Frigid Numinous Window*. It further states: The *Mysterious Window of the Southern Culmen* governs the *oral refinement and ocular tapping* of all those who attain the *Dao*.

The *Scripture of the Inner Sounds of the Heavens* states: The *Ninefold Mysterious Venerable* is sealed within the *Purple Portal* of the *Jade Capital*.

The *Golden Mystery Scripture of Grotto Radiance* states: There is the *Jade Portal*.

The *Great Grotto Jade Scripture* states: The *Grand Simplicity* lies above the *Profound Mystery*, where the *Nine Palaces* array the *Golden Gates* in the *Heaven of Grand Simplicity*. The *Jasper Feather Gate* is the name of a *gate* in the *Orchid Chamber of the Upper Clarity Palace*. Above the *Grand Supreme* is the *Jasper Feather Gate*. The *Fourfold Luminous Gate* is the *southern gate* of the *Jade Emperor of the Upper Clarity*.

The *Purple Writ of the Golden Root* states: The *Eastern Flower Square Pond Azure Lad Palace* has *six gates*, each enclosing a circumference of *three thousand li*. To the east is the *Azure Flower Gate*, to the west the *Jade Grotto Gate*, to the north the *Jasper Gate*, to the northeast the *Frigid Water Gate*, and to the southeast the *Heavenly Pass Gate*.

The *Scripture of the Two Ways’ Sequential Practice* states: Below the *Grotto Yang Palace* is the *Flowing Fire Courtyard*.

The *Great Grotto Jade Scripture* states: Within the *Vast Cold Palace* is the *Cold Courtyard*, the dwelling of the *Grand Unity*. There is also the *Cloud Pearl Courtyard*.

The *Perfected Writ of the Supreme* states: The *Celestial Thearch* attends the *perfected* in the *Golden Lad*, where *misty incense wafts through the Purple Courtyard*.

The *Twenty-Four Birth Charts* states: The *Primordial Beginning* spread out *five-colored gold* to form the *altar*.

The *Jade Emperor’s Genealogical Register* states: The *Venerable of the Primordial Beginning* ascended the *Jade Void Altar* to receive the *Upper August Treasure Scripture of the Nine Heavens’ Genealogical Register*, the *Jade Talismans*, and the *Secret Chapters*.

**Palaces**

The *Primary Record of Mount Gui* states: The *Venerable of the Primordial Beginning* resides in the *Upper Clarity Jade Heaven Palace*, the *Great Clarity Palace*, the *Opening Clarity Palace*, the *Jade Treasure Grotto Origin Palace*, the *Golden Fusion Palace*, the *Cinnabar Radiance Palace*, the *Double Darkness Palace*, and the *Phoenix Birth Palace*.

---

**Transmission and Reception (Part One)**

The *Scripture of the True Forms of the Five Peaks* states: If a Daoist obtains a scripture of secret sagely teachings, they must not conceal it within the mouth of a single person. Should the texts of true numina be allowed to perish through solitary witness, by what means could they endure for eternal generations? Transmission must be entrusted only to the worthy. How could one hoard and withhold them, thus forever obscuring these writings?

The *Scripture of the Supreme Ultimate* states: The *Jade Scripture of the Supreme* contains hidden annotations and precious oral instructions—it is the progenitor of all scriptures. The Supreme commanded that it be transmitted to the lords, dukes, ministers, and counts of the Supreme Ultimate. Those who have not attained such rank may not receive it. If a Daoist encounters this book, they are destined to become a *Celestial Duke*. Their name is predestined in the *Mysterious Register*.

The *Scripture of the Numinous Treasure and True Unity* states: The *Grand Numinous Perfected* addressed the *Celestial Duke of the Left Palace of the Supreme Ultimate*, saying: "Long ago, I transmitted the *Upper Treasure Scripture of the Numinous Treasure’s Grotto Mystery and Natural Perfection* to the *Perfected of the Supreme Ultimate*, who, in accordance with the Supreme’s method, passed it on to others."

The *Scripture of Resolute Will* states: The *Primordial Beginning* instructed the *Perfected of the Right Mysterious Unity*, saying: "You may transmit this scripture only after selecting the worthy. Disseminate it boundlessly without exclusion."

The *Scripture of the Three Sovereigns* states: Among a million people, perhaps one is fated to receive this text—all such recipients have predestined records of immortality. When seeking someone to transmit it to, one must choose carefully, entering the famous mountains and traversing the eight directions. Then, no ghost or spirit in the world will dare to violate them.

The *Queen Mother of the Primordial Beginning in the Heavenly Center of Great Clarity* is the first teacher of those who study the Dao.

It further states: The *August Person* is the emissary of the *Supreme Thearch*, dwelling on Mount Emei. The *Yellow Thearch* went there to receive the *True Unity and Five Molar Methods*.

The *Master Embracing Simplicity* states: The *Yellow Thearch* traveled east to *Green Hill*, passing *Wind Mountain*, where he met the *Master of the Purple Palace* and received the *Inner Text of the Three Sovereigns*, by which he summoned the myriad spirits. He journeyed south to *Round Canopy*, where he observed the *Hundred Numinous Ones* at the *Tree of Construction*. He went west to *Middle Yellow Master* and received the *Ninefold Augmentation Method*. Passing *Kongtong*, he studied the *Scripture of the Natural* under *Master Broad Accomplishment*. He traveled north to *Hongti* and *Juci*, where he met *Great Lord Jun* and the *Yellow Canopy Youth*, receiving the *Divine Mushroom Chart*. Returning, he reached *Wangwu Mountain* and obtained the *Divine Elixir Annotations*. At *Mount Emei*, he encountered the *Yellow Person* in the *Jade Hall* and inquired about the *Way of True Unity*, saying: "The methods for long life and immortality rely solely on *golden liquid*, while preserving form and repelling evil depends only on *True Unity*. The ancients prized this Way above all."

The *Yellow Thearch* was one who naturally embodied the Dao, yet he still journeyed to *Wangwu* to receive the *Elixir Scripture*, ascended *Kongtong* to consult *Broad Accomplishment*, went to *Juci* to serve *Great Hidden*, traveled to *Eastern Peak* to honor *Middle Yellow*, entered *Golden Valley* to seek *Master Xin*, discussed the cultivation of the Way with *Xuan Su*, refined his calculations with *Lei Qi*, exhausted the records of spirits and demons with *White Marsh*, surveyed geography with *Green Crow*, and mended wounds with *Golden Cold*. Thus, he mastered all essential secrets and fully penetrated the truth of the Dao.

According to the *Scripture of Divine Immortals*: Long ago, the *Yellow Thearch* and *Laozi* served *Original Lord*, who imparted to them essential instructions. Without the guidance of these two lords, how could they have attained transcendence and delivered the world?

The *Scripture of Mount Ke* and the *Record of the Dragon’s Head* both state that the *Yellow Thearch* ingested divine elixirs. It further says: *Peng Zu* lived eight hundred years, and *Anqi* a thousand—such longevity far surpasses ordinary people. If there truly exists a Way of undying, why did they not ascend as immortals? Is it not simply that their allotted lifespan and received qi happened to be abundant?

The *Scripture of Peng Zu* states: He assisted *Yao*, served through the *Xia* dynasty, and became a minister under the *Shang*. The *Shang* king sought his method for extending years, and when it proved effective, desired to kill *Peng Zu* to eradicate the technique. Sensing this, *Peng Zu* fled. At the time of his departure, he was eight hundred years old.

Moreover, it is said: The *Jade Flying Heavenly Writ of the Purple Tenuity Mysterious Palace* was bestowed by the Grand Primordial upon the Queen Mother of the West, who wore it at her waist and ascended to the rank of Immortal Ancestor, attended by perfected beings.

It further says: The *Myriad Immortals’ Writ of the Mysterious Continent’s Immortal Lord* was conferred by the Youth of the Eastern Sea upon those who attain the Dao, to be worn at the waist. It is also called the *Register of the Immortal’s Way* or the *Phoenix Perfected’s Thread of the Grand Mystery’s Ascension Covenant*.

Moreover, the *Numinous Flying Perfected Writ of the Kunlun Pond Terrace* was transmitted by the Grand Supreme Elder to those who attain the Dao, to be worn at the waist. They traverse the Five Marchmounts, where the mountain spirits confer office upon them. It is also called the *Five Marchmounts’ Military Tallies*—when worn, metal and stone open before them.

It further says: When the *Supreme Perfected Writ of Penglai* was completed, the August Emperor of the Azure Heavens transmitted it to Ning Feng. Those who wear this true tally traverse rivers and seas without hindrance. It is also called the *Penglai Grand Mystery Jade Tablet* or the *Nine Streams’ Perfected Writ*, which the Literary Master of Beiling transmitted to Ma Shihuang to summon dragons.

Moreover, the *Yellow Supreme Perfected Writ of the Celestial Thearch’s Literary Master*, when worn at the waist, reveals omens of fortune and misfortune before they manifest.

The *Scripture of Supreme Purity* states: The Perfected of Supreme Purity ascended Mount Canglang of the Great Thearch, where the Perfected of the Grand Ultimate bestowed upon them the *Cinnabar and Azure Jade Crucible* and the *Scripture of Refining Cloud Root*.

The *Scripture of the Three Primes’ Array* says: Formerly, Ning Xuanshu received this scripture from the August Supreme Perfected and concealed it for nine years in White Void Mountain. After a hundred days of purification, he suddenly saw upon the cliff a silver tablet inscribed with the Kingly Script. One copy remains sealed in White Void Mountain.

The *Scripture of Fundamental Conduct* states: The Cinnabar Numinous Perfected encountered Master Xuanhe and received the *Vermilion Writ of the Numinous Treasure*, the *Mysterious Writ of the Five Qi*, and one chapter of the *Perfected Writ of the Black Thearch*.

The *Scripture of the Lofty Mystery* says: Formerly, the Supreme Prime transmitted the *Hidden Writ* to the Jade Maiden of Grand Harmony, who in turn bestowed it upon the Lord of Young Yang. The text was sealed in the grotto-chamber of Mount Jiuyi.

The *Concealed Instructions for Ascending Perfection* states: The *Precious Chapters of the Grand Ultimate Thearch* were conferred by the Azure Youth of the Eastern Sea upon Juanzi, who sealed them in the palm of a famous mountain. Juanzi obtained them by splitting open a carp—these are the *Three Ones Guarding the Form*, commanded by the Most High. Written in cinnabar upon white silk and worn at the left elbow, they must not be exposed to defilement. After eight years of wearing them, the Three Ones will all manifest. The Three Ones are the Three Prime Perfected Lords of Unity. They transmit the teaching of sealing within the palm.

It further says: Li Yi, styled Zhongfu, transmitted the *Seven Transformations Method* to Zuo Ci. Ci cultivated it and achieved myriad transformations. This scripture appears in the *Biography of Perfected Lord Mao*, but later Daoists, regarding the *Returning Cinnabar Method* as exceedingly secret, extracted it and made it a separate scroll.

The *Biography of Lord Mao* states: The Primordial Perfected of the Grand Supreme, the Queen Mother of the West, bestowed and expounded the *Scripture of the Mysterious Perfected of the Luminous Hall*, saying: *The Most High established the Dual Mystery and the Fourfold Radiance. The Mysterious Perfected shines within, the Luminous Hall is pure without. Inhaling the twin luminances, one’s spirit attains long life. Above, one assists the Controller of Destinies, overseeing the numinous powers of the directions. The Sixfold Effulgences overflow, scattering the gaze of the Yellow and Tranquil.* These forty characters are the fundamental scripture of the Mysterious Perfected. Later, the Queen Mother of the West, the Perfected of Totality, further elaborated the methods of practice, just as the *Central Scripture of the Nine Perfected* takes the Dragon Script as its essence. The Most High inscribed it upon the southern pavilion of Phoenix Terrace. It is not taught to those who are not disciples of the Perfected of Totality, nor transmitted to those who are not the select of the Controller of Destinies.

It further says: The Queen Mother of the West brought Lord Mao Ying to the Palace of Solid Integrity. Solid Integrity was the second younger brother of Ying. The Queen Mother patted his back and said: *Though your Dao is accomplished, what you have heard is not yet sufficient. I have something to bestow upon you.* She then dispatched her attendant, Guo Mixiang, to convey a message to the Lady of the Supreme Prime, saying: *Though we have not met for over four thousand years, the affairs of heaven have wearied me, leaving little time for visitation. Might you come briefly? I shall await you here.*

The Lady of the Supreme Prime sent an attendant to reply: *Ahuan bows and inquires after your well-being. Separated by the Crimson River and burdened by official duties, I have not seen your face for nearly five thousand years. Yearning for your radiance, my heart remains ever bound to you.* When Mixiang arrived and delivered the message, the Lady of the Supreme Prime prepared her carriage. First, she was received by the Lord of Grand Constancy, who sent her to the Grove of Aspiration to collate the registers of the Three Primes and verify them. She would depart only briefly, then return. Upon returning, she would proceed eastward, hoping to tarry a while.

Mao Gu thereupon asked the Queen Mother: *May I inquire who the Lady of the Supreme Prime is?* The Queen Mother replied: *She is the Mother of the Perfected August Ones of the Three Heavens, the Supreme Perfected of the Supreme Prime, who governs the rosters of jade maidens throughout the ten directions.*

When the Lady of the Supreme Prime arrived, the sound of pipes and drums was heard in the clouds, and the neighing of dragon-horses. Upon her descent, her retinue was vast, all women, uniformly sixteen or seventeen years old, their countenances luminous and transcendent. Many wore garments of azure damask, their brilliance dazzling. The Lady of the Supreme Prime was not yet thirty, her celestial beauty unmatched. She wore a robe of crimson frost and a cloak of azure brocade. Her hair was arranged in a triple chignon, the rest cascading to her waist. She wore a crown of the Nine Dawns and the Moon at Night, and pendants of the Six Mountains’ Fiery Algae. She trailed a grand sash of phoenix-patterned jade brilliance and wielded the *Flowing Yellow Waving Essence Sword*. Entering the chamber, she bowed to the Queen Mother, who sat and bade her rise, sharing a seat facing north.

The Lady of the Supreme Prime prepared a feast, and the Lord of the Kings urged Mao Ying’s two younger brothers to partake. Guzhong rose to bow, prostrating himself and standing. She commanded him to sit and resume his place. The Lady of the Supreme Prime then ordered her attendant to bring forth a purple brocade pouch and open a casket of green gold, from which she transmitted to Guzhong the *Scripture of the Flowing Pearls of the Three Primes*, the *Scripture of the Cinnabar Radiance and Dao Essence*, the *Scripture of the Eight Arts of Concealing the Earth*, and the *Scripture of the Green Radiance of the Grand Ultimate*—four scriptures in all.

The Queen Mother of the West commanded her attendant, Li Fangming, to bring forth a case of cinnabar jade and open a casket of cloud pearls, from which she transmitted to the Controller of Destinies, Lord Mao, the *Hidden Book of the Grand Empyrean* and the *Inner True Tallies of the Two Luminances of Cavernous Flight*.

The Lady of the Supreme Prime said: *Mother’s hidden writings are wondrous—cherished by the Heavenly Immortals of the Supreme Perfected as inner scriptures. Sealed in golden terraces, they are worn when entering the Grand Tenuity. In motion, one rides the jade chariot of the Eight Radiant Sceneries; at rest, one reposes in the golden hall.*

This text is wondrous indeed. The *Grand Ultimate Scripture of Green Radiance* and its counterparts can summon the Bright Moon and Yellow Blossoms, attaining the Crimson Essence of the White Sun.

When the Queen Mother of the West and the Lady of the Supreme Prime both departed, only Lord Wang remained for a full day. Thereupon, Mao Ying bid farewell to his two younger brothers and left with Lord Wang, arriving at the Jade Cavern Prefecture of Red City. He addressed his brothers, saying: "I now depart to assume my duties and shall not be able to visit you frequently. Mount Juqu is your administrative seat."

In the seventh year of *Jianwu* during the reign of Emperor Guangwu of Han (31 CE), on the *dingsi* day of the third month, an emissary named Wu Lun was dispatched bearing fifty *jin* of yellow gold, which was placed beneath the shrine of the Three Lords Mao. Sacrifices of the grandest offering were made there in all four seasons. By the second year of *Yongping* during the reign of Emperor Ming (59 CE), the shrine of the Perfected Mao of Juqu in Danyang’s Jurong was ordered to be maintained and guarded. At that time, the locals commonly referred to this shrine as the White Crane Temple.

The Cavern Palace of Mount Juqu has five gates: the winding stone steps of the mountain are shaped by water, and these gates permit passage for ascent and descent. The grotto-heaven of Mount Juqu connects eastward to the Forest Chamber, northward to Mount Tai, westward to Mount Emei, and southward to Mount Luofu—all great Daoist thoroughfares. Among them, lesser paths, new trails, and winding sandbars are too numerous to count.

At the end of the *Jian’an* era (220 CE), Zuo Ci heard of this mountain in the region east of the Yangzi and thus sought it out. After three months of purification and fasting, he ascended the mountain, found its gate, and entered the Cavern’s Void to reach the Yin Palace. The Two Lords Mao bestowed upon him three kinds of divine mushrooms. Zuo Ci wandered the cavern chambers for a year, where the regulations were most solemn. He sighed, saying: "I never imagined the world could hold such marvels!"

Among the grotto-heavens beneath the earth, there are thirty-six in all, including Wangwu, Weiyu, Xicheng, Xixuan, Qingcheng, Chicheng, Luofu, Juqu, Linwu, Kuocang, Kunlun, Penglai, Yingzhou, Fangzhang, Canglang, Baishan, and the Eight Stops—all such places. The Five Marchmounts and other renowned mountains each possess cavern chambers, some thirty *li*, twenty *li*, or ten *li* in extent, while the cavern of a marchmount spans a hundred *li*.

Mount Juqu was known in Qin times as Mount Ju Jintan, for within its grotto-heaven stood a hundred-*zhang* golden altar, whence its name derived. During the reign of Emperor Ling of Han, the prefectures and counties were ordered to mine the gold of Mount Juqu to fill the imperial armories. In the time of Sun Quan, guardsmen were again dispatched to mine gold, which was regularly delivered to the court.

On the eighteenth day of the third month and the second day of the twelfth month each year, the Eastern Minister of Destinies, Lord Mao, convenes on Mount Juqu with the Jade Lord of the Assembly of Perfected Ones, the Great Void Perfected, and the Azure Lad of the Eastern Sea. Those who seek the Way of immortality should first purify themselves through fasting and await these days to ascend the mountain and present their entreaties. Lord Mao will then transmit the essential Dao, allowing them to enter the cavern gate.

It is further said: The Purple Tenuity, Primordial Numinous, White Jade, Tortoise Terrace, Nine Numinous, Supreme Perfected, and Primordial Lady—these are the Queen Mother of the West. The Supreme Minister of the Assembly of Perfected Ones, Lord Wang, is the teacher of the Eastern Minister of Destinies, Lord Mao, and the mother of the Right Canopy, the Lady of Purple Tenuity. She dwells in the Pond Terrace of Kunlun, governing separately from the Azure Forest Palace of White Jade Tortoise Mountain. Her chambers are crimson and purple; she wears a flowered coronet and a tiger-patterned sash. Her canopy is adorned with layered feathers, and her banners bear the *yin* and *ting* emblems. During the reign of Emperor Ping of Han, she descended to the Floriate Yang Palace of Mount Juqu and bestowed upon the Minister of Destinies, Lord Mao, the jade pendants, golden earrings, and scriptures. She also instructed the two younger Lords Mao.

By the time of Emperor Cheng of Jin, she descended together with the Golden Watchtower Sage Lord to the Hidden Primordial Terrace of Yangluo, where she transmitted to Lady Wei the four scrolls of the *Jade Purity Hidden Writings*. The accounts in the *Biography of King Mu* of his visit to the Queen Mother of the West and her descent to Emperor Wu of Han all refer to her. There is a separate transmission titled the *Numinous Mirror Cavern Mystery Supreme Scripture*, also called the *Great Possession Wondrous Scripture*—the very text now held by the Assistant Minister of the Middle Prime. It has not yet been revealed to the world and serves to instruct all those who study the true Way.

It is further said: The Supreme Perfected Lord of the Western Ultimate is the teacher of the Minister of Destinies, Lord Mao. Born at the end of the Shang dynasty, he consumed the Azure Essence *qi*-infused grain and the nine-times-cycled elixir, employing the Way of the Dawn Sword and Liberation to govern the Western City Mountain Palace. At the age of thirty, he donned embroidered robes, a hibiscus coronet, and carried a bell and a single sword. During the reign of Emperor Yuan of Han, he descended to Mount Yangluo and transmitted the thirty-one scrolls of the *Jade Purity Void Supreme Scripture*. In the Jin dynasty, he again descended to the Yangluo Terrace to instruct Lady Wei. Every third and twelfth month, he likewise comes to Mount Juqu to review and examine the studies of transcendents. There is a separate transmission concerning him, though it has not yet been revealed to the world. The *Biographies of Divine Transcendents* recounts his descent to the household of Cai Jing—this refers to this very lord.

It is further said: The Perfected Lord of Pure Emptiness, a disciple of the Supreme Perfected Lord Wang, was the teacher of Lady Wei of the Southern Marchmount. During the reign of Emperor Yuan of Han, he left his family and entered Mount Huayin. After nine years, the Perfected Lord of the Grand Ultimate descended to transmit two methods. Later, he entered Mount Difei (also called Mount Zhongnan) and ascended Mount Yangluo. During the reign of Emperor Ping, the Southern Ultimate Lady and the Western City Lord Wang descended together to transmit thirty-one scrolls of the supreme scriptures. Lord Wang then journeyed with him to the Dark Continent to request his true name. Returning to the Western City, he cultivated the Way to completion. Thereupon, he rode a flying maple chariot to travel throughout the world. Later, he ascended White Void Mountain and visited the Three Primordial Lords of Purple Purity and Grand Simplicity, receiving the *Flowing Gold*, *Fire Bell*, *Expansive*, *Seven Primes*, *Eight Sceneries*, *Flying Dawn*, *Divine Strategem*, and *Jade Seal* scriptures in full. He then returned to the Western City.

The Supreme Lord sent gifts: a feathered dawn canopy, a pair of luminous moon pearls, a jade-staffed white feather banner, and a cinnabar-embroidered brocade standard. The Grand Simplicity further dispatched a decree bearing the completed mandate, appointing him the Perfected Lord of Pure Emptiness of Grand Simplicity, to govern Mount Jade House and oversee the treasury of sacred scriptures. He rides a tiger-drawn chariot with a golden canopy and jade wheels, an Eight Scenery flying carriage, and bears a nine-colored staff. He enters and exits the Supreme Purity, serves the Grand Simplicity, and reposes in the Grand Ultimate. Lady Wei of the Southern Marchmount was his disciple, and his transmission has been made manifest in the world.

*The Inner Transmission of Lady Wei of the Southern Marchmount* states:

Lady Wei bore the surname Wei, her personal name was Huacun, her courtesy name Xian’an. She was a native of Rencheng and the daughter of Wei Shu, the Duke Wenkang and Minister of Education of the Jin. From youth, she studied the *Laozi* and *Zhuangzi*, the *Three Commentaries on the Spring and Autumn Annals*, the *Five Classics*, and the writings of the Hundred Masters. She often resided alone in a separate garden, dwelling in quietude, and consumed sesame seeds. Her parents compelled her to marry Liu Youyan, the clerk of the Grand Protector of Nanyan. Yet her long-held aspirations remained steadfast and unbroken.

Later, when Youyan became magistrate of Xiuwu, she followed him to the county residence. There, she secluded herself in a separate chamber for a hundred days, awaiting the advent of the immortals. On a midwinter night at midnight, four perfected beings descended into her chamber: the Perfected Lord of the Grand Ultimate, An Duming; the Lord of Eastern Florescence, the Azure Lad; the Perfected of Azure Sea and Scenic Forest; and the Perfected Lord of Pure Emptiness, Wang Zideng.

Thereupon, Lady Wei bowed and entreated them for the Way of long life and deliverance from the world. The Azure Lad said, “This Perfected Lord of Pure Emptiness shall be your master; you must receive his teachings.” The Perfected of Scenic Forest declared, “You are destined to become the Primordial Lady of Purple Emptiness, a Perfected Controller of Destiny and Lady of the Southern Marchmount.” Lady Wei replied, “This humble servant is most fortunate to receive such a mandate of life.”

When she had finished speaking, the Lad of Eastern Florescence pointed and laughed, saying, “How bitterly earnest is your cinnabar heart!” Then the Perfected Lord Wang commanded his attendants, Hua Santiao and Li Mingci, to part the cloud-woven curtains, open the jade caskets, and bring forth the *Precious Writings of the Supreme Lord*, the *Eight Hidden Scriptures*, the *Perfect Writ of the Great Cavern*, the *Eight Daoist Writings of the Numinous Book*, the *Purple Radiance of Scorching Flame*, the *Stone Essence and Jade Steed*, the *Tiger Script of the Divine Perfected*, and the *Thirty-One Scrolls of the Lofty Immortal and Feathered Mystery*—all of which he personally bestowed upon Lady Wei.

Lord Wang had once studied the Dao on Mount Yangluo, where he encountered the Lady of the Southern Culmen and Lord Wang of the Western City, who transmitted to him these thirty-one scrolls. Through their practice, he attained perfection. What he now transmitted was the original scripture of the Southern Culmen and Western City. On Mount Yangluo stands the Terrace of Repose, a secondary palace of the Perfected of Pure Emptiness.
