As Lord Wang bestowed the scriptures upon Lady Wei, he rose, faced north, and swore an oath: “By the Supreme Three Mysteries, the Nine August High Perfected, and the Supreme Emperor, the Supreme Emperor commands that I, Wang, instruct Wei Huacun herein.”

The Perfected of Scenic Forest further transmitted to Lady Wei the *Scripture of the Inner Radiance of the Yellow Court*, also called *The Supreme Lord’s Zither Heart*, *The Golden Book of the Great Emperor*, and *The Jade Chapters of Eastern Florescence*, instructing her to recite it day and night. Lord Wang admonished her, saying, “If you do not conceal yourself in the mountains, fast, and maintain purity, you must not recklessly recite the *Perfect Writ of the Great Cavern*. As for the *Tiger Script*, the *Dragon Writings*, the *Eight Hidden Writings of the Primordial Simplicity*, and other arcane and profound mysteries—without fasting and severing worldly ties, they cannot be practiced. For now, you may recite the *Scripture of the Inner Radiance of the Yellow Court*, tread the steps of the Seven Primes, and visualize the spirits of the Five Stars. If others practice these, it will suffice to evoke transformations and resonances. When the time comes for your ascension, I shall come to receive you.”

The Azure Lad of the Square Cauldron remained joyfully, briefly tarrying to chant with the Four Perfected. Then he commanded Song Lianjuan, the Jade Maiden of the Northern Frigid Realm, to pluck the *Hymn of the Nine Qi*; Yan Jingzhu, the Jade Maiden of Eastern Florescence, to strike the bell of the Western Fullness; Jia Quting, the Jade Maiden of Cloudy Groves, to blow the phoenix-repelling flute; and Xianyu Lingjin, the Jade Maiden of Soaring Mystery, to tap the jade baton of the Nine Harmonies.

Lord Wang then said to Lady Wei, “The essential instructions are now complete.” With that, he took his leave.

Lady Wei cultivated stillness and advanced daily. She lived in the world for eighty-three years. In the ninth year of Xianhe under Emperor Cheng of Jin, when Lord Wang and the Azure Lad of Eastern Florescence descended, the year was jiawu. The two Perfected Ones gave Lady Wei elixirs: the *Divine Powder of Hidden Transcendence from White Medicine River*, and the *Spirit Pill of Stone Essence and Golden Radiance for Transforming Form*. They instructed her to feign illness and withdraw, setting a fixed date to meet at the Yangluo Palace.

After speaking, the two Perfected Ones departed. Lady Wei immediately ingested the elixirs, then claimed a foot ailment, closed her eyes, and rested, drinking but not eating. On the seventh day, after midnight, the Supreme Unity Transcendent Immortal dispatched a cloud chariot to receive her, driving through the qi and entering her bedchamber. At that time, her disciples attended her illness, and her kin filled the room, yet none perceived it. Lady Wei then employed the method of *Concealing Radiance*, entrusting her form to sword transformation. She slowly ascended the cloud carriage and proceeded directly to Yangluo.

Dwelling in the Hidden Origin Terrace, her will governed the Upper Prime. Her sincerity moved the Nine Heavens; her cinnabar heart truly aligned. Clarifying her spirit, the Lady of Supreme Simplicity then journeyed north to the Palace of Supreme Purity. The Celestial Emperor of the Grand Tenuity dispatched Li Mingqi, the Jade Prime Attendant of the Nine Palaces, to confer upon her the *Divine Phoenix Writs* and command her to seal the mountains. The Yellow Venerable Lord of the Central Clouds sent Hou Gongyangzi, the Feathered Dawn Attendant of the Orthodox Unity, to bestow upon her the *Dragon Robe and Tiger Belt*, the *Cinnabar and Azure Flying Skirt*, and the *Ten Absolute Floral Banners*, enabling her to ascend to the Supreme Purity and assume the true destiny of transcendence.

The Lofty Lady of the Three Simplicities sent Fan Dingying, the Lady of the Ninefold Left Florescence, to present her with the *Flowing Gold Fire Bell* and the *Nine-Canopied Cloud Chariot*, empowering her to subdue the demons of all directions. The Great Dao Lord of the Jade Dawn of the Supreme Void and Grand Mystery dispatched Meng Liuqi, the Embroidered Robe Messenger, to grant her the *Nine-Colored Baton*, the *Twin Pearl Moonlight*, the *Divine Tiger Talisman*, and the *Broidered Tiger Banner*, appointing her to command the host of spirits and overawe the Six Heavens.

The Lady of the Three Primes of Supreme Simplicity sent Zhong Wenjian, the Guardian of the Divine Capital, and Zhao Yueluo, the Right Consort Yuanji, to confer upon her the *Three Hundred Jade Maidens of the Western Florescence*, the *Eight Radiant Flying Chariots*, and the *Nine Dark Dragons of Mystic Radiance*, ordering them to attend and hold her towels as she ascended to the Three Clarities.

The Grand Thearch of Fusang dispatched Ke Yanshou, the Eight Mystery Immortal Earl, and the Celestial Thearchs of the Five Directions, led by Jian Suzhi, to bestow upon her the *Jade Tablet and Golden Script*, appointing her as the Purple Void Primordial Lady, overseer of the life registers of all who cultivate the Dao, and mistress of the offices that govern fate, examine sins, and inspect the Golden Pass.

Later, the Sage Lord commanded the Immortal Earl Ya Shuping to present her with the *Azure Jade Tablet* inscribed in cinnabar and green, appointing her as the Lady of the Southern Marchmount, equal in rank to the Transcendent Dukes. She was granted a *Curved Dawn Flying Canopy* to traverse the Nine Palaces and charged with governing the Great Mount Tiantai within the Terrace of Huo, instructing those below who uphold the Dao and teaching those destined to become true transcendents. She was ordered to ascend the Jade Purity twice monthly, the Supreme Simplicity thrice, and the Jade Dawn Palace and Fusang’s Lofty Terrace four times.

Thereupon, Lady Wei received the Queen Mother’s mandate and returned to the midst of Mount Wangwu’s Lesser Existence. She further purified herself for three months. The Primordial Lady of the Nine Subtleties, the Queen Mother of Tortoise Mountain, the Perfected Wang Fangping of the Western City, the Grand Void Perfected Red Pine, and the Perfected Wang Ziqiao of Paulownia and Cypress all descended to the Crimson Chamber of the Pure Void Upper Palace in Lesser Existence. Each commanded their attendant maidens to strike gold and stone instruments.

Then the Queen Mother of the West rose and paced, bowing as she chanted:
*“Alas, this parting and meeting,
When kalpas end and heaven and earth collapse.
Within the Crimson Mound’s embrace,
Together we rejoice without end.”*

As the song concluded, the registrar of destinies, the host of transcendents, and the welcoming officials of the Southern Marchmount arrived. The Queen Mother and the others departed with Lady Wei for the Terrace of Mount Tiantai and Huo.

The *Esoteric Instructions on Ascending Perfection* states: *The Golden Tiger Talisman of the Celestial Emperor of the Grand Tenuity*. The Supreme Jade Perfected Lord of Imperial Dao bestowed it upon the Celestial Emperor of the Grand Tenuity. It also states: *The Jade Seal and Golden True Tiger Talisman of the Supreme Unity*. Lady Li of the Illustrious Terrace governed the Terrace of Fangzhang, dwelling in the thirteenth vermilion pavilion, and descended during the Xingning era of Jin. Lord Yang dragged a purple brocade robe, bearing the *Divine Tiger Talisman* and *Flowing Gold Bell*, with a green jade-colored sash. He had two attendant maidens, each about twenty years old, clad in green damask. One attendant, named Yinhui, held two vermilion jade boxes bound with green cords and jade seals. The inscriptions read: *Supreme Writs* and *Supreme Scripts*. Thereafter, he descended frequently, bestowing books and composing poems.

The *Records of Immortal Gatherings* states: The Crone of Mount Li, of unknown era, once encountered Li Quan, who was fond of the Dao of transcendents and often traversed famous mountains, broadly collecting esoteric arts. In a stone chamber on Mount Song, he obtained a silk scroll of the *Yellow Emperor’s Scripture of the Hidden Talisman*, sealed most securely, inscribed: *“On the seventh day of the seventh month in the second year of Taihe under the Great Wei, the Daoist Kou Qianzhi concealed this in the famous mountains to transmit to those of like aspiration.”* Quan could not fathom its meaning. Journeying into Qin, at the foot of Mount Li, he encountered an old woman with a topknot, her remaining hair half-hanging, clad in tattered robes and leaning on a staff, her spirit and appearance most extraordinary. By the roadside, she saw a fire burning a tree and murmured to herself: *“Fire is born of wood; calamity arises and must be overcome.”* Quan heard this, stepped forward, and bowed, saying: *“This is the secret text of the *Yellow Emperor’s Scripture of the Hidden Talisman*.”* The crone replied: *“I have received this scripture for three kalpas and six cycles of sixty years—how does a youth like you come to know it?”* Quan prostrated himself, bowed twice, and fully recounted where he had obtained the scripture. He then entreated her to explain its profound meaning and received it in full.

Suddenly, the crone vanished.

**Section Twenty of the Daoist Canon**
**Section Twenty-One: Transmission (Part Two)**

*The Scripture of Golden Tablets and Jade Characters* states: The Yellow Emperor received from the Lad of Xiangcheng the method of the Six Steps of Ji. It further states: The Yellow Emperor, in his youth, received from the Lad the method of the Three Guiding Principles. And again: Guangcheng received from the Lad of the Eastern Central Primordial the method of the Six Offices.

*The Inner Transmission of the Primordial Beginning* states: The Most High dispatched an emissary clad in embroidered robes to convey the mandate to Yin Xi.

*The Mysterious Record of the Seven Sages of the Jade Emperor* states: The Seven Sages composed the chapters of the Supreme Mystery and entrusted them to the Five Elders.

The Lord of the Left of the Upper Realms and Immortal Capital concealed them within the Purple Elixir Jade Satchel, sealed with the Mandate-Opening Chapters. The Western Tortoise fixed the registers; the Eastern Flower verified the names.

*The Orthodox Methods of the Three Heavens* states: The sacred registers of the Numinous Records of the Most High were kept in the Palace of the Numinous Capital of the Most High, entrusted to the Lord of the Left of the Upper Realms and Immortal Capital of the Five Elders.

*The Luminous Regulations of the Four Poles* states: In the time of Emperor Yu, the Nine True Kings of the Nine Heavens descended in a chariot drawn by nine dragons to the Terrace of Pastoral Virtue, where they bestowed upon the Emperor these true writings. It further states: All who receive the precious scriptures of the Supreme Clarity must prepare their faith—faith sealed by a vow, treasuring the Dao. To receive scriptures without faith is to transgress the celestial Dao; to transmit scriptures without a covenant is to leak the celestial treasure.

*The Hidden Writings of the Jade Clarity* states: There are imperial tablets of gold and records of dark jade, by which the *Scripture of the Dark Feather and Jade* may be transmitted. The *Scripture of the Dark Feather and Jade* is entrusted to the Jade Gentleman of the Dark Feather for transmission to the Perfected of the Supreme Clarity. It further states: The transmission of the *Hidden Writings of the Jade Wisdom of the Supreme Sovereign* and the *Feather Writings of the Golden Mystery* is overseen by the Five Elders, who examine the charts, while the Great Unity observes the celestial patterns. And again: The Jade Emperor of the Supreme Sovereign commanded the True Man of the Great Elder to open the casket of pearl and produce the *Hidden Writings of the Jade Clarity* and the *Scripture of the Dark Feather and Jade*, transmitting them to the Lord Emperor of the Supreme Tenuity.

*The Twenty-Four Images of Life* states: The Celestial Emperor of the Primordial Beginning, in the Azure Grove of Long Sang, heard the August Lord proclaim to the Perfected and Sacred Spirits the profound and mysterious celestial writings of the *Numinous Treasure and Jade Mysteries*. And again: In accordance with the ancient statutes of the celestial treasuries, the *Regulations of the Palace of the Supreme True Jade Emperor of the Upper Realms* were transmitted to the Lord of the Dao, as recorded in the *Statutes of the Lady of Azure Youth*: the ancient scriptures, untransmitted for kalpas uncounted. And again: The August Lord, in the Pavilion of Harmonious Dawn, ascended the White Jade Throne, fully expounding the secret essentials and disclosing the wondrous gate.

*The Scripture of the Great Mystery* states: Laozi transmitted the scriptures, precepts, registers, and ritual instructions, saying: Place the scriptures upon a small-legged table, covering them with a silken cloth.

*The Scripture of Illuminating the Real* states: The August Lord of the Primordial Beginning expounded the *Scripture of Illuminating the Real* in the Grove of Fragrant Forest.

*The Central Scripture of the Great Clarity* states: The Dao says: Guard against selling, for I seek treasure. Guard against transmitting, for I am not the right person. Guard against concealing, for I sever my own learning. And again: *The Scripture of the Great Perfection* states: In the transmission from master to disciple, select those who above bear the marks of immortality, in the middle possess benevolence and filial piety, and below have talent, resolve, and steadfast purpose—only then transmit to them.

*The Scripture of the Supreme Perfection* states: The Most High said: To accomplish the Dao is to return to the origin, merging indistinguishably with the beginningless. Emerging beyond the Three Realms, one saves beings within the Nine Heavens. One delivers the living and those of goodness, bestowing prophecies upon the virtuous.

*The Scripture of the Dark Feather* states: Yuan Chuo inscribed golden tablets and jade tablets, transmitting them to Ge Xuan.

*The Scripture of the Golden Root* states: The Most High entrusted the *True Scripture of the Great Cavern* to the Blue Lad of the Upper Minister, who kept the registers in the Azure Palace of the Eastern Flower, transmitting them to later sages destined to become Perfected Ones. These golden tablets and jade slips emerged from the Palace of the Numinous Capital of the Most High, carved from jade into slips and bound with gold into tablets, inscribed in vermilion script and bound with vermilion cords.

*The Regulations of the Great Perfection* states: The Most High addressed Celestial Master Zhang Daoling, saying: The inner and outer methods accord with the Three Officials of Heaven, Earth, and Water—break the stone, drink the cinnabar, and swear the oath. Zhang Daoling received the mandate as Celestial Master and commanded his disciples to assist as successor masters. Ascending the Hall of the Lofty Void and mounting the Altar of the White Void, they performed the libation and memorialized the Great Unity, transmitting the oral instructions and the mandate to the successor masters, who inherited the foundation and propagated the teachings among heaven and humanity.

*The Declarations of the Perfected* states: Master Pei said: Those who recite the *True Scripture of the Great Cavern* ascend lightly. In former times, the Yellow Lord of the Center concealed this scripture, and the world knew it not. If one knows it, one guards it in secrecy and does not transmit it. And again: The Perfected of Purple Yang received from Lord Su the Dao of the Three-One and the Mysterious Elixir. And again: There was Lord Juanzi of the Northern Sea, who received the Dao of Guarding the One and the Mysterious Elixir! And again: The True Lady of the Central Attendant of the Eastern Palace received from the Perfected of the Paulownia and Cypress the Dao of the Flying Goblet and the Net of Liberation. And again: In former times, Lord Zhou studied the Dao in the mountains of Chang, cultivating his essence and thought for years. Suddenly, he saw an old man, knowing him to be a numinous being, and bowed his head to entreat the Dao. The old man produced seven scrolls of plain silk and bade him recite them. Lord Zhou departed as an immortal. And again: Zhao Shuqi studied the Dao on Mount Wangwu, often appearing among the people. He heard of a diviner in the marketplace and said: To enter the Gate of Heaven, harmonize the Three Passes, visualize the vermilion robes, and rectify Kunlun. Shuqi knew him to be a divine person and bowed, begging for the essential instructions. The man produced a book and gave it to him—*The Record of the Womb Essence*. Bowing in gratitude, Shuqi entered the mountains and recited it. Later, he compounded the divine elixir, ingested it, and ascended to heaven.

*The Inner Transmission of Lord Wang* states: Wang Zideng received from the Venerable Elder of the Most High the *Hidden Writings of the Jade Enshrouded* and the method of the Flying Elixir of Azure Yang Water. After ingesting it, he could perceive distant things, sit in disappearance, stand in vanishing, and command a host of spirits. And again: The Three Primordial Lords of the Great Simplicity dispatched the Divine Consort of the Western Flower, Zhen Youxiao, to bestow the *Writings of the Mandate’s Completion*, inscribed on plates of cloud jade with purple gold, transmitting them to Lord Wang Zideng, the later sage.

*The Arrayed Records of the Lord of the Dao* states: The Lord of the Dao commanded the Five Elders and Upper Perfected to open the Purple Elixir Jade Satchel and the cloud-brocade bag, producing the *Upper Scripture of the Numinous Writings in Purple Script* and transmitting it to the Blue Lad.

*The Eight Essentials of the Perfected Scripture* states: If one is diligent in practice, one should inscribe the teachings on medicinal slips and carve them with jade script, thereby attaining the rank of Left Perfected Lord of Highest Clarity.

*The Scripture of Ascending Mystery* records: Zhang Daoling said, "I dare not transmit this teaching in person." The Most High replied, "How can you hesitate and thus obstruct the transmission of the Dao? You must resolve your intent and never say it cannot be passed on. If in the world there is a Daoist who obtains this immortal scripture, unfolds it to the end, and recognizes its true essentials—even without a master to transmit it—they may uphold and practice it."

*The Scripture of Heavenly Admonitions* states: Ge Xuan told his disciple Zheng Yin, "The virtuous Dao I once received is what the Most High treasures. Now, as your teacher and friend, I transmit it to you. When I depart this world, there will be a lay practitioner of compassionate heart who comes to be born in my lineage. You must transmit this entire teaching to them, for the Dharma is to be passed down through the generations. You should transmit one copy in accordance with the precepts to a worthy disciple. If no such person exists, seal one copy and deposit it in the Five Marchmounts."

It further states: Liu Yi, styled Zishuo, was a man of Yingchuan known for his virtue and power. His family had long practiced benevolence, moving others to compassion, and his hidden virtue reached even the spirits. The Most High commended his intent and sent Master Horse Healer to instruct him in the Dao of long life. "I am an immortal official," the master said. "Would you follow me?" Yi replied, "I wish to receive your teaching."

Then he entered Mount Tongbo specially to transmit the Eight Arts of Concealing Earth and instructed him in ingesting the essences of the Five Stars. Later, his name was changed to Donghua, and he came to reside in the grotto, serving as the Right Supervisor of the Register Repository.

It further states: Chunyu Zhen, styled Shutong, was a native of Kuaiji. During the reign of Emperor Huan of the Han, he served as magistrate of Xu County. Fond of Daoist arts, he frequently ingested sesame and Solomon’s seal. Later, he entered Mount Wumu in Wu to live in seclusion. Someone transmitted to him the *Rainbow Radiance Elixir Canon*, and through cultivation, he attained the Dao, serving in the grotto as the Dignitary of Law Enforcement, overseeing those of sincere and virtuous practice.

It further states: Tao Jun, a native of Qiantang, served as a minor official in his youth. At the end of the Han, he entered Mount Zengcheng to study the Dao, where he encountered Dongguo Youping. Youping, a man of the Qin era, had long concealed himself in Mount Zengcheng and attained the Dao. He transmitted to Jun the arts of ingesting the Nine Essences, refining qi, aligning with the stars, and stabilizing the mind. Jun cultivated these precepts and served in the Donghua Palace as the Controller of the Northern River.

It further states: Zhang Feng, styled Gongxian, was a native of Henei. The Grand Tutor Yuan Wei often praised his lofty conduct. Later, Feng entered Mount Shan, where he met the Master of the Mountain Chart, who transmitted to him the Nine Clouds Water and the Strong Yang Refinement of Cassia. In the Donghua Palace, he became the Immortal Marquis of the Supreme Ultimate.

It further states: Xia Fu, styled Zizhi, was a native of Chenliu. From youth, he was fond of the Dao and ingested pine resin and mica. Later, he entered Mount Wu, where he received the Refinement of the Soul from the Red-Bearded Master. He also encountered the Perfected of Mount Tongbo, who transmitted to him the Yellow Water Cloud Nectar method. Having attained the Dao, he served in the grotto as the Attendant of the Bright Dawn.

It further states: Liu Kuan, styled Wenrao, of the Later Han, was fond of the Dao from his youth and served as Minister of Education and Grand Commandant. At the age of seventy-three, he encountered the Master of the Green Valley, who descended into his bedchamber and transmitted to him the Staff Liberation method. He entered Mount Taihua, practiced the Nine Breaths and qi ingestion, and was further instructed in the furnace elixir formula. Upon completing the Dao, he served in the grotto as the Supreme Master of the Youthful Beginning Repository, guiding beginning learners.

It further states: Liu Shaoweng frequently entered Mount Taihua, where he encountered the Old Man of the Western Marchmount, who transmitted to him the immortal Dao.

It further states: Huang Jinghua, daughter of the Minister of Works Huang Qiong, was instructed by Han Zhong in the Min Mountain Elixir and attained the immortal method through ingestion.

It further states: Zhao Weibo, a native of Dongjun, was fond of the Dao from his youth and studied under Master Deng E and Master Zhang. In his later years, he resided in the Central Marchmount, where he received the *Jade Pendant and Golden Earrings Canon* from Qiu Lin—a Daoist adept and wife of the Han general Lou Hong. He then practiced the Embrace of the Sun and Moon’s Radiance and ingested the Ninefold Luminous Mirror. Huang subsequently attained the Dao and served in the Huayang Realm as the Guardian of Life, overseeing the immortal registers and recording those who study the Dao. He also governed sudden rains and floods and presided over the Five Fungi, Gold, Jade, and Sacred Writings.

It further states: Zhang Xuanbin, a man of the Wei Emperor Wu’s time, encountered the Perfected Fan Ziming on Mount Shaoshi, who transmitted to him the arts of Daoist transformation and concealment of radiance. He resided on Mount Tianzhu.

The *Lingbao Canon* states: Beneath the trees of Mount Jialuo, three heavenly beings expounded the *Primal Yang Canon*.

The *Mingzhen Regulations* states: The Most High Lord of the Primordial Beginning, in the Fragrant Grove Garden, taught and transformed all dharmas to the assembly.

The *Inner Tone Jade Scriptures* states: The Great Brahma concealed his words from the Queen Mother of the West. In the first year of the Supreme August, on the bingwu day of the seventh month, he taught them in the grotto chamber and transmitted them to the Perfected of Pure Emptiness, Lord Wang, who passed them to Yu the Great. The texts were sealed in a stone coffer in the Southern Floating Grotto Chamber. Thus, the *Five Talismans Canon* says: "The numinous writings of the Nine Heavens remain sealed in the stone coffer."

The *Jade Instructions, Lower Scroll* states: The Five Elder Perfected sealed and inscribed jade coffers—this is another such example.

The *Kong Lingfu* states: South of Mount Kuaiji lies Mount Wanwei, atop which stands a stone cliff locally called the Stone Coffer. Its sheer walls rise into the clouds, and one must ascend by ladder to reach it. In ancient times, when Yu was regulating the floodwaters and his work was not yet complete, he fasted at this mountain. Opening the stone coffer, he obtained golden tablets and jade script, through which he understood the configuration of mountains and rivers. Thereupon, he dredged and guided the hundred rivers, each according to its proper course.

The *Shangqing Canon* states: The Primordial Celestial Emperor and the Supreme Pole Lord of the Southern Culmen ascended the Jade Terrace of the Great Void. The Five Elder Perfected and the Immortal Capital opened the bamboo chest of the Fragrant Grove and the cloud-brocade satchel, transmitting the seventy-four methods of the *Shangqing* for transformation and dissolution of form, along with the *Three Primordials’ Arrangement of Scriptures*, to the Supreme Lord.

The *Transmission of Daoist Learning* states: The Queen Mother said, "This *Numinous Radiance Life Canon* may be transmitted to one person every four thousand years. For the *Primal Canon*, it may be transmitted to two persons every eight thousand years. To transmit to an unworthy recipient is to leak the heavenly Dao. To withhold transmission when one should is to block the heavenly treasure. To transmit recklessly without regard for limits is to trifle with the Heavenly Elder. To receive without reverence is to slight the heavenly ornament. Leaking, blocking, trifling, and slighting—these four bring calamity."

Those of the same Dao are called "heavenly kin"; those of the same mind are called "earthly affection." In transmission, one should cherish mutual affection and share honor and disgrace alike.

It further states: Emperor Wu of the Han personally compiled the teachings of the Queen Mother of the West into a single scroll, along with the associated scriptures and charts. These were placed in a golden table and sealed in a white jade case, then stored atop the Wuliang Terrace.

The *Image and Name Canon* states: The Supreme Lord of the East rests upon a curved table inlaid with the seven treasures and phoenix patterns, spreading the essential true scriptures.

The *Supreme Yellow Plain Canon* states: When studying and receiving the *Great Grotto True Canon*, one must always place the scripture on a clean, cool table or shelf.

The *Dharma Wheel Canon* states: Those who wish to transmit scriptures must present gifts of gold and treasure to their master and formally request the Dao. To honor the Dharma and revere the Way, one must not act merely through words. To transmit lightly is to treat the treasure as worthless; to cultivate emptily is to debase the Dao.

The *Assembled Chapters Canon* states: The ancients attained immortality through the mind, but in the latter age, one cannot transcend without wealth. This is to show that in the latter age, wealth is prized and the Dao is scorned. If one were to offer a catty of gold and a volume of immortal scripture to the barren mountains of the latter age, they would seize the gold and flee, leaving the scripture behind. The gold would be engraved as a personal treasure, while the immortal scripture would be engraved to attain long life.

Knowing this yet unable to curb greed—this is what it means to say the Dao does not ennoble man.

The *Great Possession Scripture* states: The Supreme Treasure Chapters were transmitted to the Grand Thearch, the Grand Thearch to the Heavenly Thearch, the Heavenly Thearch to the Thearch of the Grand Tenuity, the Thearch of the Grand Tenuity to the Thearch of the Golden Portals, and the Thearch of the Golden Portals to Green of the Eastern Sea. Upon receiving them, they swore an oath with gold—nine inches long, four inches wide, and three *fen* thick—engraved and inscribed to seal the true essence of the mountains, rivers, and Five Peaks.

The *Scripture of the Three Primes and True Unity* states: To swear an oath before the Three Officials, one presents silk and a blood altar, cutting leather and binding it with great vows, only then may the transmission be conferred. The oath serves to fortify the spirit and steel the heart, so that the myriad things cannot violate it, nor heaven and earth oppose it. One prepares one *liang* of plain silk, fasting for a hundred days, or fifty, thirty, twenty, or ten days. The method stipulates that one may transmit it only once every forty years.

The *Scripture of Receiving the Mysterious Cinnabar and Jade* states: Thirty-two feet of blue cloth, thirty-two feet of vermilion silk, two bright mirrors, and a vow of secrecy are required as an unbreakable covenant.

The *Hidden Writ of the Eight Arts and Divine Tiger* states: Those who seek to receive the Hidden Writ of the Eight Guards must present a golden dragon and jade fish as tokens of their oath. The same applies to receiving the *Perfect Scripture of the Great Cavern*. It further states: Ten *liang* of refined gold serve as a pledge to the divine perfected. Ninety feet of brocade are used to swear an oath to the Nine Heavens. Forty feet of blue silk seal the text. Only those who cherish the Dao, delight in truth, devote their hearts to profound study, and hold the Dao in higher esteem than material wealth may be spoken to of such matters. It also states: To receive the *Tiger Writ of the Three Heavens*, one must present a solid gold tiger, jade seals, forty feet each of plain silk and dark gauze, as a sacred oath before heaven and earth—an unspoken covenant.

The *Mysterious Scripture of the Grand Unity and Perfect Truth* states: In ancient times, those who transmitted scriptures swore oaths by drinking blood and cutting hair, erecting altars to pledge before heaven. Today, gold and silk may serve in place of flesh and hair. It further warns that violating this oath results in the loss of both eyes.

The *Scripture of the Eight Gates of the Mysterious Mother* states: The methods of *langgan*, *huadan*, the Five Stones, and *xuanyu* all require sworn covenants.

The *Scripture of Cultivating and Examining True Unity* states: The method of the Grand Unity may be transmitted only once every twenty-four years. It also states: The Jade Flower Consort of the Eastern Sea, younger sister of the Azure Lad of the Written Term, descended to bestow upon Zhang Weizi the method of ingesting mist. It further states: The Lord of the Immortal Dao commanded his attendants Fan Yunhua, Zhao Junzhu, and Wang Baotai to open the jade casket, unfurl the green scrolls, and produce the two-scroll *Dragon Writ of the Eight Numinous Perfected* of the *Supreme Clarity Hidden Writ*, which they transmitted to Fan Xiangping.

The *Scripture of the Great Thoroughfare* states: Ren An wandered deep into the mountains and forests, where in the Cold Numinous Grotto he encountered Master Xuanhe, who bestowed upon him the *True Writ of the Black Thearch of the Numinous Treasure*. It also states: In the West, the Nine Radiant Divine Lads bestowed the *True Writ of the White Thearch* upon the Imperial Consort. It further states: In the Land of Color, the Ageless Lad of the Center transmitted the *True Writ of the Red Thearch of the Numinous Treasure* to the Perfected Lady Xinran.

The *Scripture of the Three Primes* states: The Primordial Beginning, at the Bright Rosy Clouds Abbey, bestowed the Jade Tallies of the Perfected upon the Jade Lads of the Three Heavens.

The *Inner Biography of Ma Mingsheng* states: Gong Zhongyang received the method of *Buji* from the Lad of Mount Songgao.

The *Pearl Satchel* states: Lu Yuande, a native of Dongqian in Wuxing, was summoned into the palace by Emperor Wen of the Song. He served with reverence and was held in high esteem. At the time, Empress Dowager Wang was deeply devoted to the Yellow and the Old, humbling her imperial dignity to observe the rites of a disciple.

It is further stated: Tao Hongjing, styled Tongming, was a native of Pingyang in Weizhou. He styled himself the Recluse of Huayang. The Crown Prince of Emperor Wu of Liang received the Dao from him. The princes of Shaoling under Emperor Jianwen of Liang—Xie Lan, Shen Yue, Ruan Xin, and Yu Quan—all revered him as their teacher and served him with devotion.

It is further stated: Liu Faxian, a native of Pengcheng, served as the Director of the Chongling Abbey under Emperor Ming of the Song. The Emperor had first studied under Lu Yuande; after Yuande’s passing, he then studied under Faxian, observing the full rites of a disciple.

It is further stated: Xue Biaozhi, a native of Jinling, was well-versed in the methods of incense burners and divine crucibles, discerning their refinement and coarseness, mastering their difficulties and simplicities. When disciples sought instruction, he would teach them with earnestness, then dismiss them according to their capacity.

It is further stated: Xie Xuan, styled Yuanying, was a native of Yangxia in Chenjun. At the age of twelve, he left his family to enter Gaoshou Mountain, where he studied under Zhu Tianci, subsisting on a vegetable diet and observing long-term fasting while devoting himself to Daoist cultivation. Zhu was stern and severe, and Xuan was the only one permitted to enter his chamber. Though Xie later secluded himself on Yu Mountain, living in profound solitude, seekers from near and far flocked to him, filling the forests and valleys.

It is further stated: Yu Chengxian, styled Chongguang, was a native of Yanling in Yingchuan. From childhood, he was perceptive and erudite, mastering a wide range of texts. At the time, the scholar Liu Hongshuo, who was particularly versed in the teachings of Laozi and Zhuangzi, was secluded on a sandbar in Jingzhou. Chengxian studied under him, delving deeply into his teachings. Though his family was poor and lacked books, he would borrow them, read them once, and commit them to memory.

It is further stated: Sun Youyue, styled Xuanda, was a native of Yongkang in Wuyang. During the Taishi era of the Song, Lu Yuande descended from Mount Lu to the capital to propagate the supreme teachings. Youyue then left the capital to seek the Dao and attend upon him, becoming one of the select few permitted to enter his chamber. The profound and abstruse doctrines were transmitted only to Youyue.

The *Record of the Great One* states: Master Pei meditated in seclusion for five years. The Five Thearchs declared: "You shall ascend to the Eight Poles City and the Luminous Terrace of the Perfected, where you will receive the arts of wielding the spirits of the Nine Provinces."

The *Register of the Jade Thearch* states: The Venerable Lord of the Primordial Beginning ascended the Altar of Jade Clarity and received the Registers of the Nine Heavens.

Ge Hong’s *Biographies of Divine Transcendents* states: Yan Qing, a native of Kuaiji, lived in poverty. While in the mountains, he encountered a man who spoke with him and, upon parting, presented him with a scroll of plain silk. He instructed Qing to place it in a clean vessel on a high shelf and also taught him the method of ingesting stalactites. The twenty-first section of the Daoist Canon concludes here.
